RavEngine is a C++23 cross-platform game framework designed to address pain points in existing game engines through modern architecture patterns and high-performance subsystems. The engine provides a complete stack from low-level graphics abstraction through high-level gameplay systems, with emphasis on parallel execution, GPU-driven rendering, and deterministic memory management via reference counting.

This page provides a high-level introduction to RavEngine's architecture, core subsystems, and design philosophy. For detailed information about specific systems, refer to the dedicated pages listed in subsequent sections (e.g., [Entity Component System](#3.2), [Rendering Architecture](#4.1), [Physics](#5), [Audio](#7)).

## Architecture Philosophy

RavEngine follows several key design principles:

| Principle | Implementation |
|-----------|----------------|
| **Data-Oriented Design** | ECS architecture with sparse sets and GPU-friendly memory layouts |
| **Parallelism First** | Taskflow-based multithreading, GPU-driven rendering, parallel physics |
| **Modern Graphics** | Reverse-Z depth, compute shader utilization, bindless resources |
| **Platform Abstraction** | RGL graphics layer abstracts Metal/DirectX 12/Vulkan |
| **Deterministic Memory** | Reference counting (`Ref<T>`) instead of garbage collection |
| **Build System Integration** | CMake-driven asset pipeline with cross-compilation support |

Sources: [README.md:1-144](), [CMakeLists.txt:1-350]()

## High-Level System Architecture

```mermaid
graph TB
    App["App<br/>(Application Entry Point)"]
```

**Architecture Diagram**: Shows the layered organization of RavEngine's major subsystems. The `App` class orchestrates top-level systems, `World` manages the ECS simulation, and platform-specific backends are abstracted through interface layers like `RGL` and `SDL3`.

Sources: [src/App_priv.hpp:1-353](), [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:1-269](), [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:1-496](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:1-365]()

## Core Subsystems

### Application Framework

The `App` class [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:49-269]() serves as the application entry point and orchestrates the main loop:

```mermaid
graph LR
    AppRun["App::run()"]
    Configure["OnConfigure()"]
    Startup["OnStartup()"]
    MainLoop["Main Loop"]
    Tick["Tick()"]
    Shutdown["OnShutdown()"]
    
    AppRun --> Configure
    Configure --> Startup
    Startup --> MainLoop
    MainLoop --> Tick
    Tick --> Tick
    Tick --> Shutdown
    
    subgraph "Main Loop Components"
        ProcessEvents["Process SDL Events"]
        TickWorlds["Tick All Worlds"]
        Render["Render Frame"]
        Audio["Process Audio"]
        
        Tick --> ProcessEvents
        ProcessEvents --> TickWorlds
        TickWorlds --> Render
        Render --> Audio
    end
```

**Main Loop Flow**: The `App::run()` method [src/App_priv.hpp:123-352]() implements the application lifecycle, processing events, ticking simulation, and coordinating rendering/audio on each frame.

Key responsibilities:
- **World Management**: Maintains list of active `World` instances and dispatches tick updates
- **Resource Initialization**: Creates `RenderEngine`, `AudioPlayer`, `VirtualFilesystem` [src/App_priv.hpp:174-220]()
- **Threading**: Owns Taskflow `executor` for parallel task execution [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:112-118]()
- **Timing**: Manages frame delta time and supports both dynamic and fixed tick rates [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:36-39]()

Sources: [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:49-269](), [src/App_priv.hpp:99-352]()

### Entity Component System

The `World` class [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:156-496]() implements a high-performance ECS using sparse set storage:

| Component | Purpose | Key Type |
|-----------|---------|----------|
| **Entity Storage** | Sparse entity IDs with versioning | `entity_t` with version field |
| **Component Stores** | Type-specific `EntitySparseSet<T>` per component | Dense array + sparse lookup |
| **Systems** | Parallel processing via Taskflow tasks | `AnimatorSystem`, `PhysicsLinkSystem`, etc. |
| **Render Data** | GPU-friendly parallel buffers | `BufferedVRAMSparseSet`, `BufferedVRAMVector` |

```mermaid
graph TB
    World["World"]
    
    subgraph "Entity Management"
        EntityIDs["Entity ID Pool<br/>(versions + available queue)"]
        ComponentMaps["componentMap<br/>(ctti_t â†’ AnySparseSet)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Component Storage"
        ESS["EntitySparseSet&lt;T&gt;<br/>(dense_set + sparse_set + aux_set)"]
        Dense["Dense Array<br/>(cache-friendly iteration)"]
        Sparse["Sparse Lookup<br/>(O(1) entityâ†’component)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "System Execution"
        Taskflow["Taskflow Task Graph"]
        PhysicsLinkSys["PhysicsLinkSystemWrite/Read"]
        AnimSys["AnimatorSystem"]
        ScriptSys["ScriptSystem"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Render Data Sync"
        RenderData["World::RenderData"]
        WorldTransforms["worldTransforms<br/>(BufferedVRAMVector)"]
        LightData["Light SSBOs<br/>(BufferedVRAMSparseSet)"]
        MeshCommands["staticMeshRenderData<br/>(MDI Commands)"]
    end
    
    World --> EntityIDs
    World --> ComponentMaps
    ComponentMaps --> ESS
    ESS --> Dense
    ESS --> Sparse
    
    World --> Taskflow
    Taskflow --> PhysicsLinkSys
    Taskflow --> AnimSys
    Taskflow --> ScriptSys
    
    World --> RenderData
    RenderData --> WorldTransforms
    RenderData --> LightData
    RenderData --> MeshCommands
```

**ECS Architecture**: The `World` uses type-erased `AnySparseSet` storage [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:286-325]() to store arbitrary component types, with Taskflow-based parallel system execution and dedicated render data structures for GPU upload.

Sources: [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:156-496](), [src/World.cpp:1-304]()

### Rendering Pipeline

The `RenderEngine` class [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:63-364]() implements a GPU-driven, multi-pass rendering pipeline:

**Key Features**:
- **GPU Culling**: Compute shader-based frustum/occlusion culling [shaders/defaultcull.csh:1-205]()
- **Multi-Draw Indirect**: Batched rendering via `IndirectCommand` buffers
- **Clustered Forward+**: Light assignment to 3D grid tiles [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:47-61]()
- **Depth Pyramid**: Hierarchical depth buffer for occlusion culling
- **PBR Lighting**: Physically-based shading with IBL, shadows, SSAO/SSGI

**Render Pass Sequence** (see [Rendering Architecture](#4.1) for details):
1. Depth Prepass (reverse-Z with `depthFunction = Greater`)
2. Depth Pyramid Generation
3. Light Cluster Assignment
4. GPU Culling (opaque)
5. Shadow Mapping (optional)
6. Main Opaque Pass (PBR lighting)
7. Skybox Rendering
8. Transparent Pass (order-independent)
9. Post-Processing (SSAO/SSGI/Bloom/DOF)
10. Tonemapping
11. GUI Overlay
12. Debug Rendering

Sources: [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:63-364](), [src/RenderEngine.cpp:1-1544](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:1-2640]()

### Graphics Abstraction Layer

**RGL** (RavEngine Graphics Library) provides a unified interface over modern graphics APIs:

```mermaid
graph TB
    App["Application Code"]
    RGL["RGL API Layer<br/>(Common Interface)"]
    
    subgraph "Backend Implementations"
        VkBackend["Vulkan Backend<br/>(Linux/Windows/Android)"]
        D3DBackend["DirectX 12 Backend<br/>(Windows)"]
        MTLBackend["Metal Backend<br/>(macOS/iOS/tvOS)"]
        WebGPUBackend["WebGPU Backend<br/>(Emscripten)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Core Abstractions"
        Device["RGLDevicePtr<br/>(GPU Device)"]
        CommandBuffer["RGLCommandBufferPtr<br/>(Command Recording)"]
        Pipeline["RGLRenderPipelinePtr<br/>(Shader Pipeline)"]
        Texture["RGLTexturePtr<br/>(Images/Textures)"]
        Buffer["RGLBufferPtr<br/>(GPU Buffers)"]
    end
    
    App --> RGL
    RGL --> Device
    RGL --> CommandBuffer
    RGL --> Pipeline
    RGL --> Texture
    RGL --> Buffer
    
    Device --> VkBackend
    Device --> D3DBackend
    Device --> MTLBackend
    Device --> WebGPUBackend
```

**RGL Architecture**: The graphics abstraction layer exposes common GPU primitives through smart pointer types (`RGLDevicePtr`, `RGLCommandBufferPtr`, etc.), with platform-specific implementations selected at runtime.

Cross-compilation support: When targeting platforms different from the host (e.g., building for Android on Windows), RavEngine builds host-native tools (`rglc`, `rvesc`, etc.) in a separate `host-tools` directory [deps/host-tools/CMakeLists.txt:1-45]() before compiling the target binaries.

Sources: [CMakeLists.txt:354-366](), [deps/host-tools/CMakeLists.txt:1-45](), [src/RenderEngine.cpp:296-322]()

### Asset Pipeline

RavEngine uses a CMake-integrated build-time asset pipeline:

| Tool | Purpose | Input | Output |
|------|---------|-------|--------|
| **rvemc** | Mesh compilation | `.obj`, `.fbx` + `config.json` | `.rvem` (optimized mesh) |
| **rveskc** | Skeleton compilation | Assimp-supported formats | `.rves` (Ozz skeleton) |
| **rveac** | Animation compilation | Animation data + `.json` config | `.rvea` (Ozz animation) |
| **rvesc** | Shader compilation | `.vsh`, `.fsh`, `.csh` (GLSL) | Platform bytecode |
| **pack_resources.cmake** | Archive packaging | All processed assets | `.rvedata` ZIP archive |

**Runtime Loading**:
- **PhysFS** virtual filesystem mounts `.rvedata` archives [src/App_priv.hpp:116-119]()
- Assets loaded on-demand via manager classes (`MeshAsset::Manager`, `Texture::Manager`, etc.)
- Shaders embedded via CMRC on non-Apple platforms, Metal libraries on Apple platforms

Sources: [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-354](), [CMakeLists.txt:355-398](), [include/RavEngine/Texture.hpp:57-59]()

### Physics Simulation

**PhysicsSolver** [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:101]() integrates NVIDIA PhysX for rigid body simulation:

- **Parallel Execution**: Physics tick runs asynchronously in Taskflow graph [src/World.cpp:184-197]()
- **Component Bridge**: `PhysicsLinkSystemRead`/`PhysicsLinkSystemWrite` sync transforms between PhysX and ECS [src/World.cpp:82-85]()
- **Collision Callbacks**: `PhysicsBodyComponent` receives contact events
- **Spatial Queries**: Raycasting, overlap tests against physics world

See [Physics](#5) for detailed documentation.

Sources: [src/World.cpp:77-303](), [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:101]()

### Audio System

**AudioPlayer** implements a lock-free, snapshot-based 3D audio architecture:

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Main Thread (World)"
        AudioSources["AudioSourceComponent"]
        AudioSpaces["SimpleAudioSpace<br/>GeometryAudioSpace<br/>BoxReverbationAudioSpace"]
        CreateSnapshot["Create AudioSnapshot"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Double-Buffered Snapshots"
        Current["Current Snapshot<br/>(Main thread writes)"]
        Render["Render Snapshot<br/>(Audio thread reads)"]
        SwapAtomic["Atomic Swap"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Audio Thread"
        AudioTick["AudioPlayer::Tick()"]
        Taskflow["Taskflow (2 workers)"]
        SteamAudio["Steam Audio<br/>(HRTF + Occlusion)"]
        Resonance["Resonance Audio<br/>(Reverb)"]
        Mix["Mix & Output"]
    end
    
    AudioSources --> CreateSnapshot
    AudioSpaces --> CreateSnapshot
    CreateSnapshot --> Current
    Current --> SwapAtomic
    SwapAtomic --> Render
    
    Render --> AudioTick
    AudioTick --> Taskflow
    Taskflow --> SteamAudio
    Taskflow --> Resonance
    SteamAudio --> Mix
    Resonance --> Mix
    Mix --> SDL["SDL Audio Stream"]
```

**Audio Architecture**: Lock-free snapshot system allows main thread to populate audio state while dedicated audio thread processes previous frame's data in parallel using Taskflow and external audio libraries.

Sources: [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:222-264](), [src/World.cpp:204-301]()

### User Interface

**GUIComponent** integrates **RmlUi** for declarative HTML/CSS-based UI:

- **Document Loading**: Load `.rml` files from virtual filesystem [src/GUI.cpp:53-94]()
- **Input Forwarding**: SDL events translated to RmlUi input [src/GUI.cpp:21-51]()
- **Rendering**: Custom `RenderInterface` implementation renders UI geometry [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:1-248]()
- **Data Binding**: Support for RmlUi's data model system

See [GUI Components and RmlUi](#8.1) for details.

Sources: [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:1-81](), [src/GUI.cpp:1-237](), [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:1-248]()

## Platform Support Matrix

| Platform | Architectures | Rendering API | Status |
|----------|---------------|---------------|--------|
| **Windows 10+** | x64, ARM64 | DirectX 12, Vulkan | Stable |
| **macOS 12+** | x64, Apple Silicon | Metal | Stable |
| **Linux** | x64, ARM64 | Vulkan | Stable |
| **iOS 16+** | ARM64 (Device + Simulator) | Metal | Stable |
| **tvOS 16+** | ARM64 (Device + Simulator) | Metal | Stable |
| **visionOS 1+** | ARM64 (Device + Simulator) | Metal | WIP |
| **Android** | x86, x64, ARMv7, ARM64 | Vulkan | WIP |
| **Emscripten** | WebAssembly | WebGPU | Early WIP |

**Build Requirements**:
- **Cross-Compilation**: Supports building for target platforms from different host OSes [CMakeLists.txt:78-181]()
- **CMake 3.25+**: All platforms use CMake for configuration
- **Compilers**: MSVC 2022+, Clang 16+, GCC 13+, Apple Clang (Xcode 16.2+)
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions tests build on all platforms [.github/workflows/build.yml:1-204]()

Sources: [README.md:82-96](), [CMakeLists.txt:78-181](), [.github/workflows/build.yml:1-204]()

**Repository Structure**: The codebase separates public API headers in `include/RavEngine/`, implementation in `src/`, platform-native shaders in `shaders/`, CMake build logic in `cmake/`, and extensive third-party dependencies in `deps/`.

Sources: [CMakeLists.txt:1-900](), [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-354](), [cmake/importers.cmake:1-45]()

## Getting Started

To integrate RavEngine into a project:

1. **Add as Subdirectory**: Include RavEngine via CMake `add_subdirectory()`
2. **Link Target**: `target_link_libraries(MyGame PUBLIC RavEngine)`
3. **Pack Resources**: Use `pack_resources()` CMake function to process assets [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:2-354]()
4. **Implement App Hooks**: Override `OnStartup()`, `OnShutdown()`, `OnConfigure()` in your `App` subclass

For detailed build instructions and example code, see [Getting Started](#2) and [Creating Your First Application](#2.3).

Example minimal CMakeLists.txt structure is shown in [README.md:30-75]().

Sources: [README.md:29-75](), [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:2-354]()

## Memory Management

RavEngine uses deterministic reference counting instead of garbage collection:

- **`Ref<T>`**: Smart pointer for shared ownership [include/RavEngine/Ref.hpp]()
- **`WeakRef<T>`**: Non-owning reference that can detect deletion
- **Automatic Cleanup**: Objects destroyed when reference count reaches zero
- **No GC Pauses**: Predictable frame timing without stop-the-world collection

This approach provides Rust-like memory safety guarantees in C++ while maintaining deterministic performance characteristics critical for real-time applications.

Sources: [README.md:1-144]()

## Threading Model

RavEngine employs extensive parallelism:

| Component | Threading Approach |
|-----------|-------------------|
| **Main Loop** | Single main thread coordinates subsystems |
| **ECS Systems** | Taskflow parallel execution per `World::Tick()` [src/World.cpp:126-138]() |
| **Physics** | PhysX internal threading + async ECS integration |
| **Audio** | Dedicated audio thread + Taskflow workers (2 threads) |
| **Rendering** | GPU command buffer recording on main thread, async execution |
| **Asset Loading** | Lazy loading on-demand, can be parallelized by user |

The global `App::executor` Taskflow instance [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:112-118]() provides a thread pool sized to `hardware_concurrency() - 2` (reserving threads for audio).

Sources: [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:112-118](), [src/World.cpp:126-138]()18:T4844,# Getting Started

This page guides you through setting up a RavEngine project, understanding the basic application structure, and building your first application. For a complete walkthrough of creating a minimal application, see [Creating Your First Application](#2.3).

## Prerequisites

RavEngine requires specific software and hardware to build and run applications.

### Development Hardware Requirements

| Component | Minimum | Recommended |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| CPU | 4 cores | 16 threads |
| RAM | 16 GB | 32 GB |
| GPU | DX12/Vulkan 1.3/Metal 3 support | - |
| Disk | SSD with 40GB free | - |

**Sources:** [README.md:97-105]()

### Software Requirements by Platform

**macOS, iOS, tvOS, visionOS:**
- Xcode 16.2+
- CMake

**Windows:**
- Visual Studio 2022 with "Desktop Development in C++" and "Game Development in C++" modules
- CMake (included with Visual Studio)
- LunarG Vulkan SDK (optional, for Vulkan support)

**Linux:**
- ninja (recommended) or make
- clang 16+ (recommended) or gcc 13+
- cmake
- libatomic, libx11-dev, libwayland-dev, uuid-dev
- ALSA or PulseAudio development libraries
- LunarG Vulkan SDK

**Android:**
- Android Studio 4.2+ with NDK 27+
- Host platform requirements (Windows, macOS, or Linux as above)
- SDL Android Builder wrapper project

**Sources:** [README.md:108-140]()

## Project Structure

RavEngine applications follow a standard CMake-based project structure that integrates the engine as a subdirectory.

### CMake Project Integration

```mermaid
graph TB
    YourProject["Your Project CMakeLists.txt"]
    RavEngine["RavEngine Subdirectory"]
    YourExecutable["Your Executable Target"]
    PackResources["pack_resources Function"]
    Assets["Asset Files<br/>(meshes, textures, shaders, etc.)"]
    DataArchive["TARGET.rvedata Archive"]
    
    YourProject -->|"add_subdirectory"| RavEngine
    YourProject -->|"add_executable"| YourExecutable
    YourExecutable -->|"target_link_libraries"| RavEngine
    YourProject -->|"calls"| PackResources
    PackResources -->|"processes"| Assets
    PackResources -->|"produces"| DataArchive
    DataArchive -->|"linked to"| YourExecutable
```

**Minimal CMakeLists.txt Structure:**

The following structure is required for all RavEngine projects:

```cmake
cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.23)
set(CMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX ${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR})
set(CMAKE_RUNTIME_OUTPUT_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/$<CONFIGURATION>)
set(CMAKE_LIBRARY_OUTPUT_DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/$<CONFIGURATION>)

PROJECT(YourProjectName)

add_subdirectory("RavEngine")

file(GLOB SOURCES "src/*.cpp" "src/*.hpp" "src/*.h")
add_executable("${PROJECT_NAME}" ${SOURCES})
target_link_libraries("${PROJECT_NAME}" PUBLIC "RavEngine")
target_compile_features("${PROJECT_NAME}" PRIVATE cxx_std_23)

# Asset packaging - see Asset Pipeline section below
pack_resources(TARGET "${PROJECT_NAME}" 
   # ... asset lists ...
)
```

**Sources:** [README.md:30-64](), [CMakeLists.txt:1-31]()

### Cross-Compilation Host Tools

When cross-compiling (e.g., building for Android from Windows, or iOS from macOS), RavEngine automatically builds host-native tools in a separate directory:

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Build Configuration Detection"
        Crosscomp["CMAKE_CROSSCOMPILING<br/>or VS_CROSSCOMP"]
        HostTools["Build Host Tools"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Host Tools Directory"
        ToolsDir["TOOLS_DIR<br/>build/host-tools"]
        Protoc["protoc"]
        Rglc["rglc<br/>(shader compiler)"]
        Flatc["flatc"]
        Rvesc["rvesc<br/>(shader processor)"]
        Rvemc["rvemc<br/>(mesh compiler)"]
        Rveac["rveac<br/>(animation compiler)"]
        Rveskc["rveskc<br/>(skeleton compiler)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Target Build"
        TargetBuild["Target Platform Build"]
        UseTools["Uses host-built tools"]
    end
    
    Crosscomp -->|"if true"| HostTools
    HostTools --> ToolsDir
    ToolsDir --> Protoc
    ToolsDir --> Rglc
    ToolsDir --> Flatc
    ToolsDir --> Rvesc
    ToolsDir --> Rvemc
    ToolsDir --> Rveac
    ToolsDir --> Rveskc
    
    Protoc --> UseTools
    Rglc --> UseTools
    Flatc --> UseTools
    Rvesc --> UseTools
    Rvemc --> UseTools
    Rveac --> UseTools
    Rveskc --> UseTools
    
    UseTools --> TargetBuild
```

The `RVE_CROSSCOMP` variable controls this behavior. When enabled, tools are built for the host platform first, then referenced by the target build.

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:90-181](), [deps/host-tools/CMakeLists.txt:1-76]()

## Application Class Structure

All RavEngine applications must define a class inheriting from `RavEngine::App`. This class provides the application lifecycle hooks and manages the main loop.

### App Class Lifecycle

```mermaid
graph TD
    Constructor["App::App()<br/>- Initialize VFS<br/>- Set signal handlers"]
    
    Run["App::run(argc, argv)<br/>Entry point"]
    
    OnConfigure["OnConfigure(argc, argv)<br/>User override<br/>Returns AppConfig"]
    
    Init["Initialization<br/>- SDL_Init<br/>- Create Window<br/>- RGL::Init(api)<br/>- Create RenderEngine<br/>- Initialize RmlUi<br/>- Create AudioPlayer<br/>- GameNetworkingSockets_Init"]
    
    OnStartup["OnStartup(argc, argv)<br/>User override<br/>Load worlds, setup scene"]
    
    MainLoop["Main Loop<br/>while (!exit)"]
    
    Tick["Tick()<br/>- Poll SDL events<br/>- World::Tick<br/>- RenderEngine::Draw<br/>- Present swapchain"]
    
    OnShutdown["OnShutdown()<br/>User override<br/>Return exit code"]
    
    Destructor["~App()<br/>- Cleanup worlds<br/>- Shutdown subsystems<br/>- PHYSFS_deinit"]
    
    Constructor --> Run
    Run --> OnConfigure
    OnConfigure --> Init
    Init --> OnStartup
    OnStartup --> MainLoop
    MainLoop --> Tick
    Tick -->|"repeat"| MainLoop
    MainLoop -->|"exit"| OnShutdown
    OnShutdown --> Destructor
```

**Key Application Class Methods:**

| Method | Purpose | Required Override |
|--------|---------|-------------------|
| `OnConfigure(argc, argv)` | Configure engine settings before initialization | Optional |
| `OnStartup(argc, argv)` | Initialize game state, load worlds | Yes |
| `OnShutdown()` | Cleanup, return exit code | Optional |
| `OnFatal(msg)` | Custom fatal error handler | Optional |
| `NeedsAudio()` | Return false to disable audio subsystem | Optional |
| `NeedsNetworking()` | Return true to enable networking | Optional |

**Sources:** [App.cpp:99-352](), [App.hpp:49-365](), [src/App_priv.hpp:1-47]()

### Core App Member Variables and Methods

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Core Subsystems (App members)"
        Renderer["Renderer<br/>unique_ptr&lt;RenderEngine&gt;<br/>GPU-driven rendering"]
        Device["device<br/>RGLDevicePtr<br/>Graphics device handle"]
        Window["window<br/>unique_ptr&lt;Window&gt;<br/>Main window"]
        Resources["Resources<br/>unique_ptr&lt;VirtualFilesystem&gt;<br/>Asset loading"]
        Player["player<br/>unique_ptr&lt;AudioPlayer&gt;<br/>3D audio playback"]
        InputMgr["inputManager<br/>Ref&lt;InputManager&gt;<br/>Input binding system"]
        NetMgr["networkManager<br/>NetworkManager<br/>Client/Server networking"]
    end
    
    subgraph "World Management"
        LoadedWorlds["loadedWorlds<br/>locked_hashset&lt;Ref&lt;World&gt;&gt;<br/>All active worlds"]
        RenderWorld["renderWorld<br/>Ref&lt;World&gt;<br/>Currently rendered world"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Thread Management"
        Executor["executor<br/>tf::Executor<br/>Global thread pool"]
        MainTasks["main_tasks<br/>ConcurrentQueue<br/>Tasks for main thread"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Timing"
        CurrentScale["currentScale<br/>float<br/>Deltatime multiplier"]
        Time["time<br/>double<br/>Elapsed seconds"]
        TickMode["tickMode<br/>TickMode enum<br/>DynamicRate or FixedRate"]
    end
    
    App["App Class"] --> Renderer
    App --> Device
    App --> Window
    App --> Resources
    App --> Player
    App --> InputMgr
    App --> NetMgr
    App --> LoadedWorlds
    App --> RenderWorld
    App --> Executor
    App --> MainTasks
    App --> CurrentScale
    App --> Time
    App --> TickMode
```

**World Management Methods:**
- `AddWorld(world)` - Add a world to be ticked each frame
- `RemoveWorld(world)` - Stop ticking a world
- `SetRenderedWorld(world)` - Set which world is rendered
- `AddReplaceWorld(oldWorld, newWorld)` - Swap worlds, transferring render state

**Thread Dispatching:**
- `DispatchMainThread(lambda)` - Queue a task to execute on main thread
- `executor` - Taskflow executor for parallel work (hardware_concurrency - 2 threads)

**Sources:** [App.hpp:49-365](), [App.cpp:354-504]()

## Asset Pipeline Overview

RavEngine uses a build-time asset pipeline that processes source assets into optimized runtime formats and packages them into a `.rvedata` archive.

### pack_resources Function

The `pack_resources` CMake function is the primary interface for declaring and processing assets:

```cmake
pack_resources(TARGET "${PROJECT_NAME}" 
   OUTPUT_FILE DATA_PACK
   OBJECTS ${objects}              # .obj, .fbx via rvemc
   MESHES ${mesh_configs}          # .json configs for rvemc
   SKELETONS ${skeleton_configs}   # .json configs for rveskc
   ANIMATIONS ${animation_configs} # .json configs for rveac
   SHADERS ${shaders}              # .vsh, .fsh, .csh via rvesc
   TEXTURES ${textures}            # .png, .jpg, .dds, .exr
   UIS ${uis}                      # .rml, .rcss for RmlUi
   FONTS ${fonts}                  # .ttf
   SOUNDS ${sounds}                # .ogg, .wav
   STREAMING_ASSETS ${streaming}   # Files not in archive
   STREAMING_INPUT_ROOT ${root}    # Root for streaming paths
   DATA_ASSETS ${data}             # Generic data files
)
```

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-326](), [README.md:50-64]()

### Asset Processing Pipeline

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Source Assets"
        SourceMesh["3D Models<br/>.obj .fbx"]
        SourceAnim["Animation Configs<br/>.json"]
        SourceShader["Shaders<br/>.vsh .fsh .csh"]
        SourceTex["Images<br/>.png .jpg .dds .exr"]
        SourceAudio["Audio<br/>.ogg .wav"]
        SourceUI["UI<br/>.rml .rcss"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Build-Time Tools"
        Rvemc["rvemc<br/>Mesh Compiler<br/>Assimp + meshoptimizer"]
        Rveac["rveac<br/>Animation Compiler<br/>Ozz format"]
        Rveskc["rveskc<br/>Skeleton Compiler<br/>Ozz format"]
        Rvesc["rvesc + rglc<br/>Shader Compiler<br/>Platform bytecode"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Intermediate Formats"
        Rvem[".rvem<br/>Optimized mesh"]
        Rvea[".rvea<br/>Compressed animation"]
        Rves[".rves<br/>Skeleton data"]
        CompiledShaders["Compiled Shaders<br/>SPIR-V/DXIL/Metal"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Packaging"
        PackRes["pack_resources"]
        Archive["TARGET.rvedata<br/>ZIP archive"]
        ShaderEmbed["Shader Embedding<br/>CMRC or Metal Library"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Runtime Loading"
        VFS["PhysFS<br/>Virtual Filesystem"]
        Assets["Runtime Assets<br/>MeshAsset, Texture, etc."]
    end
    
    SourceMesh -->|"config.json"| Rvemc
    SourceAnim --> Rveac
    SourceMesh --> Rveskc
    SourceShader --> Rvesc
    
    Rvemc --> Rvem
    Rveac --> Rvea
    Rveskc --> Rves
    Rvesc --> CompiledShaders
    
    Rvem --> PackRes
    Rvea --> PackRes
    Rves --> PackRes
    SourceTex --> PackRes
    SourceAudio --> PackRes
    SourceUI --> PackRes
    
    PackRes --> Archive
    CompiledShaders --> ShaderEmbed
    
    Archive --> VFS
    ShaderEmbed --> VFS
    VFS --> Assets
```

**Asset Compiler Tools:**

| Tool | Input | Output | Purpose |
|------|-------|--------|---------|
| `rvemc` | `.obj`, `.fbx` + `.json` config | `.rvem` | Mesh optimization, vertex compression |
| `rveskc` | 3D model + `.json` config | `.rves` | Skeleton extraction for animation |
| `rveac` | 3D model + `.json` config | `.rvea` | Animation compression (Ozz format) |
| `rvesc` | `.vsh`, `.fsh`, `.csh` + `rglc` | Platform bytecode | Shader compilation |

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:122-180](), [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:186-237](), [cmake/importers.cmake:1-37](), [cmake/rvesc.cmake:1-17]()

### Shader Compilation

Shaders receive special handling depending on the target platform:

**Non-Apple Platforms:**
- Shaders compiled to SPIR-V or DXIL
- Embedded using CMRC (CMake Resource Compiler)
- Accessed via `cmrc_get_file_data(path)` function

**Apple Platforms:**
- Shaders compiled to Metal library (`.metallib`)
- Embedded in application bundle
- Loaded via Metal API

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:206-238]()

### Runtime Asset Access

At runtime, assets are loaded through the `VirtualFilesystem` class (backed by PhysFS):

```cpp
// Access through App
auto& vfs = GetApp()->GetResources();

// Load assets by path
auto texture = New<Texture>("myTexture.png");  // from /textures/
auto mesh = MeshAsset::Manager::Get("myMesh.rvem");  // from /meshes/
auto sound = New<AudioAsset>("sound.ogg");  // from /sounds/

// VFS paths are relative to archive root
RavEngine::Vector<uint8_t> data;
vfs.FileContentsAt("/textures/icon.png", data);
```

The `.rvedata` archive is automatically mounted by PhysFS during `App::App()` construction.

**Sources:** [App.cpp:106-120](), [src/Texture.cpp:149-206]()

## Building Your Application

### Platform-Specific Build Commands

**macOS / iOS / tvOS / visionOS (Xcode):**

```bash
mkdir build && cd build
cmake -G "Xcode" -DCMAKE_SYSTEM_NAME=<Platform> \
      -DCMAKE_OSX_ARCHITECTURES="x86_64;arm64" ..
cmake --build . --config Release
```

Replace `<Platform>` with `iOS`, `tvOS`, `visionOS`, or omit for macOS.

**Windows (Visual Studio):**

```cmd
mkdir build && cd build
cmake -A x64 ..
cmake --build . --config Release
```

For ARM64: use `-A ARM64`. For cross-compilation, you may need to run configure twice due to host tools setup.

**Linux (Ninja):**

```bash
mkdir build && cd build
CC=clang CXX=clang++ cmake -G "Ninja" ..
cmake --build . --config Release
```

**Android (Ninja with NDK):**

```bash
mkdir build && cd build
cmake -G "Ninja" \
      -DCMAKE_TOOLCHAIN_FILE="${NDK_PATH}/build/cmake/android.toolchain.cmake" \
      -DANDROID_ABI="arm64-v8a" \
      -DANDROID_PLATFORM=33 ..
cmake --build . --config Release
```

**Sources:** [.github/workflows/build.yml:15-137](), [README.md:76-81](), [CMakeLists.txt:102-178]()

### Build System Targets

The build system creates several targets:

| Target | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `RavEngine` | Main engine library |
| `YourProject` | Your application executable |
| `YourProject_CompileShaders` | Shader compilation (automatic dependency) |
| `YourProject_ShaderResources` | CMRC shader library (non-Apple) |
| `YourProject_Externs` | External symbol definitions |
| `rvesc`, `rvemc`, `rveac`, `rveskc` | Asset compiler tools |
| `rglc` | Shader compiler (via RGL) |

Build order is automatically managed: tools build first (host-native if cross-compiling), then shaders compile, then assets process, finally the executable links.

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:203-262]()

## Running Your Application

After building, your application executable and the `.rvedata` asset archive will be in the output directory:

**Desktop Platforms:**
```
build/Release/
â”œâ”€â”€ YourProject(.exe)
â””â”€â”€ YourProject.rvedata
```

**Apple Mobile Platforms:**
Assets are embedded in the `.app` bundle under `Resources/`.

**Android:**
Assets are packaged in the APK via gradle integration.

**UWP (Windows Store):**
Assets are placed in `AppX/` deployment directory.

### Execution

Simply run the executable. The engine automatically:
1. Initializes PhysFS and mounts the `.rvedata` archive
2. Calls your `OnStartup()` method
3. Enters the main loop, calling `Tick()` each frame
4. Exits when the window closes or `Quit()` is called
5. Calls your `OnShutdown()` method

**Sources:** [App.cpp:123-352](), [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:273-322]()

## Next Steps

Once you have the basic build system configured:

1. **Implement your App subclass** - Override `OnStartup()` to create your first `World` and entities. See [Creating Your First Application](#2.3).

2. **Understand the ECS** - Learn how to create entities, attach components, and write systems. See [Entity Component System](#3.2).

3. **Configure assets** - Prepare meshes, textures, and shaders for your project. See [Asset Pipeline](#2.2).

4. **Set up rendering** - Create cameras, lights, and materials. See [Rendering Architecture](#4.1).

5. **Add physics** - Integrate rigid bodies and colliders. See [Physics Bodies and Colliders](#5.1).

**Sources:** General project structure19:T5c20,# Building RavEngine

## Purpose and Scope

This document provides comprehensive instructions for building RavEngine from source across all supported platforms. It covers CMake configuration options, cross-compilation support, platform-specific requirements, and the build process architecture. For instructions on creating your first application using RavEngine, see [Creating Your First Application](#2.3). For asset preparation workflows, see [Asset Pipeline](#2.2).

---

## System Requirements

### Hardware Requirements

| Component | Recommended | Minimum |
|-----------|-------------|---------|
| CPU | 16 threads | 4 cores |
| RAM | 32 GB | 16 GB |
| GPU | Any with DX12, VK 1.3, or Metal 3 | Same |
| Disk | SSD with 40GB free space | Same |

**Sources:** [README.md:98-106]()

### Software Requirements

#### Common Requirements
- **CMake 3.25 or later** - Build system generator

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:1]()

#### Platform-Specific Requirements

| Platform | Requirements |
|----------|-------------|
| **macOS/iOS/tvOS/visionOS** | Xcode 16.2+, CMake |
| **Windows** | Visual Studio 2022+ with "Desktop Development in C++" and "Game Development in C++", LunarG Vulkan SDK (optional for Vulkan) |
| **Linux** | ninja or make, clang 16+ or gcc 13+, libatomic, libx11-dev, libwayland-dev, uuid-dev, alsa-lib-devel or pulseaudio, LunarG Vulkan SDK |
| **Android** | Android Studio 4.2+ with NDK 27+, host requirements vary by OS |
| **Emscripten** | Latest emsdk, CMake, host requirements vary by OS |

**Sources:** [README.md:108-140](), [.github/workflows/build.yml:1-204]()

## CMake Configuration Options

RavEngine provides several configuration variables to customize the build:

| Option | Type | Default | Description |
|--------|------|---------|-------------|
| `RAVENGINE_BUILD_TESTS` | OPTION | OFF | Build unit tests and test executables |
| `RAVENGINE_SERVER` | OPTION | OFF | Build as headless server (no rendering) |
| `RAVENGINE_MSVC_FAST_DEBUG_ITERATORS` | OPTION | ON | Set iterator debug level to 0 in MSVC Debug builds |
| `RAVENGINE_PROFILE_ALL_BUILDS` | OPTION | OFF | Enable instrumentation in all configurations (not just Profile) |
| `RAVENGINE_MSVC_DEBUG_ALL_BUILDS` | OPTION | OFF | Enable debugging support in all MSVC configurations |
| `RAVENGINE_ASSETS_DIR` | FILEPATH | `${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}` | Directory where packed `.rvedata` archives are written |

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:17-31]()

### Example Configuration

```cmake
# Basic configuration
cmake -G "Ninja" -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release ..

# With tests enabled
cmake -G "Ninja" -DRAVENGINE_BUILD_TESTS=ON ..

# Server build (headless)
cmake -G "Ninja" -DRAVENGINE_SERVER=ON ..

# Custom assets directory
cmake -G "Ninja" -DRAVENGINE_ASSETS_DIR="/path/to/assets" ..
```

---

## Cross-Compilation Architecture

RavEngine supports cross-compilation by building **host tools** natively on the build machine, even when the target platform is different. This is necessary because asset processing tools must run on the build machine.

### Cross-Compilation Detection

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start["Configure CMake"] --> CheckVS{"Visual Studio<br/>Platform Name?"}
    CheckVS -->|"Set and â‰  Default"| SetVSCross["VS_CROSSCOMP = ON"]
    CheckVS -->|"Not Set or = Default"| SetVSNative["VS_CROSSCOMP = OFF"]
    
    SetVSCross --> CheckHost{"CMAKE_HOST_WIN32<br/>and VS_CROSSCOMP?"}
    SetVSNative --> CheckHost
    
    CheckHost -->|"Yes"| ForceCross["CMAKE_CROSSCOMPILING = ON"]
    CheckHost -->|"No"| CheckCMakeCross{"CMAKE_CROSSCOMPILING<br/>or VS_CROSSCOMP?"}
    
    ForceCross --> SetRVECross["RVE_CROSSCOMP = ON"]
    CheckCMakeCross -->|"Yes"| SetRVECross
    CheckCMakeCross -->|"No"| SetRVENative["RVE_CROSSCOMP = OFF"]
    
    SetRVECross --> BuildHostTools["Configure and build<br/>host-tools subdirectory"]
    SetRVENative --> UseLocalTools["Build tools<br/>as part of main build"]
    
    BuildHostTools --> SetToolPaths["Set tool paths to<br/>TOOLS_DIR/tool/Release/tool.exe"]
    UseLocalTools --> NormalBuild["Standard build process"]
    
    SetToolPaths --> NormalBuild
```

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:80-181]()

### Host Tools Build Process

When cross-compiling, RavEngine invokes a separate CMake configuration for host tools:

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph "Target Build<br/>(e.g., Android ARM64)"
        TargetCMake["Main CMakeLists.txt<br/>RVE_CROSSCOMP=ON"]
        ExecHostConfig["execute_process:<br/>Configure host-tools"]
        CustomCmd["add_custom_command:<br/>Build host tools"]
        UsePaths["Use PROTOC_CMD,<br/>rglc_path, RVESC_PATH,<br/>RVEMC_PATH, etc."]
    end
    
    subgraph "Host Build<br/>(e.g., Windows x64)"
        HostCMake["deps/host-tools/CMakeLists.txt"]
        BuildProtoc["Build protoc"]
        BuildRGLC["Build rglc"]
        BuildRVESC["Build rvesc"]
        BuildRVEMC["Build rvemc"]
        BuildRVEAC["Build rveac"]
        BuildRVESKC["Build rveskc"]
        BuildFlatc["Build flatc"]
    end
    
    TargetCMake --> ExecHostConfig
    ExecHostConfig --> HostCMake
    HostCMake --> BuildProtoc
    HostCMake --> BuildRGLC
    HostCMake --> BuildRVESC
    HostCMake --> BuildRVEMC
    HostCMake --> BuildRVEAC
    HostCMake --> BuildRVESKC
    HostCMake --> BuildFlatc
    
    BuildProtoc --> CustomCmd
    BuildRGLC --> CustomCmd
    BuildRVESC --> CustomCmd
    BuildRVEMC --> CustomCmd
    BuildRVEAC --> CustomCmd
    BuildRVESKC --> CustomCmd
    BuildFlatc --> CustomCmd
    
    CustomCmd --> UsePaths
```

The host tools directory structure depends on the generator:

- **Ninja/Unix Makefiles**: `${TOOLS_DIR}/tool/tool`
- **Visual Studio**: `${TOOLS_DIR}/tool/Release/tool.exe`

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:102-177](), [deps/host-tools/CMakeLists.txt:1-76]()

---

## Build Process Flow

### Overall Build Phases

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Configure["CMake Configure Phase"] --> GenHostTools{"Cross-compiling?"}
    
    GenHostTools -->|"Yes"| ConfigHost["Configure host-tools<br/>in TOOLS_DIR"]
    GenHostTools -->|"No"| ConfigDeps["Configure dependencies"]
    
    ConfigHost --> BuildHost["Build host tools:<br/>protoc, rglc, flatc,<br/>rvesc, rvemc, rveac, rveskc"]
    
    BuildHost --> ConfigDeps
    ConfigDeps --> GenBuild["Generate build files"]
    
    GenBuild --> Build["Build Phase"]
    
    Build --> CompileEngine["Compile RavEngine library"]
    Build --> CompileTools{"Cross-compiling?"}
    
    CompileTools -->|"No"| CompileLocalTools["Compile rvesc, rvemc,<br/>rveac, rveskc"]
    CompileTools -->|"Yes"| SkipTools["Use pre-built host tools"]
    
    CompileLocalTools --> CompileApp["Compile application target"]
    SkipTools --> CompileApp
    
    CompileApp --> ProcessAssets["Asset Processing Phase"]
    
    ProcessAssets --> CompileShaders["rvesc:<br/>Compile shaders to<br/>platform bytecode"]
    ProcessAssets --> ImportMeshes["rvemc:<br/>Import and optimize<br/>.obj/.fbx meshes"]
    ProcessAssets --> ImportSkeletons["rveskc:<br/>Import skeletons"]
    ProcessAssets --> ImportAnims["rveac:<br/>Import animations"]
    
    CompileShaders --> EmbedShaders{"Platform?"}
    EmbedShaders -->|"Apple"| MetalLib["Compile to .metallib"]
    EmbedShaders -->|"Other"| CMRC["Embed via CMRC"]
    
    MetalLib --> PackAssets["pack_resources.cmake:<br/>Create .rvedata archive"]
    CMRC --> LinkShaders["Link shader resource library"]
    
    ImportMeshes --> PackAssets
    ImportSkeletons --> PackAssets
    ImportAnims --> PackAssets
    
    LinkShaders --> PackAssets
    
    PackAssets --> BundleAssets{"Platform?"}
    BundleAssets -->|"Apple"| MacBundle["Bundle .rvedata<br/>in .app/Resources"]
    BundleAssets -->|"UWP"| UWPBundle["Deploy to AppX"]
    BundleAssets -->|"Win32/Linux"| CopyExe["Copy to executable directory"]
    
    MacBundle --> LinkApp["Link application"]
    UWPBundle --> LinkApp
    CopyExe --> LinkApp
```

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:183-897](), [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-326]()

### Asset Processing Pipeline

The `pack_resources` CMake function orchestrates asset compilation:

```mermaid
flowchart TB
    subgraph Input["Input Assets"]
        OBJECTS["3D Models<br/>.obj, .fbx"]
        MESHES["Mesh Configs<br/>.json"]
        SKELETONS["Skeleton Configs<br/>.json"]
        ANIMATIONS["Animation Configs<br/>.json"]
        SHADERS["Shaders<br/>.vsh, .fsh, .csh"]
        TEXTURES["Textures<br/>.png, .jpg, .dds, .exr"]
        SOUNDS["Audio<br/>.ogg, .wav"]
        UIS["UI Files<br/>.rml, .rcss"]
        FONTS["Fonts<br/>.ttf"]
    end
    
    subgraph Tools["Asset Compilers"]
        RVEMC["rvemc<br/>Mesh Compiler"]
        RVESKC["rveskc<br/>Skeleton Compiler"]
        RVEAC["rveac<br/>Animation Compiler"]
        RVESC["rvesc<br/>Shader Compiler"]
    end
    
    subgraph Staging["Staging Directory<br/>${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${TARGET}"]
        StagedMeshes["meshes/*.rvem"]
        StagedSkeletons["skeletons/*.rves"]
        StagedAnims["animations/*.rvea"]
        StagedShaders["${TARGET}_ShaderIntermediate/<br/>platform bytecode"]
        StagedTextures["textures/*"]
        StagedSounds["sounds/*"]
        StagedUIs["uis/*.rml, *.rcss"]
        StagedFonts["fonts/*.ttf"]
    end
    
    subgraph Output["Build Artifacts"]
        Archive["${TARGET}.rvedata<br/>ZIP archive"]
        ShaderLib["${TARGET}_ShaderResources<br/>CMRC library (non-Apple)"]
        MetalLibs[".metallib files<br/>(Apple only)"]
    end
    
    OBJECTS --> RVEMC
    MESHES --> RVEMC
    RVEMC --> StagedMeshes
    
    SKELETONS --> RVESKC
    RVESKC --> StagedSkeletons
    
    ANIMATIONS --> RVEAC
    RVEAC --> StagedAnims
    
    SHADERS --> RVESC
    RVESC --> StagedShaders
    
    TEXTURES --> StagedTextures
    SOUNDS --> StagedSounds
    UIS --> StagedUIs
    FONTS --> StagedFonts
    
    StagedMeshes --> Archive
    StagedSkeletons --> Archive
    StagedAnims --> Archive
    StagedTextures --> Archive
    StagedSounds --> Archive
    StagedUIs --> Archive
    StagedFonts --> Archive
    
    StagedShaders --> ShaderLib
    StagedShaders --> MetalLibs
```

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-326]()

## Platform-Specific Build Instructions

### Windows (Win32 and UWP)

#### Configuration

```bash
# Windows x64
cmake -A x64 -DRAVENGINE_BUILD_TESTS=ON ..

# Windows ARM64
cmake -A ARM64 -DRAVENGINE_BUILD_TESTS=ON ..

# UWP (GDK)
cmake -DCMAKE_SYSTEM_NAME=WindowsStore -DCMAKE_SYSTEM_VERSION="10.0" ..
```

#### Known Issues

- **Initial configuration must be run twice** on the first build (known bug)
- On Windows 10, clone with `--recursive` to get updated DXC

**Build Command:**
```bash
cmake --build . --config Release --target RavEngine YourApp
```

**Sources:** [README.md:78-80](), [.github/workflows/build.yml:91-107]()

---

### macOS, iOS, tvOS, visionOS

#### Configuration

```bash
# macOS (Universal Binary: x86_64 + arm64)
cmake -G "Xcode" -DCMAKE_OSX_ARCHITECTURES="x86_64;arm64" ..

# iOS
cmake -G "Xcode" -DCMAKE_SYSTEM_NAME=iOS \
  -DCMAKE_OSX_ARCHITECTURES="x86_64;arm64" \
  -DCMAKE_XCODE_ATTRIBUTE_CODE_SIGNING_ALLOWED="NO" ..

# tvOS
cmake -G "Xcode" -DCMAKE_SYSTEM_NAME=tvOS \
  -DCMAKE_OSX_ARCHITECTURES="x86_64;arm64" ..

# visionOS
cmake -G "Xcode" -DCMAKE_SYSTEM_NAME=visionOS \
  -DCMAKE_OSX_ARCHITECTURES="x86_64;arm64" ..
```

#### Build Command

```bash
cmake --build . --config Release --target RavEngine YourApp -- -quiet
```

#### Bundle Fixup

Apple platforms require bundle fixup for proper app structure:

```cmake
if(APPLE)
  INSTALL(CODE 
    "include(BundleUtilities)
    fixup_bundle(\"${CMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX}/$<CONFIGURATION>/${PROJECT_NAME}.app\" \"\" \"\")
    " 
    COMPONENT Runtime
  )
endif()
```

**Sources:** [README.md:66-74](), [.github/workflows/build.yml:70-89]()

---

### Linux

#### Install Dependencies (Ubuntu/Debian)

```bash
sudo apt update
sudo apt install cmake g++-13 gcc-13 ninja-build uuid-dev \
  libwayland-dev libxkbcommon-dev libasound2-dev libvulkan-dev \
  libx11-xcb-dev libxcb-dri2-0-dev libxcb-glx0-dev \
  libxcb-icccm4-dev libxcb-keysyms1-dev libxcb-randr0-dev \
  libxrandr-dev libxxf86vm-dev mesa-common-dev
```

#### Configuration

```bash
# GCC
CC=/usr/bin/gcc-13 CXX=/usr/bin/g++-13 cmake -G "Ninja" ..

# Clang
CC=/usr/bin/clang-18 CXX=/usr/bin/clang++-18 \
  cmake -G "Ninja" -DCMAKE_LINKER_TYPE=LLD ..
```

#### Build Command

```bash
cmake --build . --config Release --target RavEngine YourApp
```

**Platform Definitions:**
The build system automatically defines `POSIX` and `LINUX` for Linux builds.

**Sources:** [.github/workflows/build.yml:15-46](), [.github/workflows/build.yml:139-172]()

---

### Android

#### Prerequisites

- Android Studio 4.2+ with NDK 27+
- Host build tools (cmake, compilers) for the host OS

#### Configuration

```bash
# Set up NDK path
export NDK_PATH=/path/to/ndk/r27

# Configure for desired ABI
cmake -G "Ninja" \
  -DCMAKE_TOOLCHAIN_FILE="${NDK_PATH}/build/cmake/android.toolchain.cmake" \
  -DANDROID_ABI=arm64-v8a \
  -DANDROID_ARM_NEON=ON \
  -DANDROID_PLATFORM=33 \
  ..
```

#### Supported ABIs

- `arm64-v8a` (64-bit ARM)
- `armeabi-v7a` (32-bit ARM)
- `x86_64` (64-bit Intel/AMD)
- `x86` (32-bit Intel/AMD)

#### Build Command

```bash
cmake --build . --config Release --target RavEngine YourApp
```

**Special Notes:**
- SDL3 shared library on Android has no debug postfix (hardcoded)
- Requires linking against `camera2ndk` and `mediandk`
- For full app integration, use the [SDL Android Builder](https://github.com/Ravbug/sdl-android-builder/) wrapper project

**Sources:** [README.md:116-122](), [.github/workflows/build.yml:109-137](), [CMakeLists.txt:321-326]()

---

### Emscripten (WebAssembly)

#### Setup Emscripten SDK

```bash
# Clone and activate emsdk
git clone https://github.com/emscripten-core/emsdk.git --depth=1
cd emsdk
./emsdk install latest
./emsdk activate latest
source ./emsdk_env.sh
```

#### Configuration

```bash
emcmake cmake -G "Ninja" ..
```

#### Build Command

```bash
cmake --build . --config Release --target RavEngine
```

**Emscripten-Specific Settings:**
- Requires `-pthread`, `-fexceptions`
- WebGPU support via `-s USE_WEBGPU`
- Memory configuration: `-s ALLOW_MEMORY_GROWTH=1 -s MAXIMUM_MEMORY=4GB`

**Note:** Emscripten support is in early WIP stage.

**Sources:** [.github/workflows/build.yml:47-68](), [CMakeLists.txt:45-53]()

---

## Host Tools Overview

RavEngine includes several command-line tools for asset processing:

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph "Asset Importers"
        RVEMC["rvemc<br/>Mesh Compiler"]
        RVESKC["rveskc<br/>Skeleton Compiler"]
        RVEAC["rveac<br/>Animation Compiler"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Shader Tools"
        RVESC["rvesc<br/>Shader Compiler"]
        RGLC["rglc<br/>RGL Compiler Library"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Shared Libraries"
        ImportLib["rve_importlib<br/>Assimp wrapper"]
        LibRGLC["librglc<br/>Shader transpilation"]
    end
    
    subgraph "External Tools"
        PROTOC["protoc<br/>Protocol Buffers"]
        FLATC["flatc<br/>FlatBuffers"]
    end
    
    RVEMC --> ImportLib
    RVESKC --> ImportLib
    RVEAC --> ImportLib
    
    ImportLib --> Assimp["Assimp<br/>Model loading"]
    ImportLib --> MeshOpt["meshoptimizer<br/>Optimization"]
    
    RVESC --> RGLC
    RGLC --> LibRGLC
    
    LibRGLC --> SPIRV["SPIRV-Cross<br/>Transpilation"]
    LibRGLC --> DXC["DXC<br/>HLSL compilation"]
```

### Tool Descriptions

| Tool | Purpose | Input | Output |
|------|---------|-------|--------|
| **rvemc** | Mesh compiler | `.json` config + 3D model | `.rvem` (optimized mesh) |
| **rveskc** | Skeleton compiler | `.json` config + 3D model | `.rves` (Ozz skeleton) |
| **rveac** | Animation compiler | `.json` config + 3D model | `.rvea` (Ozz animation) |
| **rvesc** | Shader compiler | `.vsh/.fsh/.csh` GLSL | Platform-specific bytecode |
| **rglc** | RGL shader compiler library | GLSL | Metal/HLSL/SPIR-V |
| **protoc** | Protocol Buffers compiler | `.proto` | `.pb.h/.pb.cc` |
| **flatc** | FlatBuffers compiler | `.fbs` | `.h` headers |

**Sources:** [cmake/importers.cmake:1-37](), [cmake/rvesc.cmake:1-17](), [deps/host-tools/CMakeLists.txt:1-76]()

### Import Library (rve_importlib)

The `rve_importlib` library provides shared functionality for asset importers:

**Key Components:**
- Assimp integration for loading 3D model formats
- Format conversion utilities
- Mesh optimization via meshoptimizer
- Common data structures

**Location:** [tools/importlib/]()

**Dependencies:**
- Assimp
- fmt (formatting)
- glm (math)
- meshoptimizer (mesh optimization)

**Sources:** [cmake/importers.cmake:1-10](), [deps/host-tools/CMakeLists.txt:51-72]()

---

## Build Configuration Details

### Dependency Management

RavEngine uses `add_subdirectory` to include all dependencies directly in the build tree. Key dependencies are configured as follows:

#### Graphics and Rendering
- **RGL** (RavEngine Graphics Library): `deps/RGL`
- **SDL3**: `deps/SDL` (static on desktop, shared on Android)
- **RmlUi**: `deps/RmlUi` (UI framework)

#### Physics and Animation
- **PhysX**: `deps/physx/physx/compiler/public`
- **Ozz-animation**: `deps/ozz-animation`

#### Audio
- **Steam Audio**: `deps/SteamAudio-All`
- **Resonance Audio**: `deps/resonance-audio`
- **libnyquist**: `deps/libnyquist` (audio decoding)

#### Networking
- **GameNetworkingSockets**: `deps/GameNetworkingSockets`

#### Other
- **PhysFS**: `deps/physfs` (virtual filesystem)
- **Assimp**: `deps/assimp` (asset importing)
- **Tracy**: `deps/tracy` (profiling)

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:259-477]()

### Compiler Flags and Features

#### C++ Standard
```cmake
set(CMAKE_CXX_STANDARD 20)  # 17 for GCC due to PhysX compatibility
set(CMAKE_CXX_STANDARD_REQUIRED ON)
```

#### RTTI Disabled
RavEngine disables RTTI throughout the codebase except where necessary (e.g., Assimp):
```cmake
target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE "-fno-rtti")  # GCC/Clang
target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE "/GR-")       # MSVC
```

**Sources:** [cmake/rtti.cmake:1-31](), [CMakeLists.txt:479-484](), [CMakeLists.txt:587-588]()

#### Vectorization and Optimization
```cmake
# macOS/Linux
target_compile_options("${PROJECT_NAME}" PUBLIC -ffast-math -ffp-contract=fast)

# Link-Time Optimization (Profile and Release)
set_target_properties(${target} PROPERTIES
    INTERPROCEDURAL_OPTIMIZATION_RELEASE TRUE
    INTERPROCEDURAL_OPTIMIZATION_PROFILE TRUE
)
```

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:56-67](), [CMakeLists.txt:600-604]()

### Precompiled Headers

RavEngine uses precompiled headers on non-Apple platforms to accelerate builds:

```cmake
target_precompile_headers("${PROJECT_NAME}" PRIVATE 
    "<phmap.h>"
    "<vector>"
    "<algorithm>"
    "<functional>"
    # ... additional STL and library headers
)
```

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:606-625]()

```
build/

â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ RavEngine                # Engine library (static)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ YourApp                  # Your application executable
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ YourApp.rvedata          # Packed asset archive
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ YourApp_Streaming/       # Streaming assets (if any)
â”‚

â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ protobuf/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ RGL/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ RVESC/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ rvemc/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ rveac/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ rveskc/

â”œâ”€â”€ YourApp/                     # Asset staging directory
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ meshes/*.rvem
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ skeletons/*.rves
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ animations/*.rvea

â”‚   â””â”€â”€ fonts/*
â”‚
â””â”€â”€ YourApp_ShaderIntermediate/  # Compiled shader bytecode
    â””â”€â”€ ... platform-specific files
```

### Asset Archive Format

The `.rvedata` file is a **ZIP archive** containing all compiled assets:

```
YourApp.rvedata (ZIP)
â”œâ”€â”€ meshes/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ *.rvem
â”œâ”€â”€ skeletons/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ *.rves
â”œâ”€â”€ animations/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ *.rvea
â”œâ”€â”€ textures/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ *.png, *.jpg, *.dds, *.exr
â”œâ”€â”€ sounds/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ *.ogg, *.wav
â”œâ”€â”€ uis/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ *.rml, *.rcss
â””â”€â”€ fonts/
    â””â”€â”€ *.ttf
```

At runtime, this archive is mounted via **PhysFS** virtual filesystem.

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:273-324]()

### Platform-Specific Deployment

#### macOS/iOS/tvOS/visionOS
Assets are bundled in the `.app` package:
```
YourApp.app/
â”œâ”€â”€ Contents/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ MacOS/
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ YourApp
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Resources/
â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ YourApp.rvedata
â”‚       â””â”€â”€ YourApp_Streaming/  (if any)
```

#### Windows UWP
Assets are deployed to AppX package:
```
AppX/
â”œâ”€â”€ YourApp.exe
â”œâ”€â”€ YourApp.rvedata
â””â”€â”€ YourApp_Streaming/  (if any)
```

#### Windows (Win32) and Linux
Assets are copied next to the executable:
```
build/Release/
â”œâ”€â”€ YourApp
â”œâ”€â”€ YourApp.rvedata
â””â”€â”€ YourApp_Streaming/  (if any)
```

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:70-97](), [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:275-322]()

## Troubleshooting

### Common Issues

| Issue | Solution |
|-------|----------|
| **Windows: Build fails on first configure** | Run CMake configure twice on the first setup |
| **Linux: Audio backend not found** | Install either `alsa-lib-devel` or `pulseaudio-dev` |
| **Cross-compile: Tools not found** | Ensure host tools built successfully in `build/host-tools/` |
| **Apple: Shader debugging not working** | Check that `MTL_ENABLE_DEBUG_INFO` is set (automatic in non-Release) |
| **Emscripten: Link errors** | Ensure emsdk is properly activated in the current shell |

### Verifying Build Success

After building, check for these artifacts:

1. **Engine Library**: `build/<Config>/libRavEngine.a` (or `.lib` on Windows)
2. **Your Application**: `build/<Config>/YourApp`
3. **Asset Archive**: `build/<Config>/YourApp.rvedata` or in bundle
4. **Shader Resources**: 
   - Apple: `.metallib` files in app bundle
   - Other: `YourApp_ShaderResources` library linked into executable

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:1-897](), [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-326]()
