## Frame Execution Flow

Each frame, `RenderEngine::Draw()` is called with a `World` reference and one or more `RenderViewCollection` objects representing cameras/viewports. The method returns a `RGLCommandBufferPtr` containing all GPU commands for the frame.

### Execution Sequence

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant App
    participant World
    participant RenderEngine
    participant GPU
    
    App->>World: Tick(deltaTime)
    activate World
    
    Note over World: PreTick, TickECS, PostTick
    
    World->>World: Execute Render Tasks
    Note over World: Sync GPU buffers:<br/>worldTransforms, lights,<br/>mesh command lists
    
    World->>RenderEngine: Draw(world, renderTargets, scaleFactor)
    activate RenderEngine
    
    RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Reset Command Buffer
    RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Sync Private Data
    Note over RenderEngine: EncodeSync on<br/>transformSyncCommandBuffer
    
    RenderEngine->>GPU: Commit transformSyncCommandBuffer
    
    RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Skeletal Animation Compute
    RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Particle Update Compute
    
    loop For Each Camera
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Depth Prepass
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Build Depth Pyramid
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Cluster Lights
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: GPU Culling (Opaque)
        
        alt Shadows Enabled
            RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Shadow Map Rendering
        end
        
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Main Opaque Pass
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Skybox Pass
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: GPU Culling (Transparent)
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Transparent Pass
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Post-Processing
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: GUI Rendering
        RenderEngine->>RenderEngine: Debug Rendering
    end
    
    RenderEngine->>GPU: Submit mainCommandBuffer
    deactivate RenderEngine
    
    deactivate World
```

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:98-2460](), [src/World.cpp:54-74]()

### Entry Point: RenderEngine::Draw

The `Draw` method begins by resetting the transient buffer offset and command buffer, then synchronizes render data from the `World`:

**Key Steps:**
1. **Reset Resources** - Resets `mainCommandBuffer` and destroys unused GPU resources
2. **Sync Private Buffers** - Calls `EncodeSync()` on `BufferedVRAMVector` and `BufferedVRAMSparseSet` to transfer host data to GPU
3. **Compute Cascaded Shadow Maps** - Calculates directional light shadow matrices for each cascade and camera
4. **Prepare Skeletal Meshes** - Resizes buffers and prepares indirect draw commands for skinned meshes
5. **Execute Multi-Pass Pipeline** - Iterates through all cameras, executing the full rendering pipeline for each

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:98-473](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:110-304]()

---

## Multi-Pass Rendering Pipeline

RavEngine uses a **deferred-style multi-pass forward+ renderer** with GPU-driven culling and indirect rendering. Each camera executes the following passes in sequence:

### Pass Breakdown

| Pass # | Name | Purpose | Depth Mode | Render Pass | Key Features |
|--------|------|---------|------------|-------------|--------------|
| 1 | **Depth Prepass** | Write depth and view-space normals | `Greater` (Reversed-Z) | `depthPrepassRenderPassLit` | Early Z-test optimization |
| 2 | **Depth Pyramid** | Generate hierarchical depth mipmap | N/A (Compute) | `depthPyramidPipeline` | Used for occlusion culling |
| 3 | **Light Clustering** | Assign lights to 3D grid tiles | N/A (Compute) | `clusterPopulatePipeline` | Forward+ light assignment |
| 4 | **GPU Culling (Opaque)** | Frustum/occlusion/LOD culling | N/A (Compute) | `defaultCullingComputePipeline` | Writes indirect commands |
| 5 | **Shadow Mapping** | Render shadow maps for lights | `Greater` | `shadowRenderPass` | Directional, point, spot |
| 6 | **Main Opaque Pass** | Render opaque geometry | `Equal` | `litRenderPass` / `unlitRenderPass` | Deferred-style equality test |
| 7 | **Skybox** | Render environment background | Read-only | `envSkyboxPass` | Screen-space quad |
| 8 | **GPU Culling (Transparent)** | Cull transparent objects | N/A (Compute) | `defaultCullingComputePipeline` | Separate from opaque |
| 9 | **Transparent Rendering** | Order-independent transparency | Read-only | `litTransparentPass` | MLAB (Multi-Layer Alpha) |
| 10 | **AO/SSGI** | Ambient occlusion and GI | N/A (Compute) | `gtaoPipeline` / `ssgipipeline` | Optional screen-space effects |
| 11 | **Post-Processing** | Bloom, DOF, etc. | None | `postProcessRenderPass` | User-defined stack |
| 12 | **Tonemap** | HDR to LDR conversion | None | Final blit | Linear to sRGB |
| 13 | **GUI** | RmlUi UI elements | Read-only | `finalRenderPass` | Alpha blending |
| 14 | **Debug Draw** | Im3d debug overlays | Read-only | `finalRenderPass` | Wireframe, points, lines |

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:632-2460]()

### Depth Prepass and Reversed-Z

The depth prepass writes depth values using **reversed-Z** (`depthFunction = Greater`) for improved depth precision. This writes `z=1.0` at the near plane and `z=0.0` at the far plane. View-space normals are also written for SSAO/SSGI.

```cpp
// Depth function configured in render pipeline
depthFunction = RGL::DepthCompareFunction::Greater
```

The main opaque pass then uses `depthFunction = Equal` to perform an **early-Z optimization** (sometimes called "Z-prepass occlusion"), rejecting fragments that don't match the prepass depth.

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:781-893](), [src/RenderEngine.cpp:628-653]()

### Clustered Forward+ Lighting

Light assignment uses a **3D grid** of clusters covering the view frustum. The compute pipeline `clusterPopulatePipeline` iterates all lights and assigns them to overlapping clusters:

| Parameter | Value | Purpose |
|-----------|-------|---------|
| `gridSizeX` | 12 | Horizontal tiles |
| `gridSizeY` | 12 | Vertical tiles |
| `gridSizeZ` | 24 | Depth slices |
| `numClusters` | 3456 | Total clusters (12Ã—12Ã—24) |

Each cluster stores indices of point lights (max `CLUSTER_MAX_POINTS`) and spot lights (max `CLUSTER_MAX_SPOTS`) overlapping it. During shading, fragments query their cluster to retrieve affecting lights.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:47-61](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:931-1005]()

---

## GPU-Driven Rendering

RavEngine uses **GPU-driven rendering** to maximize parallelism and reduce CPU overhead. All culling and draw command generation happens on the GPU via compute shaders.

### GPU Culling Pipeline

```mermaid
graph LR
    Input["Input Data:<br/>- Model Matrices<br/>- Bounding Spheres<br/>- Entity IDs<br/>- Render Layers"]
    
    CullShader["defaultcull.csh<br/>Compute Shader<br/>(64 threads/group)"]
    
    Frustum["Frustum Culling<br/>CullSphere()"]
    Occlusion["Occlusion Culling<br/>Depth Pyramid Query"]
    LOD["LOD Selection<br/>Distance-based"]
    
    IndirectBuffer["Indirect Draw Buffer<br/>IndirectCommand structs"]
    EntityIDBuffer["Entity ID Buffer<br/>Visible entity IDs"]
    
    Input --> CullShader
    CullShader --> Frustum
    Frustum --> Occlusion
    Occlusion --> LOD
    LOD --> IndirectBuffer
    LOD --> EntityIDBuffer
    
    IndirectBuffer --> DrawIndirect["GPU Indirect Draw<br/>vkCmdDrawIndexedIndirect"]
```

**Sources:** [shaders/defaultcull.csh:1-315](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:1091-1281]()

### Culling Shader Structure

The `defaultcull.csh` compute shader ([shaders/defaultcull.csh:1-315]()) executes per-entity and performs:

1. **Render Layer Filtering** - Tests if entity layers intersect camera layers
2. **Attribute Check** - Reads per-object flags (frustum culling enabled, casts shadows, etc.)
3. **Frustum Culling** - Projects bounding sphere against 6 frustum planes
4. **Occlusion Culling** - Queries depth pyramid at appropriate mip level to test visibility
5. **LOD Selection** - Chooses LOD based on camera distance using "Price Is Right" rules
6. **Atomic Increment** - Atomically increments `instanceCount` in indirect buffer and writes entity ID

**Key Data Structures:**

```cpp
struct CUBO {
    uint32_t indirectBufferOffset;
    uint32_t numObjects;
    uint32_t cullingBufferOffset;
    float radius;  // Bounding sphere radius
    uint32_t numLODs;
    uint32_t idOutputBufferBindlessHandle;
    uint32_t entityIDInputBufferBindlessHandle;
    uint32_t indirectOutputBufferBindlessHandle;
    uint32_t lodDistanceBufferBindlessHandle;
};
```

**Sources:** [shaders/defaultcull.csh:7-17](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:212-222]()

### Indirect Rendering

After culling, the GPU directly consumes the updated `IndirectCommand` buffer:

```cpp
struct IndirectCommand {
    uint32_t indexCount;
    uint32_t instanceCount;  // Written by compute shader
    uint32_t indexStart;
    uint32_t baseVertex;
    uint32_t baseInstance;
};
```

The `instanceCount` starts at 0 and is atomically incremented by the culling shader for each visible entity. Rendering uses `DrawIndexedIndirect()` to process all instances in a single draw call per material/mesh combination.

**Sources:** [shaders/defaultcull.csh:37-43](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:1368-1492]()

### Occlusion Culling via Depth Pyramid

The depth pyramid is a hierarchical mipmap chain of the depth buffer, where each mip level stores the **minimum depth** of a 2Ã—2 quad from the previous level. The culling shader projects an entity's bounding sphere to screen space, selects the appropriate mip level based on screen size, and samples the 4 corners to determine visibility.

**Depth Pyramid Generation:**
- Format: `R32_Float` ([include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:144]())
- Method: Compute shader `depthPyramidPipeline` with reduction sampler (or software emulation on Metal/WebGPU)
- Levels: Automatically generated down to 1Ã—1

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:895-929](), [shaders/defaultcull.csh:222-274]()

---

## Render Data Synchronization

The `World` maintains parallel GPU-friendly copies of component data in its `RenderData` structure. These are synchronized from the ECS during the `World::Tick()` render tasks phase.

### World::RenderData Structure

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "CPU Side (World ECS)"
        TransformComp["Transform Components<br/>Local matrices, dirty flags"]
        LightComp["Light Components<br/>Directional, Point, Spot, Ambient"]
        MeshComp["Mesh Components<br/>StaticMesh, SkinnedMesh"]
    end
    
    subgraph "GPU-Friendly Parallel Storage (World::RenderData)"
        WorldTransforms["BufferedVRAMVector<br/>worldTransforms<br/>Per-entity matrices"]
        DirLightData["BufferedVRAMSparseSet<br/>directionalLightData<br/>Per-light upload data"]
        PointLightData["BufferedVRAMSparseSet<br/>pointLightData"]
        SpotLightData["BufferedVRAMSparseSet<br/>spotLightData"]
        AmbientLightData["BufferedVRAMSparseSet<br/>ambientLightData"]
        RenderLayers["BufferedVRAMVector<br/>renderLayers<br/>Per-entity layer masks"]
        PerObjectAttrs["BufferedVRAMVector<br/>perObjectAttributes<br/>Per-entity flags"]
        StaticMeshData["OrderedMap<MaterialSort, MDIICommand><br/>staticMeshRenderData"]
        SkinnedMeshData["OrderedMap<MaterialSort, MDIICommandSkinned><br/>skinnedMeshRenderData"]
    end
    
    subgraph "GPU Side (Private Buffers)"
        TransformBuffer["RGL Private Buffer<br/>Transform SSBO"]
        LightBuffers["RGL Private Buffers<br/>Light SSBOs"]
        IndirectBuffers["RGL Indirect Buffers<br/>Per-material MDI commands"]
    end
    
    TransformComp --> WorldTransforms
    LightComp --> DirLightData
    LightComp --> PointLightData
    LightComp --> SpotLightData
    LightComp --> AmbientLightData
    MeshComp --> StaticMeshData
    MeshComp --> SkinnedMeshData
    
    WorldTransforms -- "EncodeSync()" --> TransformBuffer
    DirLightData -- "EncodeSync()" --> LightBuffers
    PointLightData -- "EncodeSync()" --> LightBuffers
    SpotLightData -- "EncodeSync()" --> LightBuffers
    AmbientLightData -- "EncodeSync()" --> LightBuffers
    RenderLayers -- "EncodeSync()" --> TransformBuffer
    PerObjectAttrs -- "EncodeSync()" --> TransformBuffer
    
    StaticMeshData --> IndirectBuffers
    SkinnedMeshData --> IndirectBuffers
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:418-449](), [src/World.cpp:311-521]()

### BufferedVRAMVector and BufferedVRAMSparseSet

These templated containers ([include/RavEngine/VRAMSparseSet.hpp](), not shown in provided files) maintain:
- **Host-side buffer** - Modified by ECS systems during `World::Tick()`
- **Staging buffer** - Shared memory for CPU writes
- **Private buffer** - GPU-only memory for shader reads

The `EncodeSync()` method compares the host and staging buffers, and if they differ, records a copy command from staging to private on the provided command buffer.

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:112-147]()

### Transform Dirty Tracking

The `Transform` component tracks modifications via a `isTickDirty` flag. During render tasks, dirty transforms trigger updates to `worldTransforms`:

```cpp
if (transform.isTickDirty && mesh.GetEnabled()) {
    auto ownerID = transform.GetOwner().GetID();
    renderData.worldTransforms.SetValueAt(ownerID.id, transform.GetWorldMatrix());
    transform.ClearTickDirty();
}
```

**Sources:** [src/World.cpp:330-365](), [src/World.cpp:392-427]()

### Material-Based Mesh Grouping

Meshes are grouped by material in `OrderedMap<MaterialSort, MDIICommand>`. Each `MDIICommand` contains:
- **commands** - Vector of mesh/skeleton pairs
- **entities** - `BufferedVRAMSparseSet` of entity IDs for this material
- **indirectBuffer** - GPU buffer of `IndirectCommand` structs for indirect rendering
- **cullingBuffer** - Output buffer of visible entity IDs from culling shader

This structure enables efficient material batching and minimizes draw call overhead.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:334-362]()

---

## Command Buffer Management

RavEngine uses three primary command buffers for different stages of frame execution:

| Command Buffer | Purpose | Submission | Wait Condition |
|----------------|---------|------------|----------------|
| `transformSyncCommandBuffer` | Uploads host data to GPU private buffers (transforms, lights, mesh data) | After render data sync, before main rendering | Implicit (same queue guarantee) |
| `mainCommandBuffer` | Encodes all rendering commands (compute, rasterization, present) | After full pipeline execution | Presented to screen |
| `transientCommandBuffer` | Uploads transient data for the current frame | After transient writes, before reads | Explicit (`BlockUntilCompleted()`) |

### Transient Buffer

The transient buffer is a 32MB staging buffer reset every frame for temporary data like shader uniforms. The `WriteTransient()` method appends data and returns an offset:

```cpp
uint32_t RenderEngine::WriteTransient(RGL::untyped_span data) {
    auto offset = transientOffset;
    std::memcpy(static_cast<char*>(transientStagingBuffer->GetMappedDataPtr()) + offset, 
                data.data(), data.size());
    transientOffset += data.size();
    return offset;
}
```

Before reading on the GPU, the staging buffer is copied to the private buffer via `transientCommandBuffer`, which blocks until completion.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:324-333](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:469-472]()

### Multi-Threaded Safety

Command buffer encoding is **not thread-safe** by design. All encoding happens on the main thread during `RenderEngine::Draw()`. However, `World::Tick()` runs ECS systems in parallel using Taskflow, and these systems update `RenderData` structures that are later synchronized to the GPU.

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:98-108]()

---

## Integration with World

The `World` class prepares render data asynchronously during its tick phase via Taskflow tasks, then synchronously calls `RenderEngine::Draw()`:

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant World
    participant ECS_Systems
    participant RenderTasks
    participant RenderEngine
    
    World->>ECS_Systems: Execute TickECS
    Note over ECS_Systems: PhysicsLinkSystem,<br/>AnimatorSystem, etc.
    
    par Async Render Data Preparation
        World->>RenderTasks: updateRenderDataStaticMesh
        World->>RenderTasks: updateRenderDataSkinnedMesh
        World->>RenderTasks: updateInvalidatedDirs
        World->>RenderTasks: updateInvalidatedSpots
        World->>RenderTasks: updateInvalidatedPoints
        World->>RenderTasks: updateInvalidatedAmbients
    end
    
    RenderTasks->>RenderTasks: Wait for All Tasks
    
    World->>RenderEngine: Draw(world, renderTargets, scaleFactor)
```

**Sources:** [src/World.cpp:54-74](), [src/World.cpp:311-521]()

### Render Task Graph

The render tasks are configured during `World::setupRenderTasks()` and include:
1. **Resize Buffer** - Ensures `worldTransforms` can hold all entities
2. **Update Static Mesh Data** - Synchronizes dirty transform matrices for static meshes
3. **Update Skinned Mesh Data** - Synchronizes dirty transform matrices for skinned meshes
4. **Update Particle Systems** - Synchronizes particle emitter transforms
5. **Update Invalidated Lights** - Copies light color/intensity/shadow data to GPU structures

These tasks run in parallel using Taskflow and complete before `RenderEngine::Draw()` is called.

**Sources:** [src/World.cpp:311-521]()

---

## GPU Resource Management

### Unified Vertex/Index Buffers

All meshes share two large GPU buffers:
- **Vertex Buffer** - Stores per-attribute data (`sharedPositionBuffer`, `sharedNormalBuffer`, etc.)
- **Index Buffer** - Stores triangle indices (`sharedIndexBuffer`)

Meshes allocate ranges from these buffers using free lists (`vertexFreeList`, `indexFreeList`). When a buffer fills up, it's reallocated to a larger size (next power of 2), and existing allocations are copied.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:335-342](), [src/RenderEngine.cpp:1061-1062]()

### Bindless Resources

RavEngine uses **bindless textures** and **bindless buffers** (via descriptor indexing extensions) to avoid descriptor set binding overhead. Resources are assigned bindless handles and accessed via dynamic indexing in shaders:

```glsl
layout(set = 3, binding = 0) buffer idOutputBlock { 
    uint entityIDsToRender[]; 
} idOutputBufferArray[];

// Access via bindless handle
idOutputBufferArray[cubo.idOutputBufferBindlessHandle].entityIDsToRender[idx] = entityID;
```

**Sources:** [shaders/defaultcull.csh:56-60](), [shaders/defaultcull.csh:312]()

### Garbage Collection

Unused GPU resources are queued for deferred deletion using concurrent queues:
- `gcBuffers` - Buffers to destroy
- `gcTextures` - Textures to destroy
- `gcPipelineLayout` - Pipeline layouts to destroy
- `gcRenderPipeline` - Render pipelines to destroy

These are processed at the start of each frame by `DestroyUnusedResources()`.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:311-314](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:104]()

---

## Performance Characteristics

### GPU-Driven Benefits

| Optimization | CPU Impact | GPU Impact | Benefit |
|--------------|------------|------------|---------|
| **GPU Culling** | No CPU iteration over entities | Parallel compute execution | Scales to millions of objects |
| **Indirect Rendering** | One draw call per material | GPU reads commands directly | Minimal driver overhead |
| **Bindless Resources** | No descriptor set updates | Direct array indexing | No descriptor limits |
| **Occlusion Culling** | Zero CPU involvement | Hierarchical depth queries | Automatic visibility optimization |
| **LOD Selection** | No CPU distance calculations | Per-entity LOD in shader | Precise level selection |

### Multi-Pass Overhead

Each camera/viewport incurs a full pipeline execution. For split-screen or multi-view rendering, passes scale linearly with the number of views. Shadow maps add additional passes (one per shadowing light).

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:632-2460]()

---

## Summary

RavEngine's rendering architecture is designed around:
1. **GPU-driven culling and rendering** to minimize CPU overhead
2. **Multi-pass forward+ pipeline** with deferred-style depth prepass for optimal performance
3. **Efficient data synchronization** between ECS `World` and GPU via parallel data structures
4. **Material-based batching** with indirect rendering to reduce draw calls
5. **Bindless resources** for scalable descriptor management

The `RenderEngine::Draw()` method serves as the central orchestrator, executing a sophisticated pipeline of compute and rasterization passes to produce the final frame from high-level ECS component data.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:63-364](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:98-2460](), [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:418-449]()23:T6231,# Materials and Shaders

The material and shader system provides the interface between application-level rendering intent and GPU execution. Materials define rendering pipelines, manage shader programs, and configure GPU state for drawing geometry. This system supports physically-based rendering (PBR), unlit shading, custom materials, and transparency with multiple pipeline variants for different rendering passes.

For information about the broader rendering pipeline execution, see [Rendering Architecture](#4.1). For lighting computations, see [Lighting System](#4.3).

## Material System Architecture

The material system consists of three primary layers: **Material** classes defining shader pipelines and GPU state, **MaterialInstance** classes holding per-object parameters and resource bindings, and the shader compilation infrastructure that produces platform-specific bytecode.

### Class Hierarchy

```mermaid
graph TB
    Material["Material<br/>Base class<br/>Pipeline management"]
    LitMaterial["LitMaterial<br/>Physically-based lighting<br/>Shadow/cluster support"]
    UnlitMaterial["UnlitMaterial<br/>No lighting computation<br/>Simpler bindings"]
    PBRMaterial["PBRMaterial<br/>Full PBR workflow<br/>Texture inputs"]
    PBRMaterialBaked["PBRMaterialBaked<br/>PBR + lightmap UV"]
    
    MaterialInstance["MaterialInstance<br/>Per-object settings<br/>Buffer/texture bindings"]
    PBRMaterialInstance["PBRMaterialInstance<br/>Albedo/normal/metallic/etc<br/>Push constants"]
    
    MaterialVariant["MaterialVariant<br/>std::variant wrapper<br/>Type erasure"]
    
    Material --> LitMaterial
    Material --> UnlitMaterial
    LitMaterial --> PBRMaterial
    PBRMaterial --> PBRMaterialBaked
    
    MaterialInstance --> PBRMaterialInstance
    
    LitMaterial -.->|"referenced by"| MaterialVariant
    UnlitMaterial -.->|"referenced by"| MaterialVariant
    MaterialVariant -.->|"held by"| MaterialInstance
    
    MaterialManager["Material::Manager<br/>WeakReadThroughCache<br/>Singleton access"]
    MaterialManager -.->|"caches"| Material
    
    StaticMesh["StaticMesh<br/>Component"]
    SkinnedMeshComponent["SkinnedMeshComponent<br/>Component"]
    
    StaticMesh -.->|"holds Ref"| MaterialInstance
    SkinnedMeshComponent -.->|"holds Ref"| MaterialInstance
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:1-224](), [include/RavEngine/BuiltinMaterials.hpp:1-96](), [include/RavEngine/StaticMesh.hpp:1-62](), [include/RavEngine/SkinnedMeshComponent.hpp:1-53]()

## Material Base Class

The `Material` class ([include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:45-115]()) represents a complete rendering pipeline configuration. Each material creates multiple pipeline variants for different rendering passes.

### Pipeline Variants

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Material Construction"
        MaterialConfig["MaterialConfig<br/>Vertex layout<br/>Blend config<br/>Bindings"]
        VertexShader["Vertex Shader<br/>name_vsh"]
        FragmentShader["Fragment Shader<br/>name_fsh"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Pipeline Creation"
        MainPipeline["renderPipeline<br/>Main rendering<br/>depthFunction=Equal if opaque"]
        ShadowPipeline["shadowRenderPipeline<br/>Depth-only<br/>Backface culling<br/>name_vsh_shadow + name_fsh_shadow"]
        DepthPrepass["depthPrepassPipeline<br/>Depth + normals<br/>depthFunction=Greater<br/>name_vsh_prepass + name_fsh_prepass"]
    end
    
    MaterialConfig --> MainPipeline
    VertexShader --> MainPipeline
    FragmentShader --> MainPipeline
    
    MaterialConfig --> ShadowPipeline
    MaterialConfig --> DepthPrepass
    
    OpacityMode{"OpacityMode?"}
    OpacityMode -->|"Opaque"| CreatePrepass["Create depth prepass<br/>and shadow pipelines"]
    OpacityMode -->|"Transparent"| SkipVariants["No shadow/prepass<br/>MLAB bindings added"]
    
    CreatePrepass --> ShadowPipeline
    CreatePrepass --> DepthPrepass
```

**Sources:** [src/Material.cpp:30-196](), [include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:99-103]()

### Material Configuration

The `MaterialConfig` struct ([include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:19-33]()) defines all pipeline state:

| Field | Type | Purpose |
|-------|------|---------|
| `vertConfig` | `VertexConfig` | Vertex buffer bindings and attribute locations |
| `colorBlendConfig` | `ColorBlendConfig` | Main pass color attachment formats and blending |
| `depthPrepassColorBlendConfig` | `ColorBlendConfig` | Depth prepass attachment configuration |
| `bindings` | `vector<LayoutBindingDesc>` | Shader resource bindings (buffers, textures, samplers) |
| `pushConstantSize` | `uint32_t` | Size of push constant data in bytes |
| `cullMode` | `RGL::CullMode` | Face culling mode (Back/Front/None) |
| `opacityMode` | `OpacityMode` | Opaque or Transparent rendering |
| `requiredAttributes` | `MeshAttributes` | Which vertex attributes are required |
| `verbatimConfig` | `bool` | Skip automatic binding injection (for special materials) |

The constructor ([src/Material.cpp:32-196]()) performs several automatic augmentations:
- Adds model matrix binding at slot `MODEL_MATRIX_BINDING` (10) unless `verbatimConfig` is true
- Adds entity ID vertex input at location `ENTITY_INPUT_LOCATION` unless `verbatimConfig` is true  
- Trims unused vertex attributes based on `requiredAttributes`
- Creates shadow and depth prepass variants for opaque materials

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:19-33](), [src/Material.cpp:30-196]()

## LitMaterial and UnlitMaterial

### LitMaterial

`LitMaterial` ([include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:136-142]()) extends `Material` for physically-based lighting. The constructor automatically adds bindings required for lighting computation:

```mermaid

        B11["Binding 11: Engine constants<br/>StorageBuffer<br/>Camera, light counts"]
        B12["Binding 12: Ambient lights<br/>StorageBuffer"]
        B13["Binding 13: Directional lights<br/>StorageBuffer"]
        B14["Binding 14: Shadow sampler<br/>Sampler"]
        B15["Binding 15: Point lights<br/>StorageBuffer"]
        B16["Binding 16: Light clusters<br/>StorageBuffer"]
        B17["Binding 17: Spot lights<br/>StorageBuffer"]
        B28["Binding 28: Render layers<br/>StorageBuffer"]
        B29["Binding 29: Per-object flags<br/>StorageBuffer"]
        B30["Binding 30: Dir light varying<br/>StorageBuffer"]
        B31["Binding 31: Environment sampler<br/>Sampler"]
        Bindless1["Binding 1 Set 1: Shadow maps<br/>Bindless texture2D array<br/>2048 slots"]
        Bindless2["Binding 2 Set 2: Cubemaps<br/>Bindless textureCube array<br/>2048 slots"]
    end
    
    TransparentCheck{"opacityMode ==<br/>Transparent?"}
    
    MLABBindings["Bindings 23-27:<br/>Storage images for<br/>Multi-Layer Alpha Blending"]
    
    UserBindings --> Augment["augmentLitMaterialBindings()"]

    Augment --> TransparentCheck

    TransparentCheck -->|"No"| SkipMLAB["Skip MLAB bindings"]
```

The fragment shader receives these bindings and performs full lighting computation including shadow mapping, clustered forward+ lighting, and image-based lighting (IBL).

**Sources:** [src/Material.cpp:208-343](), [src/Material.cpp:345-358](), [tools/rvesc/lit_mesh.fsh:63-117]()

### UnlitMaterial

`UnlitMaterial` ([include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:146-161]()) provides simpler rendering without lighting. It only adds:
- Binding 11: Engine constants (for camera matrices)
- Bindings 23-27: MLAB storage images (if transparent)

This makes unlit materials lighter on GPU resources and faster to execute.

**Sources:** [src/Material.cpp:360-408](), [src/Material.cpp:410-419]()

## Built-in Materials

### PBRMaterial

The `PBRMaterial` ([include/RavEngine/BuiltinMaterials.hpp:17-21]()) implements a complete physically-based rendering workflow with texture inputs:

| Binding | Purpose | Default Texture |
|---------|---------|-----------------|
| 0 | Material sampler | - |
| 1 | Albedo texture | `Texture::Manager::defaultTexture` (white) |
| 2 | Normal map | `Texture::Manager::defaultNormalTexture` (flat) |
| 3 | Specular texture | `Texture::Manager::defaultTexture` |
| 4 | Metallic texture | `Texture::Manager::defaultTexture` |
| 5 | Roughness texture | `Texture::Manager::defaultTexture` |
| 6 | Ambient occlusion | `Texture::Manager::defaultTexture` |
| 7 | Emissive texture | `Texture::Manager::zeroTexture` (black) |
| 8 | Lightmap (baked only) | `Texture::Manager::zeroTexture` |

The material uses push constants ([include/RavEngine/BuiltinMaterials.hpp:10-15]()) for scalar tinting:

```cpp
struct PBRPushConstantData {
    ColorRGBA color{1,1,1,1};         // Albedo tint
    float metallicTint = 0;            // Metallic multiplier
    float roughnessTint = 0.4;         // Roughness multiplier
    float specularTint = 0.5;          // Specular multiplier
};
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/BuiltinMaterials.hpp:10-25](), [src/BuiltinMaterials.cpp:161-224]()

### PBRMaterialBaked

`PBRMaterialBaked` ([include/RavEngine/BuiltinMaterials.hpp:23-25]()) extends `PBRMaterial` with lightmap UV support. It uses shaders `pbr_baked_vsh` and `pbr_baked_fsh` which read the lightmap UV attribute.

**Sources:** [src/BuiltinMaterials.cpp:226-233]()

### Default Vertex Configuration

The `defaultVertexConfig` ([src/BuiltinMaterials.cpp:13-78]()) defines the standard vertex layout used by most materials:


Materials can specify `requiredAttributes` in `MeshAttributes` to trim unused buffers, reducing bandwidth and storage.

**Sources:** [src/BuiltinMaterials.cpp:13-78](), [src/Material.cpp:94-133]()

## Shader System

### Shader Loading

Materials load pre-compiled shaders using `LoadShaderByFilename()` ([src/Material.cpp:46-47]()):

```mermaid
graph LR
    MaterialName["Material name:<br/>'pbr'"]
    
    VertexName["Vertex shader:<br/>'pbr_vsh'"]
    FragmentName["Fragment shader:<br/>'pbr_fsh'"]
    
    Variants["Pipeline variants:<br/>'pbr_vsh_shadow'<br/>'pbr_fsh_shadow'<br/>'pbr_vsh_prepass'<br/>'pbr_fsh_prepass'"]
    
    TBDR{"Platform supports<br/>tile-based rendering?"}
    TBDRSuffix["Append '_tbdr'<br/>to transparent shaders"]
    
    MaterialName --> VertexName
    MaterialName --> FragmentName
    
    OpacityCheck{"Transparent?"}
    OpacityCheck -->|"Yes"| TBDR
    OpacityCheck -->|"No"| Variants
    
    TBDR -->|"Yes"| TBDRSuffix
    TBDR -->|"No"| Variants
    
    ShaderModule["RGL::ShaderModule<br/>Platform-specific bytecode<br/>Metal/SPIR-V/DXIL"]
    
    VertexName --> ShaderModule
    FragmentName --> ShaderModule
    Variants --> ShaderModule
    TBDRSuffix --> ShaderModule
```

Shaders are compiled at build-time by `rvesc` and embedded into the application. On Apple platforms, they're compiled into Metal libraries; on other platforms, CMRC embeds them as resources.

**Sources:** [src/Material.cpp:36-47](), [src/Material.cpp:169-194]()

### Shader Structure

Fragment shaders implement a user-defined `frag()` function that returns material properties:

```glsl
// From tools/rvesc/lit_mesh.fsh:13-21
struct LitOutput{
    vec4 color;           // Albedo + alpha
    vec3 normal;          // Surface normal (tangent space)
    vec3 emissiveColor;   // Emissive contribution
    float roughness;      // Surface roughness [0,1]
    float specular;       // Specular intensity
    float metallic;       // Metallic factor [0,1]
    float ao;             // Ambient occlusion
};

// User implements this function
LitOutput frag(EnvironmentData envData);
```

The engine-provided `main()` ([tools/rvesc/lit_mesh.fsh:119-374]()) calls `frag()` and applies lighting:

```mermaid
graph TD
    FragMain["main() entry"]
    
    GetModel["Get model matrix<br/>model[varyingEntityID]"]
    BuildTBN["Construct TBN matrix<br/>from vertex data"]
    
    CallUserFrag["LitOutput user_out = frag()"]
    
    AlphaTest{"user_out.color.a < 0.5?"}
    AlphaTest -->|"Yes (opaque only)"| Discard["discard"]
    AlphaTest -->|"No"| TransformNormal
    
    TransformNormal["Transform normal to world space<br/>worldNormal = mat3(entityModelMtx) * objectSpaceNormal"]
    
    DepthPrepass{"RVE_PREPASS?"}
    DepthPrepass -->|"Yes"| WriteViewNormal["Write view-space normal<br/>outViewSpaceNormal"]
    DepthPrepass -->|"No"| DepthOnly
    
    DepthOnly{"RVE_DEPTHONLY?"}
    DepthOnly -->|"Yes"| End["return"]
    DepthOnly -->|"No"| LightLoop
    
    subgraph "Lighting Computation"
        LightLoop["Iterate ambient lights<br/>IBL + BRDF"]
        DirLights["Iterate directional lights<br/>Shadow mapping<br/>Cascaded PCF"]
        ClusterLookup["Compute cluster index<br/>from fragment position"]
        PointLights["Iterate clustered point lights<br/>Cubemap shadows"]
        SpotLights["Iterate clustered spot lights<br/>Shadow mapping"]
        Emissive["Add emissive component"]
    end
    
    TransformNormal --> DepthPrepass
    WriteViewNormal --> LightLoop
    LightLoop --> DirLights
    DirLights --> ClusterLookup
    ClusterLookup --> PointLights
    PointLights --> SpotLights
    SpotLights --> Emissive
    
    Transparent{"RVE_TRANSPARENT?"}
    Emissive --> Transparent
    
    Transparent -->|"Yes"| MLAB["writeTransparency()<br/>Multi-layer alpha blending"]
    Transparent -->|"No"| WriteColor["result = outcolor"]
    
    MLAB --> End
    WriteColor --> End
    
    FragMain --> GetModel
    GetModel --> BuildTBN
    BuildTBN --> CallUserFrag
    CallUserFrag --> AlphaTest
```

**Sources:** [tools/rvesc/lit_mesh.fsh:13-374](), [shaders/lit_mesh_shared.glsl:1-23]()

### Engine Data Bindings

The fragment shader receives engine data through structured buffers ([shaders/lit_mesh_shared.glsl:1-23]()):

```glsl
// Binding 10: Model matrices
layout(std430, binding = MODEL_MATRIX_BINDING) readonly buffer modelMatrixBuffer{
    mat4 model[];
};

// Binding 11: Engine constants
layout(scalar, binding = 11) readonly buffer lightAuxDataSSBO{
    EngineData_Internal engineConstants[];
};
```

The `EngineData_Internal` struct contains camera matrices, screen dimensions, light counts, and clustering parameters.

**Sources:** [shaders/lit_mesh_shared.glsl:1-23](), [tools/rvesc/lit_mesh.fsh:63-111]()

## Material Management

### Material Manager

Materials are cached using a weak reference cache ([include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:57-81]()):

```cpp
// Get or create a material
auto pbr = Material::Manager::Get<PBRMaterial>();

// Get with custom key (for material variants)
auto customKey = std::hash<std::string>{}("custom_variant");
auto variant = Material::Manager::GetWithKey<PBRMaterial>(customKey, options);

// Remove expired weak references
Material::Manager::Compact<PBRMaterial>();
```

The cache uses `GenericWeakReadThroughCache` which stores `WeakRef<T>` and constructs new instances on cache miss.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:57-81]()

### MaterialVariant Type Erasure

`MaterialVariant` ([include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:163-178]()) wraps `std::variant<Ref<LitMaterial>, Ref<UnlitMaterial>>` to provide uniform access to different material types:

```cpp
struct MaterialVariant {
    PipelineUseConfiguration GetShadowRenderPipeline() const;
    PipelineUseConfiguration GetMainRenderPipeline() const;
    PipelineUseConfiguration GetDepthPrepassPipeline() const;
    
private:
    std::variant<Ref<LitMaterial>, Ref<UnlitMaterial>> variant;
};
```

This allows `MaterialInstance` to hold any material type without templates.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:163-178](), [src/Material.cpp:422-468]()

## Creating Custom Materials

### Custom LitMaterial

To create a custom lit material with additional textures:

```cpp
struct MyCustomMaterial : public LitMaterial {
    MyCustomMaterial() : LitMaterial("my_shader", {
        .bindings = {
            // Binding 0-9: Your custom resources
            {
                .binding = 0,
                .type = RGL::BindingType::Sampler,
                .stageFlags = RGL::BindingVisibility::Fragment,
            },
            {
                .binding = 1,
                .type = RGL::BindingType::SampledImage,
                .stageFlags = RGL::BindingVisibility::Fragment,
            },
            // LitMaterial automatically adds bindings 10-31, bindless heaps
        },
        .pushConstantSize = sizeof(MyPushConstants)
    }, {
        .cullMode = RGL::CullMode::Back,
        .opacityMode = OpacityMode::Opaque,
        .requiredAttributes = {
            .position = true,
            .normal = true,
            .tangent = true,
            .bitangent = true,
            .uv0 = true,
            .lightmapUV = false
        }
    }) {}
};
```

Create shader files:
- `my_shader.vsh` - Vertex shader
- `my_shader.fsh` - Fragment shader implementing `LitOutput frag(EnvironmentData)`
- `my_shader_vsh_shadow.vsh` / `my_shader_fsh_shadow.fsh` - Shadow pass variants
- `my_shader_vsh_prepass.vsh` / `my_shader_fsh_prepass.fsh` - Depth prepass variants

The fragment shader must include engine headers:

```glsl
#include "ravengine_shader.glsl"
#include "BRDF.glsl"
#include "cluster_shared.glsl"
#include "lit_mesh_shared.glsl"
#include "mesh_shared.glsl"
#include "enginedata.glsl"
#include "make_engine_data.glsl"

LitOutput frag(EnvironmentData envData) {
    // Sample your custom textures
    vec4 customColor = texture(sampler2D(myTexture, mySampler), inUV);
    
    return LitOutput(
        /* color */ customColor,
        /* normal */ vec3(0,0,1),
        /* emissiveColor */ vec3(0),
        /* roughness */ 0.5,
        /* specular */ 0.5,
        /* metallic */ 0.0,
        /* ao */ 1.0
    );
}
```

**Sources:** [src/Material.cpp:345-358](), [tools/rvesc/lit_mesh.fsh:1-374]()

### Custom MaterialInstance

Extend `MaterialInstance` to provide typed accessors:

```cpp
struct MyCustomMaterialInstance : public MaterialInstance {
    MyCustomMaterialInstance(Ref<MyCustomMaterial> m) 
        : MaterialInstance(m) {
        // Set default textures
        textureBindings[1] = Texture::Manager::defaultTexture;
    }
    
    void SetCustomTexture(Ref<Texture> tex) {
        textureBindings[1] = tex;
    }
    
    void SetCustomValue(float value) {
        pushData.customValue = value;
    }
    
    virtual const RGL::untyped_span GetPushConstantData() const override {
        return pushData;
    }
    
private:
    struct {
        float customValue = 1.0f;
    } pushData;
};
```

Use the material manager cache for instances:

```cpp
using MyMatInstManager = MaterialInstanceManager<MyCustomMaterialInstance>;
auto instance = MyMatInstManager::Get();
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:184-223](), [include/RavEngine/BuiltinMaterials.hpp:39-83]()

## Opacity Modes and Transparency

The `OpacityMode` enum controls rendering behavior:

| Mode | Behavior |
|------|----------|
| `Opaque` | Alpha < 0.5 discards fragments. Creates shadow and depth prepass pipelines. Main pass uses `depthFunction = Equal`. |
| `Transparent` | No alpha discard. No shadow/depth prepass. Uses Multi-Layer Alpha Blending (MLAB) via storage images. Requires fragment interlock on non-TBDR hardware. |

On tile-based deferred rendering (TBDR) platforms, transparent materials use specialized shaders with `_tbdr` suffix that write directly to tile memory attachments instead of storage images.

**Sources:** [src/Material.cpp:40-44](), [src/Material.cpp:76-77](), [src/Material.cpp:158-159](), [src/Material.cpp:266-302](), [src/BuiltinMaterials.cpp:106-158]()

## Pipeline Binding Slots

### Reserved Bindings

| Binding | Usage | Material Type |
|---------|-------|---------------|
| 0-9 | User-defined resources | All |
| 10 | Model matrices (`mat4 model[]`) | All (auto-added) |
| 11 | Engine constants (`EngineData_Internal`) | All (auto-added) |
| 12 | Ambient lights | LitMaterial |
| 13 | Directional lights | LitMaterial |
| 14 | Shadow sampler | LitMaterial |
| 15 | Point lights | LitMaterial |
| 16 | Light clusters | LitMaterial |
| 17 | Spot lights | LitMaterial |
| 23-27 | MLAB storage images | Transparent only |
| 28 | Entity render layers | LitMaterial |
| 29 | Per-object attribute flags | LitMaterial |
| 30 | Directional light varying data | LitMaterial |
| 31 | Environment sampler | LitMaterial |
| Set 1, Binding 0 | Shadow maps (bindless `texture2D[2048]`) | LitMaterial |
| Set 2, Binding 0 | Cubemaps (bindless `textureCube[2048]`) | LitMaterial |

**Sources:** [src/Material.cpp:208-343](), [tools/rvesc/lit_mesh.fsh:63-117]()

## Mesh Attribute Requirements

The `MeshAttributes` struct ([include/RavEngine/MaterialShared.hpp]()), declared in `MaterialConfig.requiredAttributes`, controls which vertex buffers are bound:

```cpp
struct MeshAttributes {
    bool position = true;
    bool normal = true;
    bool tangent = true;
    bool bitangent = true;
    bool uv0 = true;
    bool lightmapUV = false;
};
```

The material constructor ([src/Material.cpp:94-133]()) removes vertex buffer bindings for unused attributes, reducing bandwidth and memory usage. This is especially important for large meshes and skinned meshes where vertex data is duplicated for GPU skinning.

**Sources:** [src/Material.cpp:94-133](), [include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:32]()24:T4d7a,# Lighting System

## Purpose and Scope

This document covers RavEngine's lighting system, which provides dynamic real-time illumination using a **clustered forward+ rendering architecture**. The system supports multiple light types with optional shadow mapping and is designed for efficient GPU-driven rendering with minimal CPU overhead.

For information about the overall rendering pipeline, see [Rendering Architecture](#4.1). For material-light interaction (PBR shading), see [Materials and Shaders](#4.2). For post-processing effects like SSAO/SSGI, see [Post-Processing and Effects](#4.6).

---

## Light Types Overview

RavEngine provides five light types that inherit from a common base class hierarchy. All lights support **render layer filtering** to control which objects they illuminate.

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Light {
        +ColorRGBA color
        +float Intensity
        +renderlayer_t illuminationLayers
        +SetColorRGBA()
        +SetIntensity()
        +SetIlluminationLayers()
    }
    
    class ShadowLightBase {
        +bool doesCastShadow
        +renderlayer_t shadowLayers
        +SetCastsShadows()
        +SetShadowLayers()
    }
    
    class AmbientLight {
        +optional~EnvironmentLight~ environment
        +CastsShadows() false
    }
    
    class DirectionalLight {
        +ShadowMap shadowData
        +Array~float~ shadowCascades
        +uint8_t numCascades
        +float maxShadowDistanceFactor
    }
    
    class PointLight {
        +ShadowData shadowData
        +CalcProjectionMatrix()
        +CalcViewMatrix()
        -CalculateRadius()
    }
    
    class SpotLight {
        +float coneAngle
        +float penumbraAngle
        +ShadowMap shadowData
        +CalcProjectionMatrix()
        +CalcViewMatrix()
    }
    
    Light <|-- ShadowLightBase
    Light <|-- AmbientLight
    ShadowLightBase <|-- DirectionalLight
    ShadowLightBase <|-- PointLight
    ShadowLightBase <|-- SpotLight
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:1-230]()

---

## Base Light Class

The `Light` class provides common properties for all light types:

| Property | Type | Description |
|----------|------|-------------|
| `color` | `ColorRGBA` | Light color (RGB channels) |
| `Intensity` | `float` | Light intensity multiplier |
| `illuminationLayers` | `renderlayer_t` | Bitmask controlling which render layers this light affects |

All lights use an **invalidation flag** (`tickInvalidated`) to notify the World when their properties change, triggering GPU buffer updates only when necessary.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:21-63]()

---

## Shadow-Casting Lights

The `ShadowLightBase` class extends `Light` to add shadow mapping capabilities:

| Property | Type | Description |
|----------|------|-------------|
| `doesCastShadow` | `bool` | Enable/disable shadow casting |
| `shadowLayers` | `renderlayer_t` | Bitmask controlling which objects cast shadows for this light |

**Directional**, **Point**, and **Spot** lights inherit from `ShadowLightBase`, while **Ambient** lights do not cast shadows.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:69-92]()

---

## Light Type Details

### Ambient Light

`AmbientLight` provides scene-wide constant illumination. It is the only light type affected by **SSAO** (Screen Space Ambient Occlusion).

```mermaid
graph LR
    AmbientLight["AmbientLight<br/>Component"]
    EnvironmentLight["EnvironmentLight<br/>(optional)"]
    Skybox["Skybox<br/>Material"]
    CubemapTexture["CubemapTexture<br/>outputTexture"]
    IrradianceTexture["CubemapTexture<br/>irradianceTexture"]
    
    AmbientLight --> EnvironmentLight
    EnvironmentLight --> Skybox
    EnvironmentLight --> CubemapTexture
    EnvironmentLight --> IrradianceTexture
```

When an `EnvironmentLight` is provided, the ambient light's color and intensity act as **multipliers** for the environment map data. The environment map is rendered in six cubemap faces and convolved for roughness-based reflections.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:98-129](), [src/Light.cpp:176-206]()

---

### Directional Light

`DirectionalLight` emits parallel rays across the entire scene, suitable for modeling sunlight. It supports **Cascaded Shadow Maps (CSM)** for high-quality shadows at multiple distance ranges.

**Key Properties:**

| Property | Type | Description |
|----------|------|-------------|
| `shadowCascades` | `Array<float, MAX_CASCADES>` | Normalized distances for shadow cascade splits |
| `numCascades` | `uint8_t` | Number of active cascades (max 4) |
| `maxShadowDistanceFactor` | `float` | Multiplier for maximum shadow distance |

**Shadow Data Structure:**

```mermaid
graph TD
    DirectionalLight["DirectionalLight"]
    ShadowMap["ShadowMap struct"]
    Pyramids["pyramid[4]<br/>DepthPyramid"]
    Textures["shadowMap[4]<br/>RGLTexturePtr"]
    
    DirectionalLight --> ShadowMap
    ShadowMap --> Pyramids
    ShadowMap --> Textures
```

Each cascade has its own 4096Ã—4096 depth texture and depth pyramid for occlusion culling. The cascade computation uses a **frustum-fitting algorithm** that projects the camera frustum into light space for each cascade range.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:134-152](), [src/Light.cpp:89-116](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:149-294]()

---

### Point Light

`PointLight` emits light omnidirectionally from a single point, suitable for modeling light bulbs or torches. It casts shadows in all six cubemap directions.

**Key Methods:**

- `CalcProjectionMatrix()` - Returns 90Â° FOV perspective projection
- `CalcViewMatrix(lightPos, index)` - Returns view matrix for one of six cubemap faces
- `CalculateRadius()` - Computes light radius based on intensity and minimum influence threshold

**Shadow Data Structure:**

```mermaid
graph TD
    PointLight["PointLight"]
    ShadowData["ShadowData struct"]
    CubePyramids["cubePyramids[6]<br/>DepthPyramid"]
    CubeShadowmaps["cubeShadowmaps[6]<br/>RGLTexturePtr"]
    MapCube["mapCube<br/>RGLTexturePtr<br/>(cubemap)"]
    
    PointLight --> ShadowData
    ShadowData --> CubePyramids
    ShadowData --> CubeShadowmaps
    ShadowData --> MapCube
```

Each cubemap face is 1024Ã—1024. The six individual faces are copied into a single cubemap texture for efficient sampling in shaders.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:157-184](), [src/Light.cpp:126-143](), [src/Light.cpp:208-246]()

---

### Spot Light

`SpotLight` emits light in a cone, suitable for modeling flashlights or spotlights.

**Key Properties:**

| Property | Type | Description |
|----------|------|-------------|
| `coneAngle` | `float` | Full cone angle in degrees |
| `penumbraAngle` | `float` | Soft edge falloff angle |

**Shadow Data Structure:**

```mermaid
graph TD
    SpotLight["SpotLight"]
    ShadowMap["ShadowMap struct"]
    Pyramid["pyramid<br/>DepthPyramid"]
    Texture["shadowMap<br/>RGLTexturePtr"]
    
    SpotLight --> ShadowMap
    ShadowMap --> Pyramid
    ShadowMap --> Texture
```

The shadow map is a single 4096Ã—4096 depth texture. The projection matrix uses `coneAngle * 2` as the field of view. The view matrix applies a -90Â° rotation to align the light's -Y axis with the forward direction.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:189-228](), [src/Light.cpp:118-174]()

---

## Shadow Mapping System

### Cascaded Shadow Maps (Directional Lights)

Directional lights use **Cascaded Shadow Maps (CSM)** to provide high-resolution shadows near the camera and lower-resolution shadows at a distance.

```mermaid
graph TD
    Camera["Camera Frustum"]
    Split0["Cascade 0<br/>Near Range"]
    Split1["Cascade 1<br/>Mid Range"]
    Split2["Cascade 2<br/>Far Range"]
    Split3["Cascade 3<br/>Distant Range"]
    
    Fit0["Fit Frustum Segment<br/>to Light View"]
    Fit1["Fit Frustum Segment<br/>to Light View"]
    Fit2["Fit Frustum Segment<br/>to Light View"]
    Fit3["Fit Frustum Segment<br/>to Light View"]
    
    ShadowMap0["4096Ã—4096<br/>Shadow Texture 0"]
    ShadowMap1["4096Ã—4096<br/>Shadow Texture 1"]
    ShadowMap2["4096Ã—4096<br/>Shadow Texture 2"]
    ShadowMap3["4096Ã—4096<br/>Shadow Texture 3"]
    
    Camera --> Split0
    Camera --> Split1
    Camera --> Split2
    Camera --> Split3
    
    Split0 --> Fit0
    Split1 --> Fit1
    Split2 --> Fit2
    Split3 --> Fit3
    
    Fit0 --> ShadowMap0
    Fit1 --> ShadowMap1
    Fit2 --> ShadowMap2
    Fit3 --> ShadowMap3
```

**Cascade Computation Algorithm** (per camera, per light, per cascade):

1. **Determine near/far planes** - Interpolate between camera near/far using `shadowCascades` array values
2. **Extract frustum corners** - Compute 8 corners of the frustum segment in world space
3. **Center on frustum** - Calculate centroid of the 8 corners
4. **Compute light view matrix** - `lookAt(center + lightDir, center, up)`
5. **Compute light projection** - Fit orthographic projection to transformed frustum corners
6. **Store matrices** - Upload to `DirLightUploadDataPassVarying` for GPU use

The cascade distances are stored in the `DirectionalLight::shadowCascades` array as normalized values [0,1] and must be sorted in ascending order.

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:149-294]()

---

### Point Light Cubemap Shadows

Point lights render six shadow maps, one for each cubemap face (+X, -X, +Y, -Y, +Z, -Z). The view matrices are pre-computed using standard cubemap face orientations.

**Pre-computed View Matrices:**

The view matrices for each face are stored in `pointLightViewMats` array in [src/Light.cpp:21-42](). Each face uses a 90Â° FOV perspective projection.

During rendering, these static matrices are translated to the light's world position using `glm::translate(pointLightViewMats[index], -lightPos)`.

**Sources:** [src/Light.cpp:21-143](), [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:166-171]()

---

### Spot Light Shadows

Spot lights use a single shadow map with a perspective projection. The cone angle determines the field of view (FOV = `coneAngle * 2`).

The view matrix is computed by:
1. Creating a -90Â° rotation around X axis (to align -Y as forward)
2. Combining with the light's world transform
3. Inverting the result

**Sources:** [src/Light.cpp:145-155](), [src/Light.cpp:157-174]()

---

## Clustered Forward+ Rendering

RavEngine uses **clustered forward+ rendering** to efficiently handle many lights. The view frustum is subdivided into a 3D grid of clusters, and lights are assigned to clusters based on their bounding volumes.

### Cluster Grid Configuration

```mermaid
graph LR
    Frustum["Camera Frustum"]
    Grid["3D Cluster Grid<br/>12Ã—12Ã—24<br/>=3456 clusters"]
    ClusterData["Cluster Buffer<br/>Per-cluster light lists"]
    
    Frustum --> Grid
    Grid --> ClusterData
```

**Grid Dimensions:**

| Axis | Size | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| X | 12 | Horizontal subdivisions |
| Y | 12 | Vertical subdivisions |
| Z | 24 | Depth subdivisions (exponential distribution) |

Total clusters: **3,456**

Each cluster stores:
- Min/max 3D points (AABB)
- Point light count and indices (max `CLUSTER_MAX_POINTS`)
- Spot light count and indices (max `CLUSTER_MAX_SPOTS`)

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:47-61](), [src/RenderEngine.cpp:922-971]()

---

### Cluster Building Pipeline

```mermaid
graph TD
    BuildGrid["Compute:<br/>cluster_build_grid_csh<br/>Build cluster AABBs"]
    SyncLightData["Sync Light Buffers<br/>Point/Spot Light Data"]
    AssignLights["Compute:<br/>cluster_assign_lights_csh<br/>Assign lights to clusters"]
    ClusterBuffer["lightClusterBuffer<br/>GPU Storage"]
    
    BuildGrid --> ClusterBuffer
    SyncLightData --> AssignLights
    ClusterBuffer --> AssignLights
    AssignLights --> ClusterBuffer
```

**Build Grid Shader (`cluster_build_grid_csh`):**

Computes the 3D AABB for each cluster in view space using the camera's projection matrix. The Z subdivision uses exponential distribution for better depth precision.

**Input UBO:**
```cpp
struct GridBuildUBO {
    glm::mat4 invProj;
    glm::uvec3 gridSize;      // (12, 12, 24)
    float zNear;
    glm::uvec2 screenDim;
    float zFar;
};
```

**Assign Lights Shader (`cluster_assign_lights_csh`):**

For each cluster, tests all point and spot lights against the cluster's AABB. Stores light indices in the cluster buffer for later fragment shader access.

**Input UBO:**
```cpp
struct GridAssignUBO {
    glm::mat4 viewMat;
    uint32_t pointLightCount;
    uint32_t spotLightCount;
};
```

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine.cpp:922-971](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:104-117]()

---

## Render Data Synchronization

Light data is synchronized from CPU components to GPU buffers using `BufferedVRAMSparseSet`, which provides efficient double-buffered updates with dirty flag tracking.

```mermaid
graph LR
    DirLightComp["DirectionalLight<br/>Component"]
    PointLightComp["PointLight<br/>Component"]
    SpotLightComp["SpotLight<br/>Component"]
    AmbientLightComp["AmbientLight<br/>Component"]
    
    DirUpload["DirLightUploadData<br/>BufferedVRAMSparseSet"]
    PointUpload["PointLightUploadData<br/>BufferedVRAMSparseSet"]
    SpotUpload["SpotLightDataUpload<br/>BufferedVRAMSparseSet"]
    AmbientUpload["AmbientLightUploadData<br/>BufferedVRAMSparseSet"]
    
    GPU["GPU Private Buffers"]
    
    DirLightComp --> DirUpload
    PointLightComp --> PointUpload
    SpotLightComp --> SpotUpload
    AmbientLightComp --> AmbientUpload
    
    DirUpload --> GPU
    PointUpload --> GPU
    SpotUpload --> GPU
    AmbientUpload --> GPU
```

### GPU Data Structures

**Directional Light:**
```cpp
struct DirLightUploadData {
    glm::vec3 color;
    glm::vec3 direction;
    float intensity;
    int castsShadows;
    int shadowmapBindlessIndex[MAX_CASCADES];
    float cascadeDistances[MAX_CASCADES];
    renderlayer_t shadowLayers;
    renderlayer_t illuminationLayers;
    uint32_t numCascades;
};
```

**Point Light:**
```cpp
struct PointLightUploadData {
    glm::mat4 viewMats[6];
    glm::mat4 projMat;
    glm::vec3 position;
    glm::vec3 color;
    float intensity;
    int castsShadows;
    renderlayer_t shadowLayers;
    renderlayer_t illuminationLayers;
    int shadowmapBindlessIndices[6];
};
```

**Spot Light:**
```cpp
struct SpotLightDataUpload {
    glm::mat4 lightViewProj;
    glm::mat4 worldTransform;
    glm::vec3 color;
    float intensity;
    float coneAngle;
    float penumbraAngle;
    int castsShadows;
    uint32_t shadowmapBindlessIndex;
    renderlayer_t shadowLayers;
    renderlayer_t illuminationLayers;
};
```

**Ambient Light:**
```cpp
struct AmbientLightUploadData {
    glm::vec3 color;
    float intensity;
    renderlayer_t illuminationLayers;
    uint32_t skyboxBindlessIndex;
    uint32_t skyboxIrradianceBindlessIndex;
};
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:364-416](), [src/World.cpp:392-520]()

---

### Update Pipeline

Light data updates occur in the `World::setupRenderTasks` task graph:

```mermaid
graph TD
    UpdateDirLights["updateInvalidatedDirs<br/>Task"]
    UpdateSpotLights["updateInvalidatedSpots<br/>Task"]
    UpdatePointLights["updateInvalidatedPoints<br/>Task"]
    UpdateAmbientLights["updateInvalidatedAmbients<br/>Task"]
    
    TransformCheck{{"Transform Dirty?"}}
    LightCheck{{"Light Invalidated?"}}
    
    WriteTransform["Write worldTransform/<br/>direction to GPU buffer"]
    WriteLight["Write color/intensity/<br/>shadow data to GPU buffer"]
    
    ClearFlag["clearInvalidate()"]
    
    UpdateDirLights --> TransformCheck
    TransformCheck -->|Yes| WriteTransform
    UpdateDirLights --> LightCheck
    LightCheck -->|Yes| WriteLight
    WriteLight --> ClearFlag
    
    UpdateSpotLights --> TransformCheck
    UpdatePointLights --> TransformCheck
    UpdateAmbientLights --> LightCheck
```

Each light component sets its `tickInvalidated` flag when properties change. During the render task phase, only invalidated lights update their GPU buffers.

**Sources:** [src/World.cpp:392-520]()

---

## Layer System

RavEngine's lighting system uses **render layers** to control light-object interactions at a fine granularity.

### Layer Types

| Layer Type | Property | Description |
|------------|----------|-------------|
| **Illumination Layers** | `illuminationLayers` | Bitmask of objects this light affects |
| **Shadow Layers** | `shadowLayers` | Bitmask of objects that cast shadows for this light |
| **Camera Render Layers** | `cameraRenderLayers` | Bitmask of objects visible to camera |

### Layer Filtering Logic

During GPU culling, the shader performs layer tests:

```glsl
// From defaultcull.csh
const uint cameraRenderLayers = ubo.cameraRenderLayers;
const uint entityLayerMask = renderLayerBuffer[entityID];
if ((cameraRenderLayers & entityLayerMask) == 0){
    return;  // Not visible to this camera
}
```

Shadow passes use `shadowLayers` to filter which objects are rendered into shadow maps. The main lighting pass uses `illuminationLayers` to determine which lights contribute to each fragment.

**Sources:** [shaders/defaultcull.csh:173-178](), [include/RavEngine/Layer.hpp]()

---

## GPU Light Culling

The lighting system integrates with GPU-driven culling to minimize draw calls and maximize rendering efficiency.

### Shadow Pass Culling

```mermaid
graph TD
    ShadowPass["Shadow Pass"]
    CullingShader["defaultcull_csh<br/>Compute Shader"]
    
    CuboData["CUBO Structures<br/>(per material)"]
    ModelMatrices["modelBuffer[]<br/>World transforms"]
    ShadowLayers["shadowLayers<br/>Light property"]
    RenderLayers["renderLayerBuffer[]<br/>Per-entity masks"]
    
    FrustumCull{{"Frustum<br/>Culling"}}
    LayerTest{{"Shadow Layer<br/>Test"}}
    CastsShadows{{"Casts<br/>Shadows?"}}
    
    IndirectBuffer["Indirect Draw Buffer<br/>(atomically incremented)"]
    
    ShadowPass --> CullingShader
    CuboData --> CullingShader
    ModelMatrices --> CullingShader
    ShadowLayers --> CullingShader
    RenderLayers --> CullingShader
    
    CullingShader --> FrustumCull
    FrustumCull -->|Visible| LayerTest
    LayerTest -->|Match| CastsShadows
    CastsShadows -->|Yes| IndirectBuffer
```

The culling shader uses the `isSingleInstanceModeAndShadowMode` flag to distinguish shadow passes from main passes. Shadow passes only consider objects with the `castsShadows` attribute bit set.

**Relevant Code:**
- [shaders/defaultcull.csh:186-193]() - Shadow mode detection
- [shaders/defaultcull.csh:180-183]() - Per-object attribute checking

**Sources:** [shaders/defaultcull.csh:1-314]()

---

## Integration with Material System

Lights interact with materials through the PBR shading model. Fragment shaders access light data via:

1. **Clustered Light Indices** - Fragment determines its cluster ID and reads light indices from `lightClusterBuffer`
2. **Light Data Buffers** - Bindless access to `DirLightUploadData`, `PointLightUploadData`, `SpotLightUploadData`, `AmbientLightUploadData`
3. **Shadow Maps** - Bindless texture access to shadow map arrays

For details on shader bindings and PBR calculations, see [Materials and Shaders](#4.2).

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:47-61](), [src/RenderEngine.cpp:839-845]()25:T6a53,# Particle Systems

## Purpose and Scope

This document covers RavEngine's GPU-driven particle system architecture, including the `ParticleEmitter` component, particle material system (update and render materials), compute-based lifecycle management, and billboard vs mesh particle rendering modes. For general rendering architecture, see [Rendering Architecture](#4.1). For material system concepts like lighting modes and opacity, see [Materials and Shaders](#4.2).

## Architecture Overview

RavEngine's particle system is fully GPU-driven, executing particle creation, updates, and rendering entirely on the GPU using compute shaders and indirect rendering. The `ParticleEmitter` component manages GPU buffers that store particle data, while materials define both update logic (compute shaders) and rendering behavior (graphics pipelines).

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Component Layer"
        PE["ParticleEmitter<br/>(ComponentWithOwner)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Material System"
        PUM["ParticleUpdateMaterial<br/>Init + Update Shaders"]
        PUMI["ParticleUpdateMaterialInstance"]
        
        PRM["ParticleRenderMaterial<br/>Graphics Pipelines"]
        BRPM["BillboardRenderParticleMaterial&lt;mode&gt;"]
        MRPM["MeshParticleRenderMaterial&lt;mode&gt;"]
        
        BPRMI["BillboardParticleRenderMaterialInstance"]
        MPRMI["MeshParticleRenderMaterialInstance"]
        
        MPMSM["MeshParticleMeshSelectionMaterial<br/>Custom Selection Logic"]
    end
    
    subgraph "GPU Buffers (ParticleEmitter)"
        PDB["particleDataBuffer<br/>Custom particle struct"]
        PRF["particleReuseFreelist<br/>uint32_t indices"]
        STFL["spawnedThisFrameList<br/>uint32_t indices"]
        APIB["activeParticleIndexBuffer<br/>uint32_t indices"]
        ICB["indirectComputeBuffer<br/>ComputeIndirectCommand"]
        IDB["indirectDrawBuffer<br/>IndirectCommand"]
        ESB["emitterStateBuffer<br/>EmitterState"]
        PLB["particleLifeBuffer<br/>float lifetimes"]
    end
    
    subgraph "GPU Execution (RenderEngine)"
        CreateShader["create_particle.csh<br/>Spawn particles"]
        InitShader["User Init Shader<br/>Initialize new particles"]
        UpdateShader["User Update Shader<br/>Update alive particles"]
        KillShader["kill_particle.csh<br/>Recycle dead particles"]
        RenderPipeline["Render Pipeline<br/>Billboard or Mesh"]
    end
    
    PE --> PUM

    PE --> BPRMI
    PE --> MPRMI

    PRM --> BRPM
    PRM --> MRPM
    BRPM --> BPRMI
    MRPM --> MPRMI

    PE --> STFL
    PE --> APIB
    PE --> ICB
    PE --> IDB
    PE --> ESB
    PE --> PLB
    
    CreateShader --> PRF
    CreateShader --> APIB
    CreateShader --> STFL
    CreateShader --> ESB
    
    InitShader --> PDB
    InitShader --> STFL
    
    UpdateShader --> PDB
    UpdateShader --> APIB
    UpdateShader --> PLB
    
    KillShader --> PRF
    KillShader --> APIB
```

## ParticleEmitter Component

The `ParticleEmitter` component ([include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:31-139]()) is the primary interface for creating and controlling particle systems. It is a `ComponentWithOwner` attached to an entity in the ECS.

### Construction and Configuration

```mermaid
graph LR
    Constructor["ParticleEmitter(...)<br/>Creates GPU buffers"]
    
    subgraph "Constructor Parameters"
        Owner["Entity owner"]
        MaxP["uint32_t maxParticles<br/>Buffer capacity"]
        Size["uint16_t sizeOfEachParticle<br/>Bytes per particle"]
        UpdateMat["ParticleUpdateMaterialInstance<br/>Update logic"]
        RenderMat["ParticleRenderMaterialVariant<br/>Billboard or Mesh"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Created Resources"
        B1["particleDataBuffer<br/>maxParticles * sizeOfEachParticle"]
        B2["particleReuseFreelist<br/>maxParticles * sizeof(uint32_t)"]
        B3["spawnedThisFrameList<br/>maxParticles * sizeof(uint32_t)"]
        B4["activeParticleIndexBuffer<br/>maxParticles * sizeof(uint32_t)"]
        B5["indirectComputeBuffer<br/>2 * ComputeIndirectCommand"]
        B6["indirectDrawBuffer<br/>1 * IndirectCommand"]
        B7["emitterStateBuffer<br/>1 * EmitterState"]
        B8["particleLifeBuffer<br/>maxParticles * sizeof(float)"]
    end
    
    Owner --> Constructor
    MaxP --> Constructor
    Size --> Constructor
    UpdateMat --> Constructor
    RenderMat --> Constructor
    
    Constructor --> B1
    Constructor --> B2
    Constructor --> B3
    Constructor --> B4
    Constructor --> B5
    Constructor --> B6
    Constructor --> B7
    Constructor --> B8
```

The constructor ([src/ParticleEmitter.cpp:11-57]()) allocates GPU buffers with `RGL::BufferAccess::Private` (device-local) for maximum performance. The `sizeOfEachParticle` parameter defines the size of the custom particle structure used by the application.

**Sources:** [src/ParticleEmitter.cpp:11-57](), [include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:38]()

### Emission Modes and Control

| Mode | Behavior | Use Case |
|------|----------|----------|
| `Mode::Stream` | Continuous emission at `spawnRate` particles/second | Fire, smoke, rain effects |
| `Mode::Burst` | One-time emission of `spawnRate` particles | Explosions, impacts, one-shot effects |

**Control Methods:**

- `Play()` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:56]()): Starts emission
- `Stop()` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:61]()): Stops stream mode emission
- `Reset()` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:66-68]()): Kills all particles and resets state
- `SetEmissionRate(uint32_t rate)` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:78]()): Sets particles per second (Stream) or particles per burst (Burst)

In Stream mode, `GetNextParticleSpawnCount()` ([src/ParticleEmitter.cpp:79-96]()) calculates particles to spawn based on elapsed time and `spawnRate`.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:33-78](), [src/ParticleEmitter.cpp:66-96]()

### Visibility and Freezing

- `SetVisibility(bool visible)` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:91-94]()): Controls rendering and automatically freezes when invisible
- `SetFrozen(bool frozen)` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:87-89]()): Prevents particle updates without destroying them

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:85-102]()

### EmitterState Structure

The `EmitterState` buffer ([include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:20-23]()) tracks emitter state on the GPU:

| Field | Type | Purpose |
|-------|------|---------|
| `aliveParticleCount` | `uint32_t` | Number of currently alive particles |
| `freeListCount` | `uint32_t` | Number of indices in the reuse freelist |
| `particlesCreatedThisFrame` | `uint32_t` | Particles spawned this frame |
| `emitterOwnerID` | `entity_t` | Owner entity ID |

This structure is accessed atomically by compute shaders to manage particle lifecycle.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/ParticleEmitter.hpp:14-26]()

## Material System

The particle material system is split into two independent parts: **update materials** (compute-based simulation) and **render materials** (graphics pipeline-based rendering).

### Update Materials

`ParticleUpdateMaterial` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:38-54]()) defines two compute shaders:

1. **Init Shader**: Runs once per newly created particle to initialize custom data
2. **Update Shader**: Runs every frame for each alive particle to update simulation state

```mermaid
graph TB
    PUM["ParticleUpdateMaterial"]
    
    subgraph "Shader Pipelines"
        InitPipe["userInitPipeline<br/>RGLComputePipelinePtr"]
        UpdatePipe["userUpdatePipeline<br/>RGLComputePipelinePtr"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Init Shader Bindings (binding #)"
        I0["0: particleReuseFreelist (read)"]
        I1["1: spawnedThisFrameList (read)"]
        I2["2: particleDataBuffer (write)"]
        I3["3: particleLifeBuffer (write)"]
        I4["4: emitterStateBuffer (read)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Update Shader Bindings (binding #)"
        U0["0: particleDataBuffer (read/write)"]
        U1["1: activeParticleIndexBuffer (read/write)"]
        U2["2: particleLifeBuffer (read/write)"]
        U3["3: indirectDrawBuffer (read/write)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Push Constants"
        PC["ParticleUpdateUBO<br/>float fpsScale"]
    end
    
    PUM --> InitPipe
    PUM --> UpdatePipe
    
    InitPipe -.-> I0
    InitPipe -.-> I1
    InitPipe -.-> I2
    InitPipe -.-> I3
    InitPipe -.-> I4
    
    UpdatePipe -.-> U0
    UpdatePipe -.-> U1
    UpdatePipe -.-> U2
    UpdatePipe -.-> U3
    UpdatePipe -.-> PC
```

**Pipeline Creation:**

Init pipeline ([src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:158-200]()):
- Bindings 0-4 provide access to particle buffers
- No push constants

Update pipeline ([src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:203-245]()):
- Bindings 0-3 provide read/write access to simulation data
- Push constant `ParticleUpdateUBO` provides `fpsScale` for frame-rate independent updates

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:38-54](), [src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:153-245]()

### Render Materials

`ParticleRenderMaterial` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:69-106]()) is the base class for all particle render materials. It creates three render pipelines:

| Pipeline | Purpose | Depth Function |
|----------|---------|----------------|
| `userRenderPipeline` | Main rendering pass | `Equal` (opaque) or `Greater` (transparent) |
| `prepassRenderPipeline` | Depth prepass (opaque only) | `Greater` |
| `shadowRenderPipeline` | Shadow map rendering (opaque only) | `Greater` |

**Common Bindings (All Render Materials):**

| Binding | Type | Purpose |
|---------|------|---------|
| `MODEL_MATRIX_BINDING` | StorageBuffer | Transform matrices |
| `particleDataBufferBinding` (18) | StorageBuffer | Custom particle data |
| `particleAliveIndexBufferBinding` (19) | StorageBuffer | Alive particle indices |
| `particleMatrixBufferBinding` (20) | StorageBuffer | Per-particle matrices |
| `particleEmitterStateBufferBinding` (22) | StorageBuffer | Emitter state |

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:69-106](), [src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:28-151]()

#### Billboard Render Materials

`BillboardRenderParticleMaterial<LightingMode>` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:114-121]()) renders particles as camera-facing quads using `RGL::PrimitiveTopology::TriangleStrip` with `quadVertexConfig` ([src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:10-25]()).

**Vertex Configuration:**

```
ParticleQuadVert {
    vector2 pos;  // location 0, 2D quad coordinates
}
```

The vertex shader expands each particle into a billboarded quad. User bindings are augmented with lighting-specific bindings via `augmentBillboardConfig()` ([src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:440-452]()).

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:108-121](), [src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:10-25,440-452]()

#### Mesh Render Materials

`MeshParticleRenderMaterial<LightingMode>` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:129-136]()) renders particles as instanced 3D meshes using `RGL::PrimitiveTopology::TriangleList` with `defaultVertexConfig`.

**Additional Binding (Mesh Particles):**

| Binding | Type | Purpose |
|---------|------|---------|
| 21 (`kEngineDataBinding`) | StorageBuffer | Mesh geometry data |

User bindings are augmented via `augmentMeshConfig()` ([src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:421-439]()) which adds the mesh data binding and lighting-specific bindings.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:123-136](), [src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:421-439]()

#### Mesh Selection Materials

`MeshParticleMeshSelectionMaterial` ([include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:139-144]()) allows custom compute shaders to select which mesh each particle renders with. This is useful for randomized mesh selection or state-based mesh changes.

**Bindings (Selection Compute Shader):**

| Binding | Type | Purpose |
|---------|------|---------|
| 10 | StorageBuffer (write) | Output mesh indices |
| 11 | StorageBuffer (write) | Additional output data |
| 12 | StorageBuffer (read) | Particle data |
| 13 | StorageBuffer (read) | Alive particle indices |
| 14 | StorageBuffer (read) | Shadow sampler data |
| 31 | StorageBuffer (read) | Environment sampler data |
| 15 | StorageBuffer (read) | Additional input data |

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:139-144](), [src/ParticleMaterial.cpp:332-390]()

### Material Instances

Material instances ([include/RavEngine/ParticleMaterial.hpp:154-209]()) provide per-emitter configuration and texture bindings.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Update Instance"
        PUMI["ParticleUpdateMaterialInstance"]
        UMat["Ref&lt;ParticleUpdateMaterial&gt; mat"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Render Instance Base"
        PRMI["ParticleRenderMaterialInstance"]
        Tex["textureBindings[16]<br/>Ref&lt;Texture&gt;"]
        Samp["samplerBindings[16]<br/>std::bitset"]
        PushConst["SetPushConstantData()<br/>Virtual method"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Billboard Instance"
        BPRMI["BillboardParticleRenderMaterialInstance"]
        BMat["MaterialVariant<br/>Lit or Unlit"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Mesh Instance"
        MPRMI["MeshParticleRenderMaterialInstance"]
        MMat["MaterialVariant<br/>Lit or Unlit"]
        Meshes["Ref&lt;MeshCollectionStatic&gt; meshes"]
        SelFunc["Ref&lt;MeshParticleMeshSelectionMaterialInstance&gt;<br/>Optional custom selection"]
    end
    
    PRMI --> Tex
    PRMI --> Samp
    PRMI --> PushConst
    
    PRMI --> BPRMI
    PRMI --> MPRMI
    
    BPRMI --> BMat
    MPRMI --> MMat
    MPRMI --> Meshes
```
