## Purpose and Scope

This page documents RavEngine's spatial audio system through **Audio Spaces**, which define regions where 3D audio processing occurs. Audio Spaces spatialize point sources using external audio libraries (Steam Audio and Resonance Audio) to provide binaural HRTF, occlusion, transmission, and reverberation effects.

For information about audio sources and playback control, see [Audio Sources and Playback](#7.1). For the multi-threaded architecture and snapshot system, see [Audio System Architecture](#7.3).

---

## Audio Space Overview

Audio Spaces are component-based regions that process `AudioSourceComponent`s into spatialized audio output. The engine provides three types of spaces with increasing complexity:

| Space Type | Library | Primary Use Case | Features |
|------------|---------|------------------|----------|
| `SimpleAudioSpace` | Steam Audio | Lightweight HRTF | Binaural spatialization, distance attenuation |
| `GeometryAudioSpace` | Steam Audio | Advanced simulation | Mesh occlusion, transmission, pathing |
| `BoxReverbationAudioSpace` | Resonance Audio | Room acoustics | Box-shaped room reverb, wall materials |

Audio sources are **only processed if they fall within an Audio Space's activation radius**. Sources outside all spaces are not spatialized. `AmbientAudioSourceComponent`s are unaffected by spaces and always render as omnipresent audio.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/AudioSpace.hpp:38-312](), [include/RavEngine/AudioSnapshot.hpp:26-54]()

---

## Audio Space Architecture

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Components"
        SimpleSpace["SimpleAudioSpace<br/>ComponentWithOwner"]
        GeomSpace["GeometryAudioSpace<br/>ComponentWithOwner"]
        BoxSpace["BoxReverbationAudioSpace<br/>ComponentWithOwner"]
        AudioSrc["AudioSourceComponent<br/>Point source"]
    end
    
    subgraph "RoomData Structures"
        SimpleData["SimpleAudioSpace::RoomData<br/>- sourceRadius<br/>- workingBuffers<br/>- accumulationBuffer<br/>- steamAudioData map"]
        GeomData["GeometryAudioSpace::RoomData<br/>- sourceRadius, meshRadius<br/>- steamAudioSimulator<br/>- rootScene<br/>- steamAudioSourceData map<br/>- steamAudioMeshData map"]
        BoxData["BoxReverbationAudioSpace::RoomData<br/>- audioEngine (Resonance)<br/>- sourceMap<br/>- wallMaterials[6]"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Snapshot Data"
        SimpleSnapshot["SimpleAudioSpaceData<br/>- room (Ref RoomData)<br/>- worldpos<br/>- sourceRadius"]
        GeomSnapshot["GeometryAudioSpaceData<br/>- room (Ref RoomData)<br/>- worldpos, invRoomTransform<br/>- sourceRadius, meshRadius"]
        BoxSnapshot["BoxReverbationSpaceData<br/>- room (Ref RoomData)<br/>- invRoomTransform<br/>- roomHalfExts<br/>- roomProperties"]
    end
    
    subgraph "External Libraries"
        SteamAudio["Steam Audio<br/>IPL* functions<br/>HRTF, occlusion, pathing"]
        ResonanceAudio["Resonance Audio<br/>vraudio API<br/>Room reverb"]
    end
    
    SimpleSpace --> SimpleData
    GeomSpace --> GeomData
    BoxSpace --> BoxData
    
    SimpleData --> SimpleSnapshot
    GeomData --> GeomSnapshot
    BoxData --> BoxSnapshot
    
    SimpleSnapshot --> SteamAudio
    GeomSnapshot --> SteamAudio
    BoxSnapshot --> ResonanceAudio
    
    AudioSrc -.->|"processed by<br/>(if in radius)"| SimpleSnapshot
    AudioSrc -.->|"processed by<br/>(if in radius)"| GeomSnapshot
    AudioSrc -.->|"processed by<br/>(if in radius)"| BoxSnapshot
```

Each Audio Space component holds a `Ref<RoomData>` which contains the library-specific state. During audio rendering, these are captured into snapshot structures (`SimpleAudioSpaceData`, `GeometryAudioSpaceData`, `BoxReverbationSpaceData`) that are processed by the audio thread.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/AudioSpace.hpp:38-312](), [include/RavEngine/AudioSnapshot.hpp:26-54]()

---

## SimpleAudioSpace

`SimpleAudioSpace` provides lightweight binaural HRTF spatialization using Steam Audio's binaural and direct effects. It is the most performant option for basic 3D audio.

### Configuration

```cpp
class SimpleAudioSpace : public ComponentWithOwner, public Queryable<SimpleAudioSpace> {
public:
    SimpleAudioSpace(Entity owner);
    
    void SetRadius(float radius);  // sourceRadius - activation distance
    float GetRadius() const;
};
```

**Radius Check:** Sources within `sourceRadius` units (Euclidean distance) from the space's world position are processed. This check occurs in [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:181-183]().

### Processing Pipeline

```mermaid
graph LR
    SourceCheck["Check source in radius<br/>distanceÂ² < sourceRadiusÂ²"]
    FillBuffer["Source fills mono buffer<br/>ProvideBufferData()"]
    Binaural["Steam Audio Binaural Effect<br/>iplBinauralEffectApply()<br/>Mono â†’ Stereo HRTF"]
    DirectEffect["Steam Audio Direct Effect<br/>iplDirectEffectApply()<br/>Distance attenuation"]
    EffectGraph["AudioGraphComposed::Render()<br/>User effect chain"]
    Accumulate["Additive blend into<br/>accumulationBuffer"]
    
    SourceCheck -->|"in range"| FillBuffer
    FillBuffer --> Binaural
    Binaural --> DirectEffect
    DirectEffect --> EffectGraph
    EffectGraph --> Accumulate
```

The processing occurs in `CalculateSimpleAudioSpace()` [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:166-210]():

1. **Listener Check:** Verify listener is within `sourceRadius` of space [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:181-183]()
2. **Per-Source Processing:**
   - Check source within `sourceRadius` [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:192-194]()
   - Call `RenderAudioSource()` which applies:
     - **Binaural Effect:** Spatializes mono input to stereo using HRTF based on source direction [src/AudioSpace.cpp:82]()
     - **Direct Effect:** Applies distance attenuation [src/AudioSpace.cpp:93]()
   - Accumulate result into `accumulationBuffer` [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:207]()

### Steam Audio Effects Storage

Each source requires per-entity Steam Audio state stored in `RoomData::steamAudioData`:

```cpp
struct SteamAudioEffects {
    _IPLBinauralEffect_t* binauralEffect;
    _IPLDirectEffect_t* directEffect;
};

locked_hashmap<entity_id_t, SteamAudioEffects, SpinLock> steamAudioData;
```

Effects are lazily created on first render [src/AudioSpace.cpp:29-46]() and destroyed when sources are removed [src/AudioSpace.cpp:99-105]().

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/AudioSpace.hpp:38-109](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:166-210](), [src/AudioSpace.cpp:21-131]()

---

## GeometryAudioSpace

`GeometryAudioSpace` provides advanced spatial audio simulation with mesh occlusion, transmission, and pathing using Steam Audio's full simulation pipeline. This is the most feature-rich but computationally expensive option.

### Configuration

```cpp
class GeometryAudioSpace : public ComponentWithOwner, public Queryable<GeometryAudioSpace> {
public:
    GeometryAudioSpace(Entity owner);
    
    void SetAudioSourceRadius(float radius);  // Sources considered in simulation
    void SetMeshRadius(float radius);         // Mesh occluders considered
    
    float GetAudioSourceRadius() const;
    float GetMeshRadius() const;
};
```

The space maintains two independent radii:
- **sourceRadius:** Sources within this distance are simulated
- **meshRadius:** Static mesh occluders within this distance are included

### Steam Audio Simulator Architecture

```mermaid
graph TB
    RoomData["GeometryAudioSpace::RoomData"]
    
    Simulator["IPLSimulator<br/>steamAudioSimulator<br/>Simulation engine"]
    Scene["IPLScene<br/>rootScene<br/>Geometry container"]
    
    subgraph "Per-Source State"
        Source["IPLSource<br/>Added to simulator"]
        DirectEff["IPLDirectEffect<br/>Occlusion/transmission"]
        PathEff["IPLPathEffect<br/>Pathing (future)"]
        BinauralEff["IPLBinauralEffect<br/>HRTF spatialization"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Per-Mesh State"
        InstancedMesh["IPLInstancedMesh<br/>Occluder geometry"]
    end
    
    RoomData --> Simulator
    RoomData --> Scene
    
    Simulator -->|"sources registered"| Source
    Scene -->|"meshes registered"| InstancedMesh
    
    Source --> DirectEff
    Source --> PathEff
    Source --> BinauralEff
```

The simulator is created in [src/AudioSpace.cpp:133-164]() with settings for occlusion, transmission, and pathing.

### Processing Pipeline

```mermaid
graph TD
    ListenerCheck["Check listener in meshRadius<br/>distanceÂ² < meshRadiusÂ²"]
    
    subgraph "Consideration Phase"
        ConsiderSources["For each source:<br/>ConsiderAudioSource()<br/>Add/update/remove from simulator"]
        ConsiderMeshes["For each mesh:<br/>ConsiderMesh()<br/>Add/update/remove occluders"]
    end
    
    CalcRoom["CalculateRoom()<br/>iplSimulatorCommit()<br/>iplSimulatorRunDirect()"]
    
    subgraph "Render Phase"
        RenderSource["For each source:<br/>RenderAudioSource()"]
        GetOutputs["iplSourceGetOutputs()<br/>Get simulation results"]
        ApplyBinaural["iplBinauralEffectApply()<br/>Spatialize to stereo"]
        ApplyDirect["iplDirectEffectApply()<br/>Apply occlusion/transmission"]
        Accumulate["Additive blend into<br/>accumulationBuffer"]
    end
    
    ListenerCheck -->|"in range"| ConsiderSources
    ListenerCheck -->|"in range"| ConsiderMeshes
    ConsiderSources --> CalcRoom
    ConsiderMeshes --> CalcRoom
    CalcRoom --> RenderSource
    RenderSource --> GetOutputs
    GetOutputs --> ApplyBinaural
    ApplyBinaural --> ApplyDirect
    ApplyDirect --> Accumulate
```

The full process occurs in `CalculateGeometryAudioSpace()` [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:105-163]():

1. **Delete Destroyed Entities:** Clean up Steam Audio state for removed sources/meshes [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:110-117]()
2. **Listener Position Check:** Verify listener within `meshRadius` [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:124-126]()
3. **Consider Meshes:** Add/update/remove mesh occluders based on `meshRadius` [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:129-131]()
4. **Consider Sources:** Add/update/remove sources based on `sourceRadius` [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:133-136]()
5. **Calculate Room:** Run simulation [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:148]()
6. **Render Sources:** Apply effects and accumulate [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:156-162]()

### Source Management

`ConsiderAudioSource()` [src/AudioSpace.cpp:183-289]() manages Steam Audio source lifecycle:

```cpp
void ConsiderAudioSource(const vector3& sourcePos, entity_t owningEntity, 
                        const vector3& roomPos, const matrix4& invRoomTransform)
{
    bool inRange = glm::distance2(sourcePos, roomPos) <= sourceRadius * sourceRadius;
    
    auto it = steamAudioSourceData.find(owningEntity.id);
    if (it == steamAudioSourceData.end()) {
        if (!inRange) return;  // Not in range, wasn't before - skip
        
        // Create new source
        iplSourceCreate(steamAudioSimulator, &sourceSettings, &sourceData.source);
        iplSourceAdd(sourceData.source, steamAudioSimulator);
        // Create effects...
        steamAudioSourceData.emplace(owningEntity.id, sourceData);
    }
    else {
        if (!inRange) {
            // Was in range, no longer - destroy
            iplSourceRemove(sourceData.source, steamAudioSimulator);
            DestroySteamAudioSourceConfig(sourceData);
            steamAudioSourceData.erase(owningEntity.id);
            return;
        }
    }
    
    // Update source position in room space
    iplSourceSetInputs(sourceData.source, flags, &inputs);
}
```

### Mesh Occluder Management

`ConsiderMesh()` [src/AudioSpace.cpp:323-376]() manages occluder geometry similarly:

- Meshes within `mesh->GetRadius() + meshRadius` are added as `IPLInstancedMesh`
- Transform updates are applied only when position/rotation changes [src/AudioSpace.cpp:365-375]()
- Meshes are stored in `rootScene` which the simulator references

### Transform Spaces

All positions must be converted to **room space** (the space's local coordinate system) for Steam Audio:

```cpp
auto sourceInRoomSpace = invRoomTransform * vector4(sourcePos, 1);
```

This occurs because Steam Audio's simulation works in a local coordinate system where the room is centered at the origin.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/AudioSpace.hpp:111-226](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:105-163](), [src/AudioSpace.cpp:133-462]()

---

## BoxReverbationAudioSpace

`BoxReverbationAudioSpace` provides box-shaped room reverberation using Google's Resonance Audio library. It models a simple rectangular room with configurable wall materials and reverb properties.

### Configuration

```cpp
class BoxReverbationAudioSpace : public ComponentWithOwner, 
                                  public Queryable<BoxReverbationAudioSpace> {
public:
    struct RoomProperties {
        float reflection_scalar = 1;
        float reverb_gain = 1;
        float reverb_time = 1;
        float reverb_brightness = 0;
    };
    
    BoxReverbationAudioSpace(Entity owner);
    
    void SetHalfExts(const vector3& halfExts);  // Room half-dimensions
    void SetWallMaterial(uint8_t idx, RoomMat material);
    void SetWallMaterials(const Array<RoomMat, 6>& materials);
    
    vector3 GetHalfExts() const;
    Array<RoomMat, 6> GetWallMaterials() const;
    RoomProperties& GetRoomProperties();
};
```

### Wall Material Indexing

Wall materials are specified in this order [include/RavEngine/AudioSpace.hpp:240-246]():

| Index | Surface | Axis |
|-------|---------|------|
| 0 | Left | -X |
| 1 | Right | +X |
| 2 | Bottom | -Y |
| 3 | Top | +Y |
| 4 | Front | -Z |
| 5 | Back | +Z |

Available materials are defined by Resonance Audio's `RoomMat` enum (e.g., `kTransparent`, `kConcrete`, `kWood`, etc.).

### Processing Pipeline

```mermaid
graph TD
    ListenerCheck["AABB check:<br/>listener in room bounds<br/>pointInAABB(lpos, roomHalfExts)"]
    
    subgraph "Source Processing"
        ConsiderSource["For each source:<br/>ConsiderAudioSource()"]
        AABBCheck["AABB check in room space"]
        CreateOrUpdate["Create/update/destroy<br/>Resonance source ID"]
        SetBuffer["SetInterleavedBuffer()<br/>Upload mono source data"]
        SetTransform["SetSourcePosition()<br/>SetSourceRotation()"]
        CalcGain["ComputeRoomEffectsGain()<br/>Distance-based attenuation"]
    end
    
    UpdateWalls["Update room properties<br/>(if wallsNeedUpdate)"]
    SetListener["SetHeadPosition()<br/>SetHeadRotation()"]
    FillOutput["FillPlanarOutputBuffer()<br/>Render all sources with reverb"]
    EffectGraph["AudioGraphComposed::Render()"]
    
    ListenerCheck -->|"inside"| ConsiderSource
    ConsiderSource --> AABBCheck
    AABBCheck -->|"inside"| CreateOrUpdate
    CreateOrUpdate --> SetBuffer
    SetBuffer --> SetTransform
    SetTransform --> CalcGain
    
    CalcGain --> UpdateWalls
    UpdateWalls --> SetListener
    SetListener --> FillOutput
    FillOutput --> EffectGraph
```

The processing occurs in [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:213-243]() and [src/AudioSpaceBoxReverbation.cpp:20-105]():

1. **Listener AABB Check:** Verify listener is inside room bounds [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:230-232]()
2. **Consider Sources:** For each source, check if inside room (AABB in room space) and create/update/destroy Resonance source IDs [src/AudioSpaceBoxReverbation.cpp:20-63]()
3. **Render Space:** 
   - Update wall properties if changed [src/AudioSpaceBoxReverbation.cpp:71-93]()
   - Set listener transform [src/AudioSpaceBoxReverbation.cpp:68-69]()
   - Call `FillPlanarOutputBuffer()` to render all sources with reverb [src/AudioSpaceBoxReverbation.cpp:103]()

### Resonance Audio Source Management

```cpp
void ConsiderAudioSource(const PlanarSampleBufferInlineView& monoSourceData,
                        const vector3& worldPos, const quaternion& worldRot,
                        const matrix4& invRoomTransform, entity_t ownerID,
                        const vector3& roomHalfExts)
{
    auto roomSpacePos = invRoomTransform * vector4(worldPos, 1);
    bool isInRoom = RMath::pointInAABB(roomSpacePos, roomHalfExts);
    
    auto it = sourceMap.find(ownerID.id);
    SourceId src;
    
    if (it == sourceMap.end()) {
        if (!isInRoom) return;  // Not in room, wasn't before
        
        src = audioEngine->CreateSoundObjectSource(kBinauralLowQuality);
        sourceMap.emplace(ownerID.id, src);
    } else {
        src = it->second;
        if (!isInRoom) {
            // Was in room, no longer - destroy
            audioEngine->DestroySource(src);
            sourceMap.erase(ownerID.id);
            return;
        }
    }
    
    // Upload source data and transform
    audioEngine->SetInterleavedBuffer(src, monoSourceData.data(), 1, 
                                     monoSourceData.sizeOneChannel());
    audioEngine->SetSourcePosition(src, roomSpacePos.x, roomSpacePos.y, roomSpacePos.z);
    audioEngine->SetSourceRotation(src, roomSpaceRot.x, roomSpaceRot.y, 
                                  roomSpaceRot.z, roomSpaceRot.w);
    
    // Calculate and apply room effects gain
    auto gain = vraudio::ComputeRoomEffectsGain(eroompos, {0,0,0}, 
                                                eroomrot, eroomdim);
    audioEngine->SetSourceRoomEffectsGain(src, gain);
}
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/AudioSpace.hpp:228-312](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:213-243](), [src/AudioSpaceBoxReverbation.cpp:1-116]()

---

## Spatial Processing in AudioPlayer

The `AudioPlayer` orchestrates spatial processing through taskflow-based parallel execution. Each space type has dedicated processing:

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Audio Thread Taskflow"
        Preamble["PerformAudioTickPreamble<br/>Setup iterators, listener"]
        
        ProcessProviders["for_each dataProviders<br/>Fill source buffers"]
        
        ProcessSimple["for_each simpleAudioSpaces<br/>CalculateSimpleAudioSpace()"]
        ProcessGeometry["for_each geometryAudioSpaces<br/>CalculateGeometryAudioSpace()"]
        ProcessBox["for_each boxAudioSpaces<br/>CalculateBoxAudioSpace()"]
        
        FinalMix["CalculateFinalMix()<br/>Accumulate all spaces<br/>Interleave to SDL"]
    end
    
    Preamble --> ProcessProviders
    ProcessProviders --> ProcessSimple
    ProcessProviders --> ProcessGeometry
    ProcessProviders --> ProcessBox
    
    ProcessSimple --> FinalMix
    ProcessGeometry --> FinalMix
    ProcessBox --> FinalMix
```

The task graph is set up in [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:391-423](). Each space type processes in parallel after data providers fill source buffers.

### Listener Transform

The listener position and orientation are extracted from the snapshot [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:365-368]():

```cpp
lpos = SnapshotToRender->listenerPos;
lrot = SnapshotToRender->listenerRot;
listenerTransform = glm::translate(matrix4(1), (vector3)lpos) * glm::toMat4((quaternion)lrot);
invListenerTransform = glm::inverse(listenerTransform);
```

Most spatial calculations require transforming source positions into listener space using `invListenerTransform`.

### Final Mix Accumulation

`CalculateFinalMix()` [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:245-320]() accumulates outputs from all spaces:

```cpp
// Ambient sources (unspatialized)
for (auto& source : ambientSources) {
    AdditiveBlendSamples(sharedBufferView, source->renderData.GetReadonlyDataBufferView());
}

// All space types
for (const auto& r : simpleAudioSpaces) {
    AdditiveBlendSamples(sharedBufferView, r.room->accumulationBuffer.GetReadonlyDataBufferView());
}
for (const auto& r : geometryAudioSpaces) {
    AdditiveBlendSamples(sharedBufferView, r.room->accumulationBuffer.GetReadonlyDataBufferView());
}
for (const auto& r : boxAudioSpaces) {
    AdditiveBlendSamples(sharedBufferView, r.room->workingBuffers.GetReadonlyDataBufferView());
}

// Convert planar to interleaved and clamp
```

The final mix is converted from planar to interleaved format [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:300-307]() and clamped to `[-1, 1]` [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:314-317]() before submission to SDL.

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:86-423]()

---

## Best Practices and Performance

### Choosing an Audio Space Type

| Scenario | Recommended Space |
|----------|-------------------|
| Basic 3D positioning for multiple sources | `SimpleAudioSpace` |
| Outdoor environments without occlusion | `SimpleAudioSpace` |
| Indoor environments with walls/obstacles | `GeometryAudioSpace` |
| Small rooms requiring realistic reverb | `BoxReverbationAudioSpace` |
| Large open areas with distant sources | None (use `AmbientAudioSourceComponent`) |

### Performance Considerations

1. **Radius Management:**
   - Keep `sourceRadius` and `meshRadius` as small as practical
   - Larger radii increase per-frame processing cost
   - Consider multiple smaller spaces instead of one large space

2. **GeometryAudioSpace Complexity:**
   - Mesh occluders have significant cost; use sparingly
   - Simulation settings [src/AudioSpace.cpp:135-147]() control quality/performance tradeoff
   - `maxNumSources = 8` limits concurrent simulated sources

3. **BoxReverbationAudioSpace:**
   - Resonance Audio is less expensive than GeometryAudioSpace
   - Use for simple room acoustics without complex occlusion needs
   - Wall material updates are deferred until render [src/AudioSpaceBoxReverbation.cpp:71-93]()

4. **Multiple Overlapping Spaces:**
   - Sources can be processed by multiple spaces simultaneously
   - Results are additively blended [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:264-282]()
   - This can create interesting effects but increases CPU cost

### Transform Space Gotchas

All spaces except `SimpleAudioSpace` require positions in **room space** (local to the space's transform). The engine handles this conversion:

```cpp
// World space â†’ Room space
auto roomSpacePos = invRoomTransform * vector4(worldPos, 1);
```

For `SimpleAudioSpace`, the conversion to listener space happens in the rendering function [src/AudioSpace.cpp:71]():

```cpp
auto sourcePosInListenerSpace = vector3(invListenerTransform * vector4(sourcePos, 1));
```

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:105-346](), [src/AudioSpace.cpp:133-462](), [src/AudioSpaceBoxReverbation.cpp:1-116]()34:T51fb,# Audio System Architecture

## Purpose and Scope

This document covers the internal architecture of RavEngine's audio rendering system, focusing on the `AudioPlayer` threading model, snapshot-based rendering, Taskflow integration for parallel processing, and external library usage. For information about creating and using audio sources and audio spaces from a user perspective, see [Audio Sources and Playback](#7.1) and [Spatial Audio and Audio Spaces](#7.2).

---

## Overview

The `AudioPlayer` implements a sophisticated multi-threaded architecture designed to achieve low-latency 3D spatial audio while maximizing CPU parallelism. The system operates independently from the main game thread, consuming audio data through lock-free snapshot-based communication. Processing is distributed across multiple worker threads using the Taskflow library, with final output delivered to SDL's audio subsystem.

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:1-514](), [include/RavEngine/AudioPlayer.hpp:1-143]()

---

## Threading Model

### Dedicated Audio Thread

The audio system runs on a dedicated thread separate from the main `World` tick thread, continuously calling `AudioPlayer::Tick()` to maintain a steady stream of audio samples to the output device.

```mermaid
graph TD
    MainThread["Main Thread<br/>(World::Tick)"]
    AudioThread["Audio Thread<br/>(AudioPlayer::Tick)"]
    WorkerPool["Taskflow Worker Pool<br/>(2 threads)"]
    SDLDevice["SDL Audio Device"]
    
    MainThread -->|"Creates AudioSnapshot"| SnapshotA["AudioSnapshot A"]
    MainThread -->|"Creates AudioSnapshot"| SnapshotB["AudioSnapshot B"]
    
    SnapshotA -->|"Lock-free atomic swap"| AudioThread
    SnapshotB -->|"Lock-free atomic swap"| AudioThread
    
    AudioThread -->|"Dispatch tasks"| WorkerPool
    WorkerPool -->|"Parallel processing"| Mix["Final Mix Buffer"]
    Mix -->|"SDL_PutAudioStreamData"| SDLDevice
    
    AudioThread -.->|"Backpressure check<br/>SDL_GetAudioStreamQueued"| SDLDevice
```

**Thread Lifecycle:**

The audio thread is spawned during `AudioPlayer::Init()` and runs continuously until shutdown:

- **Initialization:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:487-492]()
- **Thread Loop:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:86-103]()
- **Shutdown:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:495-505]()

The thread detaches immediately after creation and polls continuously, checking the SDL audio queue for backpressure before processing each frame.

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:86-103](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:487-492](), [include/RavEngine/AudioPlayer.hpp:69-70]()

### Worker Thread Pool

The audio thread dispatches work to a Taskflow executor configured with 2 worker threads and a custom `AudioWorker` interface that sets thread names for debugging:

```cpp
// Worker thread configuration
struct AudioWorker : public tf::WorkerInterface {
    void scheduler_prologue(tf::Worker& worker) final {
        // Sets thread name to "Audio Worker"
    }
};

// Executor initialization
tf::Executor audioExecutor{2, std::make_shared<AudioWorker>()};
```

This allows parallel processing of audio sources, ambient sources, and audio spaces while the main audio thread coordinates task execution.

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:46-58](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:72-74](), [include/RavEngine/AudioPlayer.hpp:50-51]()

---

## Snapshot-Based Rendering

### Lock-Free Data Exchange

To avoid blocking either the game thread or audio thread, RavEngine uses double-buffered `AudioSnapshot` structures that are atomically swapped:

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Main Thread"
        WorldTick["World::Tick"]
        CreateSnapshot["Create AudioSnapshot"]
        PopulateSnapshot["Populate with:<br/>- Point sources<br/>- Ambient sources<br/>- Audio spaces<br/>- Listener state"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Double Buffer"
        SnapshotWrite["Write Snapshot"]
        SnapshotRead["Read Snapshot"]
        AtomicSwap["Atomic Pointer Swap<br/>(lock-free)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Audio Thread"
        CheckSwap["SwapRenderAudioSnapshotIfNeeded"]
        GetSnapshot["GetRenderAudioSnapshot"]
        ProcessAudio["Process Audio"]
    end
    
    WorldTick --> CreateSnapshot
    CreateSnapshot --> PopulateSnapshot
    PopulateSnapshot --> SnapshotWrite
    SnapshotWrite --> AtomicSwap
    AtomicSwap --> SnapshotRead
    
    CheckSwap --> AtomicSwap
    GetSnapshot --> SnapshotRead
    SnapshotRead --> ProcessAudio
```

**Snapshot Structure:**

The `AudioSnapshot` contains all data needed to render audio for one frame:

| Field | Type | Description |
|-------|------|-------------|
| `sources` | `UnorderedVector<PointSource>` | Point audio sources with world positions |
| `dataProviders` | `UnorderedSet<Ref<AudioDataProvider>>` | Unique set of data providers to process |
| `ambientSources` | `UnorderedVector<Ref<AudioDataProvider>>` | Non-spatialized audio sources |
| `simpleAudioSpaces` | `Vector<SimpleAudioSpaceData>` | Simple HRTF-only audio spaces |
| `geometryAudioSpaces` | `Vector<GeometryAudioSpaceData>` | Geometry-based occlusion spaces |
| `boxAudioSpaces` | `Vector<BoxReverbationSpaceData>` | Box reverb spaces |
| `audioMeshes` | `Vector<AudioMeshData>` | Mesh occluders for geometry spaces |
| `listenerPos` | `vector3` | Listener world position |
| `listenerRot` | `quaternion` | Listener world rotation |
| `sourceWorld` | `WeakRef<World>` | Reference to source world for cleanup |

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/AudioSnapshot.hpp:1-99](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:86-93]()

### Snapshot Access Pattern

```cpp
// In AudioPlayer::Tick()
auto queuedSize = SDL_GetAudioStreamQueued(stream);
if (queuedSize < maxAudioSampleLatency) {
    GetApp()->SwapRenderAudioSnapshotIfNeeded();
    SnapshotToRender = GetApp()->GetRenderAudioSnapshot();
    audioExecutor.run(audioTaskflow).wait();
    SDL_PutAudioStreamData(stream, interleavedOutputBuffer.data(), ...);
}
```

The audio thread only processes when the SDL queue has capacity, ensuring consistent latency without buffer underruns.

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:86-103]()

---

## Audio Processing Pipeline

### Taskflow Graph Structure

The `AudioPlayer` constructs a Taskflow DAG (Directed Acyclic Graph) at initialization that defines parallel execution dependencies:

```mermaid
graph TD
    Preamble["Preamble Task<br/>PerformAudioTickPreamble<br/>Update iterators & listener"]
    
    DataProviders["for_each: Process Data Providers<br/>Fill audio buffers from assets"]
    Ambients["for_each: Process Ambient Sources<br/>Fill ambient audio buffers"]
    
    SimpleSpaces["for_each: Calculate Simple Spaces<br/>HRTF spatialization"]
    GeometrySpaces["for_each: Calculate Geometry Spaces<br/>Occlusion & reflection"]
    BoxSpaces["for_each: Calculate Box Spaces<br/>Resonance Audio reverb"]
    
    FinalMix["Final Mix<br/>CalculateFinalMix<br/>Blend all sources, interleave, clamp"]
    
    Preamble --> DataProviders
    Preamble --> Ambients
    
    DataProviders --> SimpleSpaces
    DataProviders --> GeometrySpaces
    DataProviders --> BoxSpaces
    
    DataProviders --> FinalMix
    Ambients --> FinalMix
    SimpleSpaces --> FinalMix
    GeometrySpaces --> FinalMix
    BoxSpaces --> FinalMix
```

**Task Graph Setup:**

The taskflow graph is constructed once during initialization and reused every frame:

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:391-424](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:457-459]()

### Processing Stages

#### 1. Preamble Stage

The preamble task updates iterators for parallel iteration and computes listener transform matrices:

```cpp
void AudioPlayer::PerformAudioTickPreamble() {
    // Update iterators for parallel for_each
    dataProvidersBegin = SnapshotToRender->dataProviders.begin();
    dataProvidersEnd = SnapshotToRender->dataProviders.end();
    // ... (similar for other collections)
    
    // Compute listener transforms
    lpos = SnapshotToRender->listenerPos;
    lrot = SnapshotToRender->listenerRot;
    listenerTransform = glm::translate(matrix4(1), lpos) * glm::toMat4(lrot);
    invListenerTransform = glm::inverse(listenerTransform);
    
    // Copy destroyed entity IDs from lock-free queue
    destroyedSources.clear();
    entity_id_t id = INVALID_ENTITY;
    while (lockedworld->destroyedAudioSources.try_dequeue(id)) {
        destroyedSources.push_back(id);
    }
}
```

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:348-389]()

#### 2. Data Provider Processing

Each `AudioDataProvider` (representing a point source or ambient source) fills its render buffer with audio samples from its asset:

```cpp
constexpr auto doDataProvider = [](auto&& player) {
    auto renderData = &player->renderData;
    auto sharedBufferView = renderData->GetWritableDataBufferView();
    auto effectScratchBuffer = renderData->GetWritableScratchBufferView();
    player->ProvideBufferData(sharedBufferView, effectScratchBuffer);
};
```

This stage runs in parallel using Taskflow's `for_each`:

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:31-43](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:399-402]()

#### 3. Audio Space Processing

Three types of audio spaces process point sources in parallel:

| Space Type | Processing | Parallelization |
|------------|-----------|-----------------|
| **SimpleAudioSpace** | Steam Audio binaural HRTF + distance attenuation | Parallel for_each over spaces |
| **GeometryAudioSpace** | Steam Audio simulation with mesh occlusion/reflection | Parallel for_each over spaces |
| **BoxReverbationAudioSpace** | Resonance Audio room reverb | Parallel for_each over spaces |

Each space accumulates the spatialized output of all sources within its radius into its own accumulation buffer.

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:105-243](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:405-415]()

#### 4. Final Mix Stage

The final mix task blends all audio sources into the output buffer:

```mermaid
graph LR
    AmbientBuffers["Ambient Source Buffers"]
    SimpleAccum["Simple Space Accumulation Buffers"]
    GeometryAccum["Geometry Space Accumulation Buffers"]
    BoxWorkingBuffers["Box Space Working Buffers"]
    
    Accumulator["Planar Accumulation Buffer<br/>AdditiveBlendSamples"]
    Interleave["Convert Planar to Interleaved<br/>LLLL...RRRR â†’ LRLRLR..."]
    Clamp["Clamp samples to [-1.0, 1.0]"]
    Output["interleavedOutputBuffer"]
    
    AmbientBuffers --> Accumulator
    SimpleAccum --> Accumulator
    GeometryAccum --> Accumulator
    BoxWorkingBuffers --> Accumulator
    
    Accumulator --> Interleave
    Interleave --> Clamp
    Clamp --> Output
```

**Blending Implementation:**

```cpp
void AudioPlayer::CalculateFinalMix() {
    // Zero the accumulation buffer
    TZero(sharedBufferView.data(), sharedBufferView.size());
    
    // Blend ambient sources
    for (auto& source : SnapshotToRender->ambientSources) {
        AdditiveBlendSamples(sharedBufferView, source->renderData.GetReadonlyDataBufferView());
    }
    
    // Blend all audio space outputs
    for (const auto& r : SnapshotToRender->simpleAudioSpaces) {
        AdditiveBlendSamples(sharedBufferView, r.room->accumulationBuffer.GetReadonlyDataBufferView());
    }
    // ... (similar for geometry and box spaces)
    
    // Convert planar to interleaved and clamp
    blendBufferIn(sharedBufferView);
    for (int i = 0; i < accumView.size(); i++) {
        accumView[i] = std::clamp(accumView[i], -1.0f, 1.0f);
    }
}
```

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:245-320](), [include/RavEngine/AudioTypes.hpp:97-111]()

---

## Buffer Management

### Planar vs Interleaved Representation

RavEngine uses **planar** audio buffers internally for efficient SIMD processing, converting to **interleaved** format only when pushing to SDL:

**Planar Format (Internal):**
```
Channel 0: L L L L L L L L ...
Channel 1: R R R R R R R R ...
```

**Interleaved Format (SDL Output):**
```
L R L R L R L R L R ...
```

**Conversion:**
```cpp
// Planar to interleaved conversion with additive blend
const auto blendBufferIn = [accumView](PlanarSampleBufferInlineView sourceView) {
    const auto nchannels = sourceView.GetNChannels();
    for (int i = 0; i < accumView.size(); i++) {
        // Planar-to-interleaved: accumView[i] maps to sourceView[channel][frame]
        accumView[i] += sourceView[i % nchannels][i / nchannels];
    }
};
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/AudioTypes.hpp:20-95](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:300-311]()

### Buffer Types

| Type | Purpose | Scratch Buffer |
|------|---------|----------------|
| `SingleAudioRenderBuffer` | Stores audio data and effect scratch space | Yes |
| `SingleAudioRenderBufferNoScratch` | Accumulation buffer without scratch space | No |
| `PlanarSampleBufferInlineView` | Non-owning view of planar audio | N/A |
| `InterleavedSampleBufferView` | Non-owning view of interleaved audio | N/A |

**SingleAudioRenderBuffer Structure:**

Each audio space and data provider maintains its own render buffers:

```cpp
struct SingleAudioRenderBuffer {
    std::vector<float> dataBuffer;      // Planar audio data
    std::vector<float> scratchBuffer;   // Effect processing scratch space
    
    PlanarSampleBufferInlineView GetWritableDataBufferView();
    PlanarSampleBufferInlineView GetReadonlyDataBufferView() const;
    PlanarSampleBufferInlineView GetWritableScratchBufferView();
};
```

The scratch buffer is used during effect graph processing to avoid allocating temporary memory each frame.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/AudioSource.hpp:64-66](), [include/RavEngine/AudioSpace.hpp:82-83]()

---

## External Library Integration

### SDL Audio Subsystem

**Purpose:** SDL provides cross-platform audio device I/O and sample rate conversion.

**Initialization:**

```cpp
void AudioPlayer::Init() {
    SDL_InitSubSystem(SDL_INIT_AUDIO);
    
    SDL_AudioSpec want;
    want.freq = config_samplesPerSec;      // 44,100 Hz
    want.format = SDL_AUDIO_F32;           // 32-bit float
    want.channels = config_nchannels;      // 2 (stereo)
    
    stream = SDL_OpenAudioDeviceStream(SDL_AUDIO_DEVICE_DEFAULT_PLAYBACK, &want, NULL, this);
    SDL_ResumeAudioDevice(SDL_GetAudioStreamDevice(stream));
}
```

**Audio Output:**

Each frame, the audio thread pushes interleaved float samples to SDL's audio stream:

```cpp
SDL_PutAudioStreamData(stream, 
    interleavedOutputBuffer.data(), 
    interleavedOutputBuffer.size() * sizeof(float));
```

SDL handles buffering, resampling (if needed), and delivery to the OS audio device.

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:428-463](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:100](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:502]()

### Steam Audio (phonon)

**Purpose:** Steam Audio provides high-quality binaural HRTF spatialization and geometry-based occlusion/reflection simulation.

**Component Integration:**

```mermaid
graph TD
    subgraph "Steam Audio Resources"
        Context["IPLContext<br/>Global Steam Audio context"]
        HRTF["IPLHRTF<br/>Head-Related Transfer Function<br/>Default HRTF dataset"]
        AudioSettings["IPLAudioSettings<br/>Sample rate: 44,100<br/>Frame size: 512"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Simple Audio Space"
        BinauralEffect["IPLBinauralEffect<br/>Per-source spatialization"]
        DirectEffect["IPLDirectEffect<br/>Distance attenuation"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Geometry Audio Space"
        Simulator["IPLSimulator<br/>Occlusion/reflection simulation"]
        Scene["IPLScene<br/>Mesh occluder container"]
        Source["IPLSource<br/>Per-source simulation state"]
        InstancedMesh["IPLInstancedMesh<br/>Static mesh occluder"]
        PathEffect["IPLPathEffect<br/>Reflection paths"]
    end
    
    Context --> BinauralEffect
    Context --> DirectEffect
    Context --> Simulator
    Context --> Scene
    
    HRTF --> BinauralEffect
    
    Scene --> InstancedMesh
    Simulator --> Source
    Simulator --> PathEffect
```

**Initialization:**

Steam Audio resources are initialized once during `AudioPlayer::Init()`:

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:464-485](), [src/AudioSpace.cpp:21-97](), [src/AudioSpace.cpp:133-321]()

### Resonance Audio

**Purpose:** Resonance Audio provides room reverberation modeling for `BoxReverbationAudioSpace`.

**Integration:**

```cpp
class BoxReverbationAudioSpace::RoomData {
    vraudio::ResonanceAudioApi* audioEngine;
    UnorderedMap<entity_id_t, vraudio::ResonanceAudioApi::SourceId> sourceMap;
    
    void ConsiderAudioSource(...) {
        auto src = audioEngine->CreateSoundObjectSource(vraudio::RenderingMode::kBinauralLowQuality);
        audioEngine->SetInterleavedBuffer(src, monoSourceData.data(), 1, monoSourceData.sizeOneChannel());
        audioEngine->SetSourcePosition(src, x, y, z);
        audioEngine->SetSourceRoomEffectsGain(src, gain);
    }
    
    void RenderSpace(...) {
        audioEngine->SetHeadPosition(listenerPos.x, listenerPos.y, listenerPos.z);
        audioEngine->SetHeadRotation(listenerRot.x, listenerRot.y, listenerRot.z, listenerRot.w);
        audioEngine->FillPlanarOutputBuffer(nchannels, bufferSize, outputChannelPtrs);
    }
};
```

Resonance Audio manages its own internal source state and outputs directly to planar buffers.

**Sources:** [src/AudioSpaceBoxReverbation.cpp:1-117](), [include/RavEngine/AudioSpace.hpp:228-271]()

## Performance Characteristics

### Configuration Constants

| Constant | Value | Description |
|----------|-------|-------------|
| `config_buffersize` | 512 | Samples per audio frame |
| `config_samplesPerSec` | 44,100 | Sample rate (Hz) |
| `config_nchannels` | 2 | Output channels (stereo) |
| `maxAudioSampleLatency` | 8,192 | Maximum SDL queue size (16 frames) |
| Taskflow workers | 2 | Worker threads for parallel processing |

**Frame Duration:**
```
512 samples / 44,100 Hz = 11.6 ms per frame
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/AudioPlayer.hpp:42-44](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:453]()

### Parallel Execution

The Taskflow graph enables parallel execution across:
1. **Data providers** (point sources filling buffers)
2. **Ambient sources** (non-spatialized sources filling buffers)
3. **Audio spaces** (Simple, Geometry, and Box spaces processing in parallel)

Within each audio space, sources are processed sequentially but spaces execute concurrently. This design balances parallelism with cache locality.

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:391-424]()

---

## Entity Lifecycle and Cleanup

### Destroyed Entity Handling

When an `AudioSourceComponent` or mesh occluder is destroyed in the World, its entity ID is pushed to a lock-free queue. The audio thread consumes these IDs during the preamble stage:

```cpp
void AudioPlayer::PerformAudioTickPreamble() {
    // Consume destroyed source IDs from lock-free queue
    destroyedSources.clear();
    entity_id_t id = INVALID_ENTITY;
    while (lockedworld->destroyedAudioSources.try_dequeue(id)) {
        destroyedSources.push_back(id);
    }
    
    // Similarly for mesh components
    destroyedMeshComponents.clear();
    while (lockedworld->destroyedMeshComponents.try_dequeue(id)) {
        destroyedMeshComponents.push_back(id);
    }
}
```

Each audio space then cleans up its internal state for destroyed entities:

```cpp
void SimpleAudioSpace::RoomData::DeleteAudioDataForEntity(entity_id_t entity) {
    steamAudioData.if_contains(entity, [this](auto&& effects) {
        iplBinauralEffectRelease(&effects.second.binauralEffect);
        iplDirectEffectRelease(&effects.second.directEffect);
    });
    steamAudioData.erase(entity);
}
```

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:374-388](), [src/AudioSpace.cpp:99-105](), [src/AudioSpace.cpp:436-441]()

---

## Summary

The `AudioPlayer` architecture achieves low-latency, high-quality 3D audio through:

1. **Dedicated audio thread** with lock-free snapshot-based data exchange
2. **Taskflow parallelization** distributing work across 2 worker threads
3. **Planar buffer management** for efficient SIMD processing
4. **External library integration** leveraging Steam Audio and Resonance Audio
5. **Careful resource management** with per-entity cleanup coordination

This design decouples audio rendering from the main game loop while maximizing CPU utilization, enabling complex spatial audio simulations with minimal latency.

**Sources:** [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:1-514](), [include/RavEngine/AudioPlayer.hpp:1-143]()35:T4dbe,# User Interface

## Purpose and Scope

This document covers RavEngine's user interface system, which provides HTML/CSS-based GUI rendering through RmlUi integration. The system enables creation of interactive 2D interfaces that can be rendered in screen-space or world-space. For information about debug visualization overlays, see [Debug Rendering](#8.2). For general input handling outside of UI context, see [Input System](#3.4).

---

## Architecture Overview

RavEngine's UI system integrates the RmlUi library to provide web-standard HTML/CSS document rendering. The system handles input event routing, thread-safe UI updates, and efficient GPU rendering through the main render pipeline.

**Diagram: UI System Architecture**

```mermaid

        World["World"]
        InputMgr["InputManager"]

    end
    
    subgraph "RmlUi Integration"

    end
    
    subgraph "Rendering Backend"
        RenderEngine["RenderEngine<br/>RML Render Interface"]

        GuiPipeline["guiRenderPipeline<br/>RGL Pipeline"]
    end

        EventQueue["ConcurrentQueue<br/>Double-buffered"]
    end
```

## GUIComponent Class

The `GUIComponent` class is the primary interface for creating and managing UI in RavEngine. Each component owns an RmlUi context and can load multiple HTML documents.

### Class Structure

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class GUIComponent {
        +RenderMode Mode
        -Ref~GUIData~ data
        +GUIComponent()
        +GUIComponent(width, height, DPI)
        +AddDocument(name) ElementDocument*
        +RemoveDocument(name)
        +GetDocument(name) ElementDocument*
        +IsDocumentLoaded(name) bool
        +SetDimensions(width, height)
        +MouseX(normalized_pos)
        +MouseY(normalized_pos)
        +ScrollY(amt)
        +ExclusiveAccess(func)
        +EnqueueUIUpdate(func)
        +Update() bool
        +Render() bool
        +static LoadFont(filename) bool
    }
    
    class GUIData {
        +Rml::Context* context
        +locked_hashmap documents
        +ConcurrentQueue q_a
        +ConcurrentQueue q_b
        +atomic current
        +atomic inactive
        +SpinLock mtx
        +uint32_t modifier_state
        +MousePos
        +AnyActionDown(charcode)
        +AnyActionUp(charcode)
        +TextInput(str)
        +ScrollY(amt)
        +MouseMove()
        +SetDimensions(width, height)
    }
    
    class IInputListener {
        <<interface>>
        +AnyActionDown(charcode)
        +AnyActionUp(charcode)
        +TextInput(str)
    }
    
    GUIComponent *-- GUIData : owns
    GUIData ..|> IInputListener : implements
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:22-191](), [src/GUI.cpp:126-154]()

### Render Modes

GUIComponent supports two rendering modes:

| Mode | Description | Use Case |
|------|-------------|----------|
| `RenderMode::Screenspace` | UI rendered in 2D overlay, always on top | HUD, menus, overlays |
| `RenderMode::Worldspace` | UI rendered as 3D object in world | In-game terminals, signs, displays |

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:78-81]()

## Document Management

UI content is organized into RML documents (`.rml` files) with associated stylesheets (`.rcss` files). Documents are loaded from the virtual filesystem and managed by the RmlUi context.

### Loading and Unloading Documents

**Diagram: Document Lifecycle**

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Unloaded
    Unloaded --> Loading : AddDocument(name)
    Loading --> Loaded : context->LoadDocument()
    Loaded --> Visible : Show()
    Visible --> Unloaded : RemoveDocument(name)
    
    note right of Loading
        File loaded from /uis/{name}
        via VFSInterface
    end note
    
    note right of Visible
        Document updates each frame
        via context->Update()
    end note
```

```cpp
// Add a document from the virtual filesystem
auto* doc = guiComponent->AddDocument("main_menu.rml");

// Check if loaded
if (guiComponent->IsDocumentLoaded("main_menu.rml")) {
    auto* doc = guiComponent->GetDocument("main_menu.rml");
    // Manipulate document...
}

// Remove when done
guiComponent->RemoveDocument("main_menu.rml");
```

**Implementation Details:**

- Documents are loaded from `/uis/` directory in the virtual filesystem
- Each document is shown automatically upon loading via `Show()`
- Multiple documents can be loaded simultaneously in the same context
- Documents are stored in a thread-safe `locked_hashmap`

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:53-84](), [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:100-125]()

### Font Loading

Fonts must be loaded globally before use in any document:

```cpp
// Fonts are loaded from /fonts/ directory
GUIComponent::LoadFont("RobotoMono-Regular.ttf");
```

The engine automatically loads all `.ttf` files from the `/fonts/` directory during initialization:

**Sources:** [src/App_priv.hpp:208-214](), [src/GUI.cpp:90-94]()

## Input Integration

The UI system integrates with RavEngine's input system to receive keyboard, mouse, and gamepad events. `GUIData` implements `IInputListener` to receive global input events.

### Input Event Flow

**Diagram: Input Processing Pipeline**

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant SDL as SDL_Event
    participant IM as InputManager
    participant GD as GUIData
    participant Q as EventQueue
    participant RC as Rml::Context
    
    SDL->>IM: SDL_EVENT_KEY_DOWN
    IM->>IM: ProcessInput()
    IM->>GD: AnyActionDown(scancode)
    
    GD->>GD: Update modifier_state
    GD->>Q: EnqueueUIUpdate(lambda)
    Note over Q: Lambda captures scancode<br/>and modifier state
    
    loop Each Frame
        GUIComponent->>GUIComponent: Update()
        GUIComponent->>Q: Swap current/inactive
        Q->>RC: context->ProcessKeyDown()
    end
```

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:155-249](), [src/InputManager.cpp:99-106](), [src/InputManager.cpp:130-206]()

### Event Types Processed

| Event Type | Handler Method | RmlUi Mapping |
|------------|----------------|---------------|
| Keyboard press | `AnyActionDown()` | `ProcessKeyDown()` |
| Keyboard release | `AnyActionUp()` | `ProcessKeyUp()` |
| Mouse button | `AnyActionDown()/Up()` | `ProcessMouseButtonDown()/Up()` |
| Mouse motion | `MouseMove()` | `ProcessMouseMove()` |
| Mouse wheel | `ScrollY()` | `ProcessMouseWheel()` |
| Text input | `TextInput()` | `ProcessTextInput()` |

**Modifier Key Tracking:**

The system maintains a bitmask of active modifier keys:

- `KM_CTRL` - Control/Command keys
- `KM_SHIFT` - Shift keys  
- `KM_META` - Alt/Option keys
- `KM_CAPSLOCK` - Caps Lock
- `KM_NUMLOCK` - Num Lock
- `KM_SCROLLLOCK` - Scroll Lock

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:162-248](), [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:27-64]()

### Mouse Position Handling

Mouse position is tracked in normalized [0,1] coordinates and converted to pixel coordinates before forwarding to RmlUi:

```cpp
void GUIComponent::MouseX(float normalized_pos) {
    data->MousePos.x = normalized_pos;
}

void GUIComponent::MouseY(float normalized_pos) {
    data->MousePos.y = normalized_pos;
}

void GUIData::MouseMove() {
    auto dim = context->GetDimensions();
    EnqueueUIUpdate([this, dim] {
        context->ProcessMouseMove(
            MousePos.x * dim.x, 
            MousePos.y * dim.y, 
            modifier_state
        );
    });
}
```

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:251-273](), [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:136-144]()

## Thread Safety

The UI system is designed for thread-safe operation since rendering occurs on a different thread than game logic updates.

### Double-Buffered Event Queue

**Diagram: Thread-Safe Update Mechanism**

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Main Thread (World::Tick)"
        Input["Input Events"]
        Enqueue["EnqueueUIUpdate()"]
    end
    
    subgraph "GUIData State"
        QA["Queue A"]
        QB["Queue B"]
        Current["current ptr"]
        Inactive["inactive ptr"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Render Thread"
        Update["Update()"]
        Swap["Swap Queues"]
        Process["Process Tasks"]
        RmlUpdate["context->Update()"]
    end
    
    Input -->|"EnqueueUIUpdate(task)"| Enqueue
    Enqueue -->|"enqueue to"| Current
    Current -.->|"atomic ptr"| QA
    
    Update --> Swap
    Swap -->|"swap(current, inactive)"| Current
    Swap -->|"swap(current, inactive)"| Inactive
    
    Inactive -.->|"atomic ptr"| QB
    QB -->|"dequeue tasks"| Process
    Process --> RmlUpdate
```

The system uses two `ConcurrentQueue` instances that are swapped each frame:

1. **Enqueue Phase** (Main Thread): Tasks are added to the `current` queue
2. **Swap Phase** (Render Thread): `current` and `inactive` pointers are swapped atomically
3. **Process Phase** (Render Thread): Tasks from the now-`inactive` queue are executed

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:32-59](), [src/GUI.cpp:96-117]()

### ExclusiveAccess Pattern

For immediate access to UI state, the `ExclusiveAccess()` method provides mutex-protected access:

```cpp
guiComponent->ExclusiveAccess([&] {
    auto* doc = guiComponent->GetDocument("hud.rml");
    auto* element = doc->GetElementById("health");
    element->SetInnerRML(std::to_string(playerHealth));
});
```

**Warning:** `ExclusiveAccess()` blocks both threads. For non-critical updates, prefer `EnqueueUIUpdate()`:

```cpp
guiComponent->EnqueueUIUpdate([playerHealth] {
    auto* doc = guiComponent->GetDocument("hud.rml");
    auto* element = doc->GetElementById("health");
    element->SetInnerRML(std::to_string(playerHealth));
});
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:49-59](), [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:157-169]()

---

## Rendering Integration

The UI system integrates with RenderEngine as an RmlUi render interface, handling geometry compilation and rendering.

### Render Pipeline Integration

**Diagram: GUI Rendering in Frame Pipeline**

```mermaid
graph TD
    Start["RenderEngine::Draw()"]
    
    Start --> WorldRender["Render World Geometry"]
    WorldRender --> PostProcess["Post-Processing"]
    PostProcess --> Tonemap["Tonemap to Framebuffer"]
    
    Tonemap --> GUIPass["Pass 7: GUI Rendering"]
    
    GUIPass --> FilterGUI["World->Filter(GUIComponent)"]
    FilterGUI --> UpdateGUI["gui.Update()"]
    UpdateGUI --> RenderGUI["gui.Render()"]
    
    RenderGUI --> CompileCheck{Geometry<br/>Compiled?}
    CompileCheck -->|No| CompileGeo["CompileGeometry()"]
    CompileCheck -->|Yes| UseCached["Use Cached"]
    
    CompileGeo --> CreateBuffers["Create Vertex/Index Buffers"]
    CreateBuffers --> RenderGeo["RenderGeometry()"]
    UseCached --> RenderGeo
    
    RenderGeo --> BindPipeline["Bind guiRenderPipeline"]
    BindPipeline --> SetScissor["Set Scissor Region"]
    SetScissor --> BindTexture["Bind Texture"]
    BindTexture --> DrawIndexed["DrawIndexed()"]
    
    DrawIndexed --> DebugRender["Pass 8: Debug Rendering"]
    DebugRender --> Submit["Submit Command Buffer"]
```

**Sources:** [src/App_priv.hpp:375-397](), [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:1-240]()

### Geometry Compilation

RmlUi requests geometry compilation for static UI elements. The engine creates GPU buffers for efficient rendering:

**RenderEngine Methods:**

| Method | Purpose | Returns |
|--------|---------|---------|
| `CompileGeometry()` | Create GPU buffers for vertices/indices | `CompiledGeometryHandle` |
| `RenderGeometry()` | Draw compiled geometry with texture | void |
| `ReleaseGeometry()` | Destroy GPU buffers | void |

**Compiled Geometry Structure:**

```cpp
struct CompiledGeoStruct {
    RGLBufferPtr vb;          // Vertex buffer
    RGLBufferPtr ib;          // Index buffer
    const uint32_t nindices;  // Index count
    
    void Destroy(RenderEngine*); // Enqueue for deletion
};
```

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:26-36](), [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:77-134]()

### Texture Management

The system manages textures for UI elements:

**Texture Operations:**

| Method | Purpose | Usage |
|--------|---------|-------|
| `LoadTexture()` | Load texture from VFS | Images referenced in RML |
| `GenerateTexture()` | Create texture from memory | Procedural/dynamic textures |
| `ReleaseTexture()` | Destroy texture | Cleanup |

Textures are loaded from the `/textures/` directory via the virtual filesystem and uploaded to GPU memory.

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:59-74](), [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:190-222]()

### GPU Shaders

The UI rendering uses dedicated vertex and fragment shaders:

**Vertex Shader (`gui.vsh`):**

- Inputs: position, color, texcoord
- Uniforms: transform matrix, projection matrix, translation
- Outputs: interpolated color and texcoords

**Fragment Shader (`gui.fsh`):**

- Inputs: interpolated color and texcoords  
- Textures: UI texture sampler
- Output: final RGBA color

The projection matrix converts from pixel space to normalized device coordinates:

```glsl
vec4 pos_document = vec4(vertex_pos + ubo.translation, 0, 1);
gl_Position = ubo.projection * ubo.transform * pos_document;
```

**Sources:** [shaders/gui.vsh:1-26](), [shaders/gui.fsh:1-14]()

### Scissor Region Support

RmlUi uses scissor rectangles to clip UI elements:

```cpp
void RenderEngine::EnableScissorRegion(bool enable) {
    RMLScissor.enabled = enable;
}

void RenderEngine::SetScissorRegion(Rml::Rectanglei region) {
    const auto xy = region.TopLeft();
    RMLScissor.x = xy.x;
    RMLScissor.y = xy.y;
    RMLScissor.width = region.Width();
    RMLScissor.height = region.Height();
}
```

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:176-187]()

## DPI Scaling

The system supports high-DPI displays through density-independent pixel ratios.

### DPI Scale Flow

```mermaid
graph LR
    Window["Window::GetDPIScale()"]

    GUI --> Context

```

The App automatically updates DPI scale for screen-space UI each frame:

```cpp
world->Filter([=](GUIComponent& gui) {
    if (gui.Mode == GUIComponent::RenderMode::Screenspace) {
        gui.SetDimensions(windowSize.width, windowSize.height);
        gui.SetDPIScale(scale);
    }
    gui.Update();
});
```

**Platform Behavior:**

| Platform | DPI Scaling |
|----------|-------------|
| macOS | Automatic retina scaling |
| Windows | Manual DPI awareness (disabled in code) |
| Linux | System DPI settings |

## Initialization and Lifecycle

### Engine Initialization

The App initializes RmlUi during startup:

```cpp
// Set system interfaces
Rml::SetSystemInterface(&rmlSystemInterface);
Rml::SetRenderInterface(&GetRenderEngine());
Rml::SetFileInterface(new VFSInterface());
Rml::Initialise();

// Load built-in fonts
App::Resources->IterateDirectory("fonts", [](const std::string& filename) {
    auto p = Filesystem::Path(filename);
    if (p.extension() == ".ttf") {
        GUIComponent::LoadFont(p.filename().string());
    }
});
```

**Interfaces:**

- **RMLSystemInterface** - Provides time information
- **RenderEngine** - Handles geometry/texture operations  
- **VFSInterface** - File loading from virtual filesystem

**Sources:** [src/App_priv.hpp:194-214]()

### Component Lifecycle

**Diagram: GUIComponent Lifecycle**

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Constructed : GUIComponent()
    Constructed --> ContextCreated : Create Rml::Context
    ContextCreated --> DocumentsLoaded : AddDocument()
    DocumentsLoaded --> Active : Update()/Render()
    Active --> Active : Each Frame
    Active --> DocumentsUnloaded : RemoveDocument()
    DocumentsUnloaded --> Destroyed : ~GUIData()
    Destroyed --> ContextRemoved : RemoveContext()
    ContextRemoved --> [*]
    
    note right of ContextCreated
        Context created with UUID
        DPI scale set
    end note
    
    note right of Destroyed
        All documents unloaded
        Context removed from RmlUi
    end note
```

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:127-154]()

### Cleanup

GUIData destructor ensures proper cleanup:

```cpp
GUIData::~GUIData() {
    for (const auto& pair : documents) {
        context->UnloadDocument(pair.second);
    }
    Rml::RemoveContext(context->GetName());
}
```

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:148-153]()

## Complete Usage Example

```cpp
// Create a GUI component
auto entity = world->EmplaceEntity();
auto& gui = entity.EmplaceComponent<GUIComponent>();

// Configure for screen-space rendering
gui.Mode = GUIComponent::RenderMode::Screenspace;

// Load a document
auto* mainMenu = gui.AddDocument("main_menu.rml");

// Bind input (in your input setup)
inputManager->BindAnyAction(gui.GetData());
inputManager->BindAxis("MouseX", gui, &GUIComponent::MouseX, CID::C0);
inputManager->BindAxis("MouseY", gui, &GUIComponent::MouseY, CID::C0);
inputManager->BindAxis("Scroll", gui, &GUIComponent::ScrollY, CID::C0);

// Update UI from game logic (thread-safe)
gui.EnqueueUIUpdate([&gui, score = playerScore] {
    auto* doc = gui.GetDocument("main_menu.rml");
    auto* scoreElement = doc->GetElementById("score");
    scoreElement->SetInnerRML(std::to_string(score));
});

// Access UI immediately (blocks)
gui.ExclusiveAccess([&] {
    auto* doc = gui.GetDocument("main_menu.rml");
    auto* button = doc->GetElementById("start_button");
    button->SetAttribute("disabled", "true");
});

// Cleanup
gui.RemoveDocument("main_menu.rml");
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:22-191](), [src/GUI.cpp:1-288]()36:T5437,# GUI Components and RmlUi

## Purpose and Scope

This document covers RavEngine's GUI system, which provides HTML/CSS-based user interfaces through RmlUi integration. The `GUIComponent` class enables creation of interactive UI elements that can be rendered in screenspace (overlays) or worldspace (3D UI panels). 

For immediate-mode debug visualization, see [Debug Rendering](#8.2). For post-processing effects and tonemapping, see [Post-Processing and Effects](#4.6).

---

## Overview

RavEngine integrates **RmlUi**, an HTML/CSS UI library, to provide declarative UI authoring. Documents are written in **RML** (markup) and **RCSS** (styling), loaded from the virtual filesystem, and rendered using GPU-accelerated geometry compilation. The system is thread-safe and supports DPI scaling, input processing, and both screenspace and worldspace rendering modes.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:1-193](), [src/GUI.cpp:1-288]()

---

## GUIComponent Class

### Basic Structure

```mermaid
graph TD
    GUIComponent["GUIComponent<br/>(AutoCTTI component)"]
    GUIData["GUIData<br/>(IInputListener)"]
    RmlContext["Rml::Context<br/>(RmlUi context)"]
    Documents["locked_hashmap<br/>string â†’ ElementDocument*"]
    Queues["ConcurrentQueue q_a, q_b<br/>(double-buffered UI updates)"]
    SpinLock["SpinLock mtx<br/>(exclusive access)"]
    
    GUIComponent -->|"owns Ref<GUIData>"| GUIData
    GUIData -->|"owns"| RmlContext
    GUIData -->|"owns"| Documents
    GUIData -->|"owns"| Queues
    GUIData -->|"owns"| SpinLock
    
    RmlContext -->|"manages"| ElementDocuments["Rml::ElementDocument*<br/>(loaded UI files)"]
    Documents -->|"stores"| ElementDocuments
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:22-64]()

### Construction and Configuration

The `GUIComponent` can be constructed with default screen dimensions or custom sizes:

| Constructor | Parameters | Description |
|------------|------------|-------------|
| `GUIComponent()` | None | Creates context at 960Ã—540 pixels |
| `GUIComponent(int width, int height, float DPIScale)` | width, height, DPI | Creates context with specified dimensions and DPI scaling |

**Render Modes:**

- **`RenderMode::Screenspace`**: UI rendered as 2D overlay on top of 3D scene
- **`RenderMode::Worldspace`**: UI rendered as texture in 3D world (not fully implemented)

The mode is controlled via the `Mode` member variable.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:78-95](), [src/GUI.cpp:127-134]()

---

## Document Management

### Document Lifecycle

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Unloaded
    Unloaded --> Loading: AddDocument(name)
    Loading --> Loaded: context->LoadDocument()
    Loaded --> Visible: document->Show()
    Visible --> Loaded: document->Hide()
    Loaded --> Unloading: RemoveDocument(name)
    Unloading --> [*]: context->UnloadDocument()
    
    note right of Loaded
        Document stored in
        documents hashmap
    end note
```

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:53-84]()

### Loading Documents

Documents are loaded from the `/uis/` directory in the virtual filesystem:

```cpp
Rml::ElementDocument* AddDocument(const std::string& name);
```

The method:
1. Checks if document already loaded via `IsDocumentLoaded(name)`
2. Constructs path as `/uis/{name}`
3. Calls `context->LoadDocument(dir)` within exclusive access
4. Shows document automatically via `ed->Show()`
5. Stores pointer in `documents` hashmap

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:53-72]()

### Unloading Documents

```cpp
void RemoveDocument(const std::string& name);
```

The method:
1. Verifies document is loaded
2. Retrieves pointer from `documents` hashmap
3. Removes from hashmap
4. Calls `context->UnloadDocument(ptr)` within exclusive access

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:74-84]()

### Querying Documents

```cpp
Rml::ElementDocument* GetDocument(const std::string& name) const;
bool IsDocumentLoaded(const std::string& name) const;
```

The `GetDocument()` method returns a raw pointer to the RmlUi `ElementDocument`. **Important:** This pointer is only safe to use within an `ExclusiveAccess` lambda to ensure thread safety.

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:86-88](), [src/GUI.cpp:140-145]()

---

## Input Processing

### Input Flow Architecture

```mermaid
graph LR
    SDL["SDL_Event<br/>(OS input)"]
    InputMgr["InputManager"]
    GUIData["GUIComponent::GUIData<br/>(IInputListener)"]
    RmlContext["Rml::Context"]
    
    SDL --> InputMgr
    InputMgr -->|"ProcessInput()"| InputMgr
    InputMgr -->|"AnyActionDown/Up"| GUIData
    InputMgr -->|"TextInput"| GUIData
    
    GUIData -->|"EnqueueUIUpdate"| Queue["ConcurrentQueue<br/>(q_a or q_b)"]
    Queue -->|"Update() processes"| RmlContext
    
    RmlContext -->|"ProcessKeyDown/Up<br/>ProcessMouseButtonDown/Up<br/>ProcessTextInput"| EventHandlers["Document Event Handlers"]
```

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:162-248](), [src/InputManager.cpp:99-106]()

### Input Event Handling

The `GUIData` class implements `IInputListener` to receive global input events:

| Method | Purpose | RmlUi API |
|--------|---------|-----------|
| `AnyActionDown(int charcode)` | Key/mouse press | `ProcessKeyDown()`, `ProcessMouseButtonDown()` |
| `AnyActionUp(int charcode)` | Key/mouse release | `ProcessKeyUp()`, `ProcessMouseButtonUp()` |
| `TextInput(string_view)` | Character input | `ProcessTextInput()` |

**Modifier Key Tracking:** The system maintains a `modifier_state` bitmask for Ctrl, Shift, Alt, CapsLock, NumLock, and ScrollLock. These are applied to all input events sent to RmlUi.

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:162-248](), [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:27-64]()

### Mouse Input Binding

Mouse axes must be explicitly bound:

```cpp
void MouseX(float normalized_pos);  // Position in [0,1)
void MouseY(float normalized_pos);  // Position in [0,1)
void ScrollY(float amt);            // Scroll delta
```

The `MouseMove()` method is called automatically during `Update()` to forward accumulated position to RmlUi.

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:251-273](), [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:136-151]()

### SDL to RmlUi Scancode Conversion

```mermaid
graph TD
    SDL["SDL Scancode<br/>(USB HID codes)"]
    Converter["SDLtoRML()<br/>function"]
    RML["Rml::Input::KeyIdentifier"]
    
    SDL -->|"SDL_SCANCODE_A-Z"| AZ["A-Z range<br/>offset conversion"]
    SDL -->|"Arrow keys"| Arrows["LEFT/RIGHT/UP/DOWN"]
    SDL -->|"Control keys"| Control["DELETE/BACK/HOME/END<br/>PRIOR/NEXT/INSERT/RETURN"]
    
    AZ --> Converter
    Arrows --> Converter
    Control --> Converter
    
    Converter --> RML
```

The conversion handles:
- **A-Z keys**: Offset calculation from `SDL_SCANCODE_A` to `KI_A`
- **Arrow keys**: Direct mapping to RmlUi arrow identifiers
- **Control keys**: Delete, Backspace, Home, End, PageUp, PageDown, Insert, Return, Tab

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:16-51]()

## Thread-Safe UI Updates

### Double-Buffered Queue System

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Frame N"
        GameThread1["Game Thread<br/>(writing)"]
        QA1["Queue A<br/>(current)"]
        QB1["Queue B<br/>(inactive)"]
        
        GameThread1 -->|"EnqueueUIUpdate"| QA1
    end
    
    subgraph "Frame N+1"
        RenderThread2["Render Thread<br/>(processing)"]
        GameThread2["Game Thread<br/>(writing)"]
        QA2["Queue A<br/>(inactive)"]
        QB2["Queue B<br/>(current)"]
        
        RenderThread2 -->|"Process queued updates"| QA2
        GameThread2 -->|"EnqueueUIUpdate"| QB2
    end
    
    QA1 -.->|"Swap at Update()"| QA2
    QB1 -.->|"Swap at Update()"| QB2
```

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:96-117](), [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:32-59]()

### Update Pattern: EnqueueUIUpdate

All UI modifications must be enqueued to avoid race conditions:

```cpp
template<typename T>
constexpr inline void EnqueueUIUpdate(const T& func);
```

The system uses atomic pointers to track `current` and `inactive` queues. During `Update()`:
1. Swaps queue pointers atomically
2. Processes all tasks in the newly-inactive queue
3. Calls `context->Update()` to recalculate layout

**Critical:** Capture by value in lambdas to avoid dangling references:

```cpp
// Correct
int value = 42;
gui.EnqueueUIUpdate([=] {
    document->SetAttribute("value", value);
});

// Wrong - 'value' may be destroyed before lambda executes
gui.EnqueueUIUpdate([&] {
    document->SetAttribute("value", value);
});
```

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:96-117](), [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:162-169]()

### ExclusiveAccess Pattern

For immediate synchronous access (rare cases):

```cpp
template<typename T>
constexpr inline void ExclusiveAccess(const T& func);
```

This acquires `mtx` spinlock, executes lambda, then releases. Used internally for document loading/unloading and by the render thread.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:49-54](), [src/GUI.cpp:61-63]()

---

## Rendering Architecture

### RmlUi Render Interface Implementation

```mermaid
graph TD
    RmlUI["Rml::RenderInterface<br/>(abstract interface)"]
    RenderEngine["RenderEngine<br/>(implements interface)"]
    
    RmlUI <-.->|"implements"| RenderEngine
    
    subgraph "Geometry Pipeline"
        CompileGeo["CompileGeometry()<br/>vertices + indices"]
        VBO["RGLBufferPtr<br/>(vertex buffer)"]
        IBO["RGLBufferPtr<br/>(index buffer)"]
        CGS["CompiledGeoStruct<br/>(handle storage)"]
        
        CompileGeo --> VBO
        CompileGeo --> IBO
        VBO --> CGS
        IBO --> CGS
    end
    
    subgraph "Texture Pipeline"
        LoadTex["LoadTexture()<br/>from VFS"]
        GenTex["GenerateTexture()<br/>from memory"]
        CreateTex["createTexture()<br/>helper function"]
        THS["TextureHandleStruct<br/>(RGLTexturePtr)"]
        
        LoadTex --> CreateTex
        GenTex --> CreateTex
        CreateTex --> THS
    end
    
    subgraph "Rendering"
        RenderGeo["RenderGeometry()<br/>draw call"]
        Pipeline["guiRenderPipeline"]
        Shader["gui.vsh + gui.fsh"]
        
        RenderGeo --> Pipeline
        Pipeline --> Shader
        RenderGeo -.->|"binds"| CGS
        RenderGeo -.->|"binds"| THS
    end
    
    RenderEngine --> CompileGeo
    RenderEngine --> LoadTex
    RenderEngine --> RenderGeo
```

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:1-239]()

### Geometry Compilation

When RmlUi needs static geometry (e.g., for document backgrounds):

```cpp
Rml::CompiledGeometryHandle CompileGeometry(
    Rml::Span<const Rml::Vertex> vertices,
    Rml::Span<const int> indices
);
```

**Process:**
1. Creates vertex buffer with `RGL::BufferUsage::VertexBuffer`
2. Creates index buffer with `RGL::BufferUsage::IndexBuffer`
3. Uploads data via `SetBufferData()` (Vulkan) or transient buffer copy (D3D12)
4. Wraps buffers in `CompiledGeoStruct` with index count
5. Returns opaque handle as `reinterpret_cast<Rml::CompiledGeometryHandle>`

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:77-134]()

### Geometry Rendering

```cpp
void RenderGeometry(
    Rml::CompiledGeometryHandle geometry,
    Rml::Vector2f translation,
    Rml::TextureHandle texture
);
```

**Rendering Steps:**
1. Casts handle back to `CompiledGeoStruct*`
2. Retrieves texture or uses `Texture::Manager::defaultTexture`
3. Binds `guiRenderPipeline`
4. Sets scissor region if enabled
5. Constructs `GUIUBO` with transform matrix and projection
6. Binds vertex/index buffers
7. Sets vertex shader uniform (push constants)
8. Binds texture sampler and texture view
9. Issues `DrawIndexed(nindices)` call

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:136-168]()

### GUI Shader Pipeline

The GUI uses dedicated shaders with orthographic projection:

| Shader | Inputs | Outputs | Purpose |
|--------|--------|---------|---------|
| **gui.vsh** | `a_position`, `a_color0`, `a_texcoord0` | `v_color0`, `v_texcoord0` | Transforms vertices to clip space |
| **gui.fsh** | `v_color0`, `v_texcoord0` | `outcolor` | Samples texture and multiplies by vertex color |

**Uniform Buffer Structure (Push Constants):**

```cpp
struct GUIUBO {
    matrix4 transform;    // Document-space transform
    matrix4 projection;   // Orthographic projection
    vector2 translation;  // Pixel-space offset
};
```

**Sources:** [shaders/gui.vsh:1-26](), [shaders/gui.fsh:1-14](), [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:152-158]()

### Transform Matrix Construction

The `make_gui_matrix()` function constructs document transforms:

```cpp
matrix4 make_gui_matrix(Rml::Vector2f translation);
```

**Transformation sequence:**
1. Start with identity matrix
2. Apply Y-flip: `scale(1, -1, 1)`
3. Scale to view space: `scale(1/(width/2), 1/(height/2), 1)`
4. Translate to origin-center: `translate(-width/2, -height/2, 0)`
5. Apply pixel-space translation: `translate(translation.x, translation.y, 0)`

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:42-50]()

### Texture Loading

RmlUi requests textures via two paths:

**From VFS (images referenced in RML/RCSS):**
```cpp
Rml::TextureHandle LoadTexture(
    Rml::Vector2i& texture_dimensions,
    const Rml::String& source
);
```

Process:
1. Loads file from VFS using `GetApp()->GetResources().FileContentsAt()`
2. Decodes using **stb_image** (`stbi_load_from_memory`)
3. Creates texture via `createTexture()` helper
4. Returns handle as `TextureHandleStruct*`

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:190-211]()

**Procedurally generated:**
```cpp
Rml::TextureHandle GenerateTexture(
    Rml::Span<const Rml::byte> source,
    Rml::Vector2i source_dimensions
);
```

Directly uploads provided pixel data without decoding.

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:213-216]()

### Scissor Clipping

RmlUi uses scissor regions to clip content:

```cpp
void EnableScissorRegion(bool enable);
void SetScissorRegion(Rml::Rectanglei region);
```

The `RMLScissor` state tracks enabled status and rectangle bounds, applied before each draw call.

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:177-187]()

---

## Font Loading

Fonts are loaded globally at application startup and remain available to all contexts:

```cpp
static bool LoadFont(const std::string& filename);
```

**Automatic Loading:** The `App` constructor iterates `/fonts/` directory and loads all `.ttf` files:

```cpp
App::Resources->IterateDirectory("fonts", [](const std::string& filename) {
    auto p = Filesystem::Path(filename);
    if (p.extension() == ".ttf") {
        GUIComponent::LoadFont(p.filename().string());
    }
});
```

Fonts are accessed in RCSS via the `font-family` property using the filename without extension.

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:90-94](), [src/App_priv.hpp:208-214]()

---

## Integration with Application

### Initialization

RmlUi is initialized in `App::run()`:

```cpp
Rml::SetSystemInterface(&rmlSystemInterface);
Rml::SetRenderInterface(&GetRenderEngine());
Rml::SetFileInterface(new VFSInterface());
Rml::Initialise();
```

**System interfaces:**
- **`RMLSystemInterface`**: Provides time and logging
- **`RenderEngine`**: Implements `Rml::RenderInterface` for rendering
- **`VFSInterface`**: Implements `Rml::FileInterface` for VFS access

**Sources:** [src/App_priv.hpp:194-198]()

### Per-Frame Update

During `App::Tick()`, all worlds are filtered for `GUIComponent`s:

```cpp
world->Filter([=](GUIComponent& gui) {
    if (gui.Mode == GUIComponent::RenderMode::Screenspace) {
        gui.SetDimensions(windowSize.width, windowSize.height);
        gui.SetDPIScale(scale);
    }
    gui.Update();
});
```

This:
1. Updates screenspace GUIs to match window dimensions
2. Applies DPI scaling for high-resolution displays
3. Calls `Update()` to process queued tasks and recalculate layout

**Sources:** [src/App_priv.hpp:380-387]()

### Rendering

GUI rendering occurs during the rendering pipeline after all 3D passes:

```mermaid
graph TD
    Start["RenderEngine::Draw()"]
    Pass1["Pass 1-6:<br/>3D Rendering"]
    Pass7["Pass 7: GUI Rendering"]
    Pass8["Pass 8: Debug Rendering"]
    End["Submit Command Buffer"]
    
    Start --> Pass1
    Pass1 --> Pass7
    Pass7 --> Pass8
    Pass8 --> End
    
    Pass7 -->|"for each GUIComponent"| RenderGUI["gui.Render()<br/>context->Render()"]
    RenderGUI -->|"RmlUi callbacks"| CompileGeo["CompileGeometry"]
    RenderGUI -->|"RmlUi callbacks"| RenderGeo["RenderGeometry"]
```

Each `GUIComponent::Render()` calls `context->Render()`, which invokes the `RenderEngine` implementation of `Rml::RenderInterface` to issue GPU commands.

**Sources:** Diagram 3 in architecture overview, [src/GUI.cpp:119-125]()

---

## DPI Scaling

High-DPI displays require scaling to maintain consistent UI sizes:

```cpp
void SetDPIScale(float scale);
```

This calls `context->SetDensityIndependentPixelRatio(scale)`, which:
- Scales all pixel values by the ratio
- Adjusts font rendering sizes
- Maintains logical dimensions while increasing physical resolution

The scale is retrieved from the OS via `window->GetDPIScale()` and updated on window resize events.

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:136-138](), [src/App_priv.hpp:309-313]()

---

## Practical Usage Example

### Creating a Menu System

```cpp
// Create GUI component attached to an entity
auto menuEntity = world.Instantiate<GUIComponent>();
auto& gui = menuEntity.GetComponent<GUIComponent>();

// Load the main menu document
gui.AddDocument("main_menu.rml");

// Bind input (assuming InputManager is configured)
inputManager->BindAxis("MouseX", &gui, &GUIComponent::MouseX, CID::C0);
inputManager->BindAxis("MouseY", &gui, &GUIComponent::MouseY, CID::C0);
inputManager->BindAxis("ScrollY", &gui, &GUIComponent::ScrollY, CID::C0);

// Register for keyboard/mouse button input
inputManager->BindAnyAction(gui.GetData());

// Update UI from game logic
gui.EnqueueUIUpdate([&gui] {
    auto* doc = gui.GetDocument("main_menu.rml");
    auto* element = doc->GetElementById("score");
    element->SetInnerRML(std::to_string(currentScore));
});
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:104-145](), [src/GUI.cpp:53-72]()

### Document Structure

**File: `/uis/main_menu.rml`**
```xml
<rml>
<head>
    <link type="text/rcss" href="/uis/main_menu.rcss"/>
</head>
<body>
    <div id="menu">
        <h1>Main Menu</h1>
        <button id="start">Start Game</button>
        <button id="options">Options</button>
        <button id="quit">Quit</button>
    </div>
</body>
</rml>
```

**File: `/uis/main_menu.rcss`**
```css
body {
    font-family: LatoLatin;
    font-size: 16dp;
    color: white;
}

#menu {
    width: 300dp;
    height: 400dp;
    margin: auto;
}

button {
    display: block;
    width: 100%;
    padding: 10dp;
    margin: 5dp 0;
}
```

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:53-72]()

## Memory Management

### Resource Cleanup

RmlUi resources are managed through handle-based garbage collection:

- **Compiled Geometry**: Enqueued for deletion via `ReleaseGeometry()` â†’ `gcBuffers.enqueue()`
- **Textures**: Enqueued for deletion via `ReleaseTexture()` â†’ `gcTextures.enqueue()`
- **Documents**: Automatically unloaded in `~GUIData()` destructor

The `RenderEngine` processes garbage collection queues each frame to safely delete GPU resources after they're no longer in use.

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_RML.cpp:170-222](), [src/GUI.cpp:148-153]()

### Context Destruction

When a `GUIComponent` is destroyed:
1. `~GUIData()` unloads all documents via `context->UnloadDocument()`
2. Context removed from RmlUi via `Rml::RemoveContext(context->GetName())`
3. Shared pointer reference counting handles `GUIData` deletion

**Sources:** [src/GUI.cpp:148-153]()

---

## Limitations and Considerations

| Aspect | Limitation | Workaround |
|--------|-----------|------------|
| **Worldspace Rendering** | Not fully implemented | Use screenspace and project to screen coordinates |
| **Thread Safety** | Must use `EnqueueUIUpdate` | Always capture by value in lambdas |
| **Font Loading** | Must be TTF format | Convert fonts before packaging |
| **Texture Formats** | Limited to RGBA8_Unorm | Pre-convert textures if needed |
| **Input Forwarding** | Manual axis binding required | Bind in application setup |

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/GUI.hpp:78-81]()
