## Purpose and Scope

This page documents RavEngine's debug rendering capabilities, which provide immediate-mode drawing primitives and navigation mesh visualization for development and debugging purposes. Debug rendering enables developers to visualize collision shapes, navigation paths, bounding volumes, and other diagnostic information overlaid on the rendered scene.

For interactive GUI components, see [GUI Components and RmlUi](#8.1). For general rendering architecture, see [Rendering Architecture](#4.1).

---

## Overview

RavEngine integrates two specialized debug visualization systems:

1. **Im3d** - Immediate-mode debug drawing library for geometric primitives (lines, points, triangles)
2. **Recast/Detour** - Navigation mesh visualization via the `duDebugDraw` interface

Both systems render in **Pass 8** of the frame pipeline, after GUI rendering, ensuring debug visualizations appear on top of all other content. Debug rendering is conditionally compiled and disabled in release builds for zero runtime overhead.

---

## Architecture

### Debug Rendering System Components

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "External Libraries"
        Im3d["Im3d<br/>Immediate-Mode Debug Drawing"]
        Recast["Recast/Detour<br/>Navigation Mesh Debugging"]
    end
    
    subgraph "RenderEngine Integration"
        DebugRender["RenderEngine::DebugRender()<br/>Im3d DrawList Processing"]
        duDebugImpl["duDebugDraw Interface<br/>depthMask/begin/vertex/end"]
        
        subgraph "Debug Pipelines"
            Im3dLine["im3dLineRenderPipeline"]
            Im3dPoint["im3dPointRenderPipeline"]
            Im3dTri["im3dTriangleRenderPipeline"]
            RecastLine["recastLinePipeline"]
            RecastPoint["recastPointPipeline"]
            RecastTri["recastTrianglePipeline"]
        end
    end
    
    subgraph "GPU Resources"
        DebugShaders["debug_vsh / debug_fsh<br/>Vertex & Fragment Shaders"]
        DebugUBO["DebugUBO<br/>viewProj matrix"]
        NavUBO["navDebugUBO<br/>model & viewProj matrices"]
        DebugBuffer["debugRenderBufferUpload<br/>Vertex Upload Buffer"]
    end
    
    Im3d --> DebugRender
    Recast --> duDebugImpl
    
    DebugRender --> Im3dLine
    DebugRender --> Im3dPoint
    DebugRender --> Im3dTri
    
    duDebugImpl --> RecastLine
    duDebugImpl --> RecastPoint
    duDebugImpl --> RecastTri

    Im3dTri --> DebugShaders
    RecastLine --> DebugShaders
    RecastPoint --> DebugShaders
    RecastTri --> DebugShaders
    
    DebugShaders --> DebugUBO
    DebugShaders --> NavUBO
    
    DebugRender --> DebugBuffer
    duDebugImpl --> DebugBuffer
```

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine.cpp:848-919](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:63](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:80-81](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:295-305]()

---

## Im3d Integration

### Overview

Im3d provides an immediate-mode API for debug drawing, allowing applications to submit lines, points, and triangles for visualization. Each frame, Im3d accumulates submitted geometry into a `DrawList`, which `RenderEngine::DebugRender()` processes and renders.

### Im3d Rendering Flow

```mermaid
graph LR
    App["Application Code<br/>Im3d API calls"]
    DrawList["Im3d::DrawList<br/>Accumulated Geometry"]
    ProcessList["RenderEngine::DebugRender()<br/>Process DrawList"]
    
    subgraph "Pipeline Selection by Primitive Type"
        SelectPipe{Primitive<br/>Type?}
        LinePipe["im3dLineRenderPipeline<br/>Topology: LineList"]
        PointPipe["im3dPointRenderPipeline<br/>Topology: PointList"]
        TriPipe["im3dTriangleRenderPipeline<br/>Topology: TriangleList"]
    end
    
    Upload["Upload to<br/>debugRenderBufferUpload"]
    Draw["Draw Call"]
    
    App --> DrawList
    DrawList --> ProcessList
    ProcessList --> SelectPipe
    
    SelectPipe -->|Lines| LinePipe
    SelectPipe -->|Points| PointPipe
    SelectPipe -->|Triangles| TriPipe
    
    LinePipe --> Upload
    PointPipe --> Upload
    TriPipe --> Upload
    
    Upload --> Draw
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:305](), [src/RenderEngine.cpp:916-918]()

### Im3d Vertex Layout

Im3d geometry uses the `Im3d::VertexData` structure:

| Attribute | Location | Format | Description |
|-----------|----------|--------|-------------|
| Position | 0 | R32G32B32A32_SignedFloat | Vertex position (vec4) |
| Color | 1 | R32_Uint | Packed RGBA color (uint32) |

The vertex layout is configured during pipeline creation:

- **Vertex Binding**: Binding 0, stride `sizeof(Im3d::VertexData)`
- **Attribute Offsets**: Position at offset 0, Color at offset `sizeof(glm::vec4)`

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine.cpp:863-882]()

### Im3d Pipeline Configuration

All three Im3d pipelines share common configuration:

| Property | Value |
|----------|-------|
| Vertex Shader | `debug_vsh` |
| Fragment Shader | `debug_fsh` |
| Winding Order | Counterclockwise |
| Depth Test | Disabled |
| Depth Write | Disabled |
| Depth Function | Greater |
| Color Attachment Format | BGRA8_Unorm |
| Blending | Disabled |

The pipelines differ only in primitive topology and polygon override:

```cpp
im3dLineRenderPipeline = createDebugRenderPipeline(
    RGL::PolygonOverride::Line, 
    RGL::PrimitiveTopology::LineList
);
im3dPointRenderPipeline = createDebugRenderPipeline(
    RGL::PolygonOverride::Point, 
    RGL::PrimitiveTopology::PointList
);
im3dTriangleRenderPipeline = createDebugRenderPipeline(
    RGL::PolygonOverride::Fill, 
    RGL::PrimitiveTopology::TriangleList
);
```

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine.cpp:851-918]()

---

## Recast/Detour Debug Visualization

### duDebugDraw Interface Implementation

The `RenderEngine` class implements the `duDebugDraw` interface from Recast/Detour, enabling navigation mesh visualization. This interface provides a primitive-based drawing API similar to legacy immediate-mode OpenGL.

### duDebugDraw Method Sequence

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Nav as "Navigation System"
    participant RE as "RenderEngine<br/>(duDebugDraw)"
    participant Buf as "debugRenderBufferUpload"
    participant GPU as "GPU Command Buffer"
    
    Nav->>RE: depthMask(bool state)
    Note over RE: Set navDebugDepthEnabled flag
    
    Nav->>RE: texture(bool state)
    Note over RE: Currently unused
    
    Nav->>RE: begin(primitive_type, size)
    Note over RE: Store primitive type<br/>Prepare for vertex data
    
    loop For each vertex in primitive
        Nav->>RE: vertex(pos, color, uv)
        Note over RE: Accumulate vertex data
        RE->>Buf: Append to upload buffer
    end
    
    Nav->>RE: end()
    Note over RE: Finalize primitive batch
    RE->>RE: Select pipeline by primitive type
    RE->>GPU: Encode draw call
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:295-303]()

### duDebugDraw Methods

The `RenderEngine` implements the following `duDebugDraw` interface methods:

| Method | Parameters | Purpose |
|--------|------------|---------|
| `depthMask()` | `bool state` | Enable/disable depth testing |
| `texture()` | `bool state` | Enable/disable texturing (unused) |
| `begin()` | `duDebugDrawPrimitives prim, float size` | Start primitive batch |
| `vertex()` | `const float* pos, unsigned int color` | Add vertex with position and color |
| `vertex()` | `float x, y, z, unsigned int color` | Add vertex (overload) |
| `vertex()` | `const float* pos, unsigned int color, const float* uv` | Add vertex with UVs |
| `vertex()` | `float x, y, z, unsigned int color, float u, v` | Add vertex with UVs (overload) |
| `end()` | None | Finalize and render primitive batch |

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:295-303]()

### Navigation Debug State

The `RenderEngine` maintains navigation-specific debug rendering state:

**navDebugUBO Structure:**
```cpp
struct navDebugUBO {
    glm::mat4 model;      // Model transformation
    glm::mat4 viewProj;   // View-projection matrix
} currentNavState;
```

**Depth Control:**
- `navDebugDepthEnabled` (bool) - Controls depth testing during navigation debug rendering

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:160-163](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:348]()

### Recast Pipeline Selection

Recast/Detour supports three primitive types, each mapped to a dedicated pipeline:

```mermaid
graph TD
    Begin["duDebugDraw::begin(prim)"]
    
    subgraph "Primitive Type Determination"
        Check{prim value}
        Lines["DU_DRAW_LINES"]
        Points["DU_DRAW_POINTS"]
        Tris["DU_DRAW_TRIS"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Pipeline Selection"
        LinePipe["recastLinePipeline<br/>LineList topology"]
        PointPipe["recastPointPipeline<br/>PointList topology"]
        TriPipe["recastTrianglePipeline<br/>TriangleList topology"]
    end
    
    Accumulate["Accumulate vertices<br/>in debug buffer"]
    
    Begin --> Check
    Check --> Lines
    Check --> Points
    Check --> Tris
    
    Lines --> LinePipe
    Points --> PointPipe
    Tris --> TriPipe
    
    LinePipe --> Accumulate
    PointPipe --> Accumulate
    TriPipe --> Accumulate
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:295-303]()

## Debug Rendering in Frame Pipeline

Debug rendering executes as the final rendering pass (Pass 8) in the multi-pass rendering pipeline, ensuring debug visualizations appear on top of all other content.

### Frame Pipeline Integration

```mermaid
graph TD
    Pass6["Pass 6: Post-Processing<br/>Bloom/DOF/Motion Blur"]
    Tonemap["Tonemap HDR to LDR"]
    Pass7["Pass 7: GUI Rendering<br/>RmlUi contexts"]
    
    Pass8["Pass 8: Debug Rendering"]
    
    subgraph "Debug Rendering Pass"
        Im3dDebug["Render Im3d DrawLists<br/>RenderEngine::DebugRender()"]
        RecastDebug["Render Recast Geometry<br/>duDebugDraw accumulated data"]
    end
    
    Submit["Submit Command Buffer<br/>to GPU Queue"]
    
    Pass6 --> Tonemap
    Tonemap --> Pass7
    Pass7 --> Pass8
    
    Pass8 --> Im3dDebug
    Pass8 --> RecastDebug
    
    Im3dDebug --> Submit
    RecastDebug --> Submit
```

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:49-51]()

## Shader Uniforms and Push Constants

### DebugUBO Structure

The primary uniform structure for debug rendering contains only the view-projection matrix:

```cpp
struct DebugUBO {
    glm::mat4 viewProj;
};
```

**Push Constant Configuration:**
- **Size:** `sizeof(DebugUBO)` bytes
- **Offset:** 0
- **Stage Visibility:** Vertex | Fragment

This push constant is used by both Im3d and Recast rendering when no model matrix is needed.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:174-176](), [src/RenderEngine.cpp:686-692]()

### navDebugUBO Structure

For navigation-specific debug rendering requiring model transformations:

```cpp
struct navDebugUBO {
    glm::mat4 model;      // Model transformation matrix
    glm::mat4 viewProj;   // View-projection matrix
};
```

The `RenderEngine::currentNavState` member stores the current navigation debug state, which is updated as needed during Recast debug rendering.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:160-163]()

---

## Debug Buffer Management

### Upload Buffer State

Debug vertex data is uploaded via a dynamically-sized buffer:

| Member | Type | Purpose |
|--------|------|---------|
| `debugRenderBufferUpload` | `RGLBufferPtr` | GPU buffer for debug vertex uploads |
| `debugRenderBufferSize` | `uint32_t` | Current allocated buffer size in bytes |
| `debugRenderBufferOffset` | `uint32_t` | Current write offset into buffer |

The buffer grows as needed to accommodate debug geometry but never shrinks, as debug rendering is expected to have variable but bounded memory requirements.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:84-85]()

### Buffer Upload Pattern

```mermaid
graph LR
    Vertices["Debug Vertex Data"]
    CheckSize{Size fits<br/>in buffer?}
    Grow["Reallocate larger buffer<br/>Update debugRenderBufferSize"]
    Append["Append data at offset<br/>Increment debugRenderBufferOffset"]
    
    Vertices --> CheckSize
    CheckSize -->|No| Grow
    CheckSize -->|Yes| Append
    Grow --> Append
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:84-85]()

---

## Pipeline Initialization

Debug render pipelines are created during `RenderEngine` construction, but only in debug builds.

### Debug Build Conditional Compilation

```cpp
#ifndef NDEBUG
    auto debugVSH = LoadShaderByFilename("debug_vsh", device);
    auto debugFSH = LoadShaderByFilename("debug_fsh", device);
    
    // Create Im3d pipelines
    im3dLineRenderPipeline = createDebugRenderPipeline(
        RGL::PolygonOverride::Line, 
        RGL::PrimitiveTopology::LineList
    );
    // ... point and triangle pipelines
#endif
```

In **release builds** (when `NDEBUG` is defined), the debug rendering code is completely removed, resulting in:
- Zero memory allocation for debug pipelines
- No debug shader compilation
- No debug buffer creation
- Eliminated runtime overhead

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine.cpp:848]()

### createDebugRenderPipeline Lambda

The pipeline creation uses a lambda to reduce code duplication:

```cpp
auto createDebugRenderPipeline = [this, debugVSH, debugFSH, debugPipelineLayout, device](
    RGL::PolygonOverride drawMode, 
    RGL::PrimitiveTopology topology
) {
    RGL::RenderPipelineDescriptor rpd{
        .stages = {
            {.type = RGL::ShaderStageDesc::Type::Vertex, .shaderModule = debugVSH},
            {.type = RGL::ShaderStageDesc::Type::Fragment, .shaderModule = debugFSH}
        },
        .vertexConfig = { /* Im3d::VertexData layout */ },
        .inputAssembly = {.topology = topology},
        .viewport = {.width = 640, .height = 480},
        .rasterizerConfig = {
            .polygonOverride = drawMode,
            .windingOrder = RGL::WindingOrder::Counterclockwise
        },
        .depthStencilConfig = {
            .depthFormat = depthFormat,
            .depthTestEnabled = false,
            .depthWriteEnabled = false,
            .depthFunction = RGL::DepthCompareFunction::Greater
        },
        .pipelineLayout = debugPipelineLayout
    };
    return device->CreateRenderPipeline(rpd);
};
```

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine.cpp:851-919]()

---

## RenderEngine Multiple Interface Implementation

The `RenderEngine` class implements multiple interfaces to centralize rendering responsibilities:

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class RenderEngine {
        +DebugRender(Im3d::DrawList)
        +depthMask(bool state)
        +texture(bool state)
        +begin(duDebugDrawPrimitives prim, float size)
        +vertex(const float* pos, uint color)
        +vertex(float x, y, z, uint color)
        +vertex(const float* pos, uint color, const float* uv)
        +vertex(float x, y, z, uint color, float u, v)
        +end()
        -im3dLineRenderPipeline : RGLRenderPipelinePtr
        -im3dPointRenderPipeline : RGLRenderPipelinePtr
        -im3dTriangleRenderPipeline : RGLRenderPipelinePtr
        -recastLinePipeline : RGLRenderPipelinePtr
        -recastPointPipeline : RGLRenderPipelinePtr
        -recastTrianglePipeline : RGLRenderPipelinePtr
        -debugRenderBufferUpload : RGLBufferPtr
        -debugRenderBufferSize : uint32_t
        -debugRenderBufferOffset : uint32_t
        -navDebugDepthEnabled : bool
        -currentNavState : navDebugUBO
    }
    
    class duDebugDraw {
        <<interface>>
        +depthMask(bool)*
        +texture(bool)*
        +begin(prim, size)*
        +vertex(...)*
        +end()*
    }
    
    class RmlRenderInterface {
        <<interface>>
        +CompileGeometry(...)*
        +RenderGeometry(...)*
        +ReleaseGeometry(...)*
    }
    
    RenderEngine --|> duDebugDraw : implements
    RenderEngine --|> RmlRenderInterface : implements
```

This multi-interface design allows `RenderEngine` to serve as:
1. **Rml::RenderInterface** - GUI rendering backend (see [GUI Components and RmlUi](#8.1))
2. **duDebugDraw** - Recast/Detour navigation debug interface
3. **Im3d processor** - Via the `DebugRender()` method

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:63](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:295-305]()

---

## Debug Rendering Order

Debug geometry renders **last** to ensure it appears on top of all other content:

1. **Depth Prepass** - Early depth/normal writes
2. **Shadow Mapping** - Directional/Point/Spot light shadows
3. **Main Opaque Pass** - PBR/Unlit materials
4. **Skybox** - Environment rendering
5. **Transparent Pass** - Order-independent transparency
6. **Post-Processing** - SSAO/GTAO, SSGI, bloom, DOF
7. **Tonemapping** - HDR to LDR conversion
8. **GUI Rendering** - RmlUi contexts
9. **Debug Rendering** - Im3d + Recast/Detour â† Final pass

This ordering ensures debug visualizations are never occluded by scene geometry and remain visible for debugging purposes.

**Sources:** Based on the multi-pass rendering pipeline architecture

---

## Usage Patterns

### Im3d Immediate-Mode Drawing

Applications using Im3d for debug visualization should:

1. **Each Frame:** Call Im3d API to submit debug primitives
   ```cpp
   Im3d::DrawLine(start, end, color);
   Im3d::DrawSphere(center, radius, color);
   ```

2. **Im3d Accumulation:** Im3d internally accumulates geometry into a `DrawList`

3. **Render Integration:** Pass the `DrawList` to RenderEngine
   ```cpp
   renderEngine.DebugRender(Im3d::GetDrawLists()[0]);
   ```

4. **Pipeline Selection:** RenderEngine automatically selects the appropriate pipeline based on primitive type

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:305]()

### Recast/Detour Navigation Debugging

Navigation systems using Recast/Detour visualization should:

1. **Obtain Interface:** Get `RenderEngine` instance as `duDebugDraw*`
   ```cpp
   duDebugDraw* dd = &renderEngine;
   ```

2. **Begin Primitive:** Call `begin()` with primitive type
   ```cpp
   dd->begin(DU_DRAW_LINES, 2.0f);
   ```

3. **Submit Vertices:** Add vertices via `vertex()` calls
   ```cpp
   dd->vertex(x1, y1, z1, color);
   dd->vertex(x2, y2, z2, color);
   ```

4. **Finalize:** Call `end()` to render the batch
   ```cpp
   dd->end();
   ```

5. **Optional Depth Control:** Use `depthMask()` to control depth testing
   ```cpp
   dd->depthMask(false); // Disable depth test
   ```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:295-303]()

---

## Performance Considerations

Debug rendering is designed exclusively for **development and debugging**:

### Optimization Strategy

| Aspect | Development Build | Release Build |
|--------|------------------|---------------|
| Pipeline Creation | All 6 debug pipelines created | **Zero pipelines created** |
| Shader Compilation | `debug_vsh`, `debug_fsh` compiled | **Shaders not compiled** |
| Memory Allocation | Debug buffer allocated and grows | **No debug buffer** |
| Runtime Overhead | Minimal (last pass, small geometry) | **Zero overhead** |
| Code Size | Debug code included | **Debug code removed** |

### Key Performance Characteristics

- **Immediate Mode:** Debug geometry is not cached; submitted and rendered each frame
- **Final Pass:** Renders after all other content, potentially introducing GPU stalls
- **Buffer Growth:** Upload buffer grows to accommodate geometry but never shrinks
- **Conditional Compilation:** Entire debug system removed in release builds via `#ifndef NDEBUG`

### Recommendations

1. **Development Only:** Use debug rendering only in debug builds
2. **Minimize Geometry:** Submit only necessary debug primitives
3. **Release Builds:** Define `NDEBUG` to eliminate all debug rendering overhead
4. **Profiling:** Debug rendering appears as "Pass 8" in GPU profilers

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine.cpp:848](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:84-85]()38:T4b6d,# Advanced Topics

This section covers advanced internal systems and architectural patterns within RavEngine that are primarily relevant to engine developers, contributors, and users who need deep understanding of the implementation. These topics explain the low-level mechanisms that power RavEngine's rendering, build system, and data management.

For application-level rendering concepts, see [Rendering](#4). For physics simulation details, see [Physics](#5). For animation implementation, see [Animation](#6).

## Overview of Advanced Systems

RavEngine's architecture is built on several sophisticated subsystems that enable cross-platform operation, high performance, and developer productivity:

1. **RGL (RavEngine Graphics Library)** - A low-level graphics API abstraction layer that unifies Vulkan, DirectX 12, and Metal under a single interface
2. **GPU-Driven Rendering** - Compute shader-based culling, indirect draw commands, and GPU resource management to minimize CPU overhead
3. **Render Data Synchronization** - Double-buffered VRAM data structures that enable lock-free parallel updates from gameplay code
4. **Cross-Compilation Infrastructure** - CMake-based build system that supports building host tools separately from target platform binaries
5. **Memory Management** - Custom allocators for mesh data, texture resources, and GPU buffers with automatic defragmentation

These systems work together to provide RavEngine's core capabilities across diverse hardware platforms while maintaining a unified codebase.

**Sources:** [src/RenderEngine.hpp:1-365](), [CMakeLists.txt:1-700](), [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:1-500]()

---

## RGL Graphics Abstraction Layer

### Architecture Overview

RGL (RavEngine Graphics Library) provides a unified C++ interface over platform-specific graphics APIs. The abstraction layer consists of:

- **Core Interfaces**: `IDevice`, `ICommandQueue`, `ICommandBuffer`, `ITexture`, `IBuffer`, `IRenderPipeline`, `IComputePipeline`
- **Backend Implementations**: VkDevice, D3D12Device, MTLDevice (and their associated types)
- **Shader Compilation**: `rglc` tool for cross-compiling GLSL to SPIR-V, DXIL, and Metal bytecode

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "RGL Public API"
        Device["RGLDevicePtr<br/>IDevice"]
        CmdQueue["RGLCommandQueuePtr<br/>ICommandQueue"]
        CmdBuffer["RGLCommandBufferPtr<br/>ICommandBuffer"]
        RenderPipeline["RGLRenderPipelinePtr<br/>IRenderPipeline"]
        ComputePipeline["RGLComputePipelinePtr<br/>IComputePipeline"]
        Texture["RGLTexturePtr<br/>ITexture"]
        Buffer["RGLBufferPtr<br/>IBuffer"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Vulkan Backend"
        VkDevice["DeviceVk"]
        VkCmdQueue["CommandQueueVk"]
        VkCmdBuffer["CommandBufferVk"]
        VkPipeline["RenderPipelineVk"]
        VkTexture["TextureVk"]
        VkBuffer["BufferVk"]
    end
    
    subgraph "DirectX 12 Backend"
        D3D12Device["DeviceD3D12"]
        D3D12CmdQueue["CommandQueueD3D12"]
        D3D12CmdBuffer["CommandBufferD3D12"]
        D3D12Pipeline["RenderPipelineD3D12"]
        D3D12Texture["TextureD3D12"]
        D3D12Buffer["BufferD3D12"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Metal Backend"
        MTLDevice["DeviceMTL"]
        MTLCmdQueue["CommandQueueMTL"]
        MTLCmdBuffer["CommandBufferMTL"]
        MTLPipeline["RenderPipelineMTL"]
        MTLTexture["TextureMTL"]
        MTLBuffer["BufferMTL"]
    end
    
    Device -.->|implements| VkDevice
    Device -.->|implements| D3D12Device
    Device -.->|implements| MTLDevice
    
    CmdQueue -.->|implements| VkCmdQueue
    CmdQueue -.->|implements| D3D12CmdQueue
    CmdQueue -.->|implements| MTLCmdQueue
    
    CmdBuffer -.->|implements| VkCmdBuffer
    CmdBuffer -.->|implements| D3D12CmdBuffer
    CmdBuffer -.->|implements| MTLCmdBuffer
    
    RenderPipeline -.->|implements| VkPipeline
    RenderPipeline -.->|implements| D3D12Pipeline
    RenderPipeline -.->|implements| MTLPipeline
    
    Texture -.->|implements| VkTexture
    Texture -.->|implements| D3D12Texture
    Texture -.->|implements| MTLTexture
    
    Buffer -.->|implements| VkBuffer
    Buffer -.->|implements| D3D12Buffer
    Buffer -.->|implements| MTLBuffer
```

### Command Buffer State Tracking

Each backend's command buffer implementation tracks resource states to automatically insert synchronization barriers. For example, `CommandBufferVk` maintains `activeTextures` and `activeBuffers` maps to record how resources are accessed:

- **Texture State Tracking**: Maps `TextureLastUseKey` (texture pointer + covered mips + covered layers) to `TextureLastUse` (VkImageLayout + write flag)
- **Buffer State Tracking**: Maps `BufferVk*` to `BufferLastUse` (write flag)

When a command buffer ends, it transitions all resources back to their native states. This is visible in [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:52-85]() and [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:52-95]().

**Sources:** [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.hpp:1-280](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.hpp:1-180](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.hpp:1-120](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:63-250]()

---

## GPU-Driven Rendering Architecture

### Compute Shader Culling Pipeline

RavEngine performs frustum culling, occlusion culling, and LOD selection entirely on the GPU using compute shaders. The `defaultcull.csh` shader processes objects in parallel, writing visible instances to indirect draw buffers.

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "CPU Preparation"
        CUBO["CUBO Structures<br/>(per material batch)"]
        ModelMatrices["Model Matrix Buffer<br/>(worldTransforms)"]
        RenderLayers["Render Layer Buffer<br/>(per entity)"]
        PerObjectFlags["Per-Object Flags<br/>(culling settings)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "GPU Culling Pass"
        CullShader["defaultcull.csh<br/>Compute Shader"]
        DepthPyramid["Depth Pyramid Texture<br/>(hierarchical Z-buffer)"]
        
        CullShader -->|reads| CUBO
        CullShader -->|reads| ModelMatrices
        CullShader -->|reads| RenderLayers
        CullShader -->|reads| PerObjectFlags
        CullShader -->|samples| DepthPyramid
    end
    
    subgraph "GPU Output"
        IndirectBuffer["Indirect Draw Buffer<br/>(RGL::IndirectIndexedCommand)"]
        CulledIDs["Visible Entity IDs"]
        
        CullShader -->|writes| IndirectBuffer
        CullShader -->|writes| CulledIDs
    end
    
    subgraph "GPU Rendering"
        DrawCall["vkCmdDrawIndexedIndirect<br/>DrawIndexedInstancedIndirect<br/>drawIndexedPrimitives:indirect"]
        
        IndirectBuffer -->|consumed by| DrawCall
    end
```

### CUBO (Culling Uniform Buffer Object)

Each material batch has a `CUBO` structure containing:

- `indirectBufferOffset`: Where to write draw commands
- `numObjects`: Number of instances to cull
- `cullingBufferOffset`: Offset into culling output buffer
- `radius`: Bounding sphere radius for the mesh
- `numLODs`: Number of LOD levels available
- Bindless buffer handles for input/output data

This structure is defined in [shaders/defaultcull.csh:7-17]() and [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:212-222]().

### Occlusion Culling with Depth Pyramid

The culling shader constructs a bounding box in clip space for each object and samples the depth pyramid at the appropriate mip level:

1. Project bounding sphere corners to clip space
2. Compute bounding box in NDC coordinates
3. Calculate required mip level based on screen-space size
4. Sample depth pyramid at the four corners of the bounding box
5. Compare object's depth against sampled values

This technique is implemented in [shaders/defaultcull.csh:108-270]().

**Sources:** [shaders/defaultcull.csh:1-280](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:1064-1140](), [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:212-240]()

---

## Render Data Synchronization System

### Double-Buffered VRAM Structures

RavEngine uses specialized data structures to synchronize gameplay state with GPU-visible buffers without blocking either the CPU or GPU. The core types are:

- `BufferedVRAMVector<T>`: Contiguous array synchronized to GPU memory
- `BufferedVRAMSparseSet<IndexT, ValueT>`: Sparse array with parallel GPU representation

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "CPU Side - Game Thread"
        HostData["Host Data<br/>(std::vector)"]
        DirtyFlags["Dirty Tracking<br/>(element changed flags)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Staging Buffers"
        StagingBuffer["Staging Buffer<br/>(RGL::BufferAccess::Shared)"]
        StagingAlloc["BufferPool Allocation<br/>(transient)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "GPU Side - Private Memory"
        PrivateBuffer["Private Buffer<br/>(RGL::BufferAccess::Private)"]
        GPUShaders["Vertex/Fragment/Compute Shaders<br/>(read-only access)"]
    end
    
    HostData -->|write when dirty| StagingBuffer
    StagingBuffer -->|vkCmdCopyBuffer<br/>CopyResource<br/>blitCommandEncoder| PrivateBuffer
    PrivateBuffer -->|bound as SSBO/CBV| GPUShaders
    
    DirtyFlags -.->|triggers| HostData
    StagingAlloc -.->|provides| StagingBuffer
```

### World::RenderData Structure

The `World` maintains a `RenderData` structure containing all GPU-visible representations:

- `worldTransforms`: `BufferedVRAMVector<matrix4>` indexed by entity ID
- `renderLayers`: `BufferedVRAMVector<renderlayer_t>` for layer filtering
- `perObjectAttributes`: `BufferedVRAMVector<perobject_t>` for per-object flags
- `directionalLightData`: `BufferedVRAMSparseSet<entity_id_t, DirLightUploadData>`
- `pointLightData`, `spotLightData`, `ambientLightData`: Similar sparse sets for lights
- `staticMeshRenderData`: `OrderedMap<MaterialSort, MDIICommand>` organizing draw calls by material
- `skinnedMeshRenderData`: Similar map for skinned meshes

This structure is defined in [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:419-449]().

### Synchronization Flow

The synchronization happens in the render task graph:

1. **Game Thread** modifies components (e.g., `Transform::SetPosition`)
2. **Dirty Tracking** marks affected entities
3. **Render Tasks** (parallel) write to host-side vectors
4. **EncodeSync** phase copies dirty ranges to staging buffers
5. **Transform Sync Command Buffer** issues copy commands to private GPU buffers
6. **Main Command Buffer** binds private buffers for rendering

The copy commands are encoded in [src/World.cpp:110-304]() and executed before the main render pass.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:419-449](), [src/World.cpp:110-304](), [include/RavEngine/VRAMSparseSet.hpp](), [include/RavEngine/BufferedVRAMVector.hpp]()

---

## Cross-Platform Build System

### Host Tools Architecture

RavEngine supports cross-compilation by building certain tools (shader compiler, mesh compiler, etc.) for the host platform separately from the target platform. This is managed through a dedicated `host-tools` subdirectory.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Build Configuration Detection"
        CMakeCheck{"CMAKE_CROSSCOMPILING<br/>or VS_CROSSCOMP?"}
    end
    
    subgraph "Host Tools Build"
        HostCMake["host-tools/CMakeLists.txt"]
        HostProtoc["protoc (host)"]
        HostRglc["rglc (host)"]
        HostFlatc["flatc (host)"]
        HostRvesc["rvesc (host)"]
        HostRvemc["rvemc (host)"]
        HostRveac["rveac (host)"]
        HostRveskc["rveskc (host)"]
        
        HostCMake --> HostProtoc
        HostCMake --> HostRglc
        HostCMake --> HostFlatc
        HostCMake --> HostRvesc
        HostCMake --> HostRvemc
        HostCMake --> HostRveac
        HostCMake --> HostRveskc
    end
    
    subgraph "Target Platform Build"
        TargetCMake["CMakeLists.txt"]
        TargetRavEngine["RavEngine (target)"]
        TargetApp["Application (target)"]
        AssetProcessing["Asset Processing<br/>(uses host tools)"]
        
        TargetCMake --> TargetRavEngine
        TargetCMake --> TargetApp
        TargetApp --> AssetProcessing
    end
    
    CMakeCheck -->|"Yes (cross-compiling)"| HostCMake
    CMakeCheck -->|"No (native build)"| TargetCMake
    
    HostProtoc -.->|"used by"| AssetProcessing
    HostRglc -.->|"used by"| AssetProcessing
    HostFlatc -.->|"used by"| AssetProcessing
    HostRvesc -.->|"used by"| AssetProcessing
    HostRvemc -.->|"used by"| AssetProcessing
    HostRveac -.->|"used by"| AssetProcessing
    HostRveskc -.->|"used by"| AssetProcessing
```

### Cross-Compilation Detection

The build system detects cross-compilation scenarios in [CMakeLists.txt:80-99]():

- **Visual Studio Cross-Compilation**: Detected when `CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME` differs from `CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME_DEFAULT`
- **CMake Cross-Compilation**: Standard `CMAKE_CROSSCOMPILING` flag
- Sets `RVE_CROSSCOMP` cache variable to control subsequent configuration

### Host Tools Execution

When cross-compiling, the build system:

1. Configures and builds `deps/host-tools/CMakeLists.txt` at configure time
2. Sets cached variables pointing to host tool executables (e.g., `RVESC_PATH`, `RVEMC_PATH`)
3. Uses these tools during the target build to process assets

The host tools configuration is invoked in [CMakeLists.txt:142-169](), which runs `cmake --build` to compile `protoc`, `rglc`, `flatc`, and the RavEngine-specific compilers.

### Shader Compilation Flow

On Apple platforms, shaders follow a different path:

- **Non-Apple**: Shaders compiled to SPIR-V/DXIL, embedded via `cmrc` (CMake Resource Compiler)
- **Apple**: Shaders compiled to Metal bytecode and packaged as `.metallib` files in the app bundle

This distinction is handled in [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:228-283](), where `metal_compile_shader` function generates `.air` intermediate files and links them into `.metallib` archives.

**Sources:** [CMakeLists.txt:80-180](), [deps/host-tools/CMakeLists.txt:1-80](), [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-350]()

## GPU Memory and Mesh Allocation

### Unified Mesh Buffer Strategy

RavEngine uses a single large vertex buffer and index buffer for all meshes, managed through free-list allocators. This approach minimizes draw call overhead and enables efficient GPU-driven rendering.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Mesh Allocation Request"
        MeshAsset["MeshAsset::Load"]
        AllocRequest["RenderEngine::AllocateMesh<br/>(MeshPartView)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Free List Allocator"
        VertexFreeList["vertexFreeList<br/>(allocation_freelist_t)"]
        IndexFreeList["indexFreeList<br/>(allocation_freelist_t)"]
        AllocatedList["vertexAllocatedList<br/>indexAllocatedList"]
        
        AllocRequest --> VertexFreeList
        AllocRequest --> IndexFreeList
        VertexFreeList --> AllocatedList
        IndexFreeList --> AllocatedList
    end
    
    subgraph "Shared GPU Buffers"
        SharedVB["sharedPositionBuffer<br/>sharedNormalBuffer<br/>sharedTangentBuffer<br/>etc."]
        SharedIB["sharedIndexBuffer"]
        
        AllocatedList -.->|"allocates range in"| SharedVB
        AllocatedList -.->|"allocates range in"| SharedIB
    end
    
    subgraph "Reallocation on Growth"
        GrowthCheck{"Buffer full?"}
        Realloc["ReallocateGeneric<br/>(powers of 2)"]
        
        AllocRequest --> GrowthCheck
        GrowthCheck -->|"Yes"| Realloc
        Realloc --> SharedVB
        Realloc --> SharedIB
    end
    
    subgraph "Mesh Deallocation"
        DeallocRequest["RenderEngine::DeallocateMesh<br/>(MeshRange)"]
        ReturnToFreeList["Return range to free lists"]
        
        DeallocRequest --> ReturnToFreeList
        ReturnToFreeList --> VertexFreeList
        ReturnToFreeList --> IndexFreeList
    end
```

### Allocation Implementation

The allocation system is implemented in [src/RenderEngine.cpp:1061-1062]() with initial sizes:

- `initialVerts = 1024`
- `initialIndices = 1536`

When a mesh requests allocation via `RenderEngine::AllocateMesh`, the system:

1. Searches `vertexFreeList` for a contiguous range of the required size
2. Searches `indexFreeList` similarly
3. If no suitable range exists, triggers buffer reallocation (doubling size)
4. Returns a `MeshRange` containing vertex/index offsets and sizes

Deallocation (`RenderEngine::DeallocateMesh`) returns ranges to the free lists and coalesces adjacent free regions.

### Skinned Mesh Buffer Management

Skinned meshes use separate dynamic buffers since vertices are transformed each frame:

- `sharedSkinnedPositionBuffer`, `sharedSkinnedNormalBuffer`, etc.: Written by skinning compute shader
- `sharedSkeletonMatrixBuffer`: Contains bone transformation matrices (CPU-uploaded)

The skinning compute pipeline is dispatched in [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:577-630](), reading from static mesh data and writing to dynamic skinned buffers.

### Transient Buffer for Per-Frame Data

RavEngine provides a 32MB transient buffer for small per-frame uploads (UBOs, push constants):

- `transientBuffer`: GPU-private buffer (32MB)
- `transientStagingBuffer`: CPU-mapped staging buffer
- `transientOffset`: Current write offset, reset each frame

This is defined in [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:324-333]() and used extensively throughout the rendering code to upload small constant data without allocating persistent buffers.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:84-343](), [src/RenderEngine.cpp:792-837](), [src/RenderEngine_Draw.cpp:479-630](), [include/RavEngine/MeshAllocation.hpp]()39:T80d7,# RGL Graphics Abstraction Layer

## Overview

RGL (RavEngine Graphics Library) is a low-level graphics API abstraction layer that provides a unified interface over Vulkan, DirectX 12, and Metal. It enables RavEngine's rendering system to operate across multiple platforms without platform-specific code in the engine layer.

**Scope**: This document covers RGL's architecture, command buffer abstraction, resource state management, and backend implementations. For information about how RavEngine's renderer uses RGL, see [Rendering Architecture](#4.1). For GPU-driven rendering techniques built on top of RGL, see [GPU-Driven Rendering Techniques](#9.2).

RGL provides:
- **Command buffer recording** with automatic resource state tracking
- **Pipeline state objects** for rendering and compute
- **Resource management** for buffers, textures, and samplers
- **Synchronization primitives** including fences and barriers
- **Backend-specific optimizations** while maintaining API consistency

## Architecture Overview

RGL uses an interface-based design where abstract base classes define the API contract, and backend-specific implementations provide platform functionality.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "RavEngine Layer"
        RenderEngine["RenderEngine"]
        Material["Material"]
        Particle["ParticleEmitter"]
    end
    
    subgraph "RGL Interface Layer"
        ICommandBuffer["ICommandBuffer<br/>(interface)"]
        IRenderPipeline["IRenderPipeline<br/>(interface)"]
        IBuffer["IBuffer<br/>(interface)"]
        ITexture["ITexture<br/>(interface)"]
        IDevice["IDevice<br/>(interface)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Vulkan Backend"
        CommandBufferVk["CommandBufferVk"]
        RenderPipelineVk["RenderPipelineVk"]
        BufferVk["BufferVk"]
        TextureVk["TextureVk"]
        DeviceVk["DeviceVk"]
    end
    
    subgraph "DirectX 12 Backend"
        CommandBufferD3D12["CommandBufferD3D12"]
        RenderPipelineD3D12["RenderPipelineD3D12"]
        BufferD3D12["BufferD3D12"]
        TextureD3D12["TextureD3D12"]
        DeviceD3D12["DeviceD3D12"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Metal Backend"
        CommandBufferMTL["CommandBufferMTL"]
        RenderPipelineMTL["RenderPipelineMTL"]
        BufferMTL["BufferMTL"]
        TextureMTL["TextureMTL"]
        DeviceMTL["DeviceMTL"]
    end
    
    RenderEngine --> ICommandBuffer
    Material --> IRenderPipeline
    Particle --> IBuffer
    
    ICommandBuffer -.implements.- CommandBufferVk
    ICommandBuffer -.implements.- CommandBufferD3D12
    ICommandBuffer -.implements.- CommandBufferMTL

    IRenderPipeline -.implements.- RenderPipelineD3D12
    IRenderPipeline -.implements.- RenderPipelineMTL
    
    IBuffer -.implements.- BufferVk
    IBuffer -.implements.- BufferD3D12
    IBuffer -.implements.- BufferMTL
    
    ITexture -.implements.- TextureVk
    ITexture -.implements.- TextureD3D12
    ITexture -.implements.- TextureMTL
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/include/RGL/CommandBuffer.hpp:99-185](), [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.hpp:38-306](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.hpp:36-135](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.hpp:14-95]()

### Core Interfaces

| Interface | Purpose | Key Methods |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| `ICommandBuffer` | Command recording and submission | `Begin()`, `End()`, `Commit()`, `BeginRendering()`, `Draw()` |
| `IRenderPipeline` | Graphics pipeline state | Shader configuration, rasterizer state, blend modes |
| `IComputePipeline` | Compute pipeline state | Compute shader configuration |
| `IBuffer` | GPU buffer abstraction | Memory allocation, mapping, binding |
| `ITexture` | Texture/image abstraction | Format, dimensions, mip levels, usage flags |
| `ISampler` | Texture sampling state | Filtering, wrapping, comparison modes |
| `IDevice` | GPU device management | Resource creation, queue access |

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/include/RGL/CommandBuffer.hpp:1-185]()

## Command Buffer System

### ICommandBuffer Interface

The `ICommandBuffer` interface defines the command recording API. All graphics and compute operations are recorded into command buffers before being submitted to GPU queues.

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Command Recording Flow"
        Reset["Reset()"]
        Begin["Begin()"]
        Commands["Record Commands<br/>BindPipeline<br/>SetResources<br/>Draw/Dispatch"]
        End["End()"]
        Commit["Commit()"]
    end
    
    Reset --> Begin
    Begin --> Commands
    Commands --> End
    End --> Commit
    
    subgraph "Command Types"
        Rendering["Rendering Commands<br/>BeginRendering<br/>BindRenderPipeline<br/>Draw<br/>DrawIndexed"]
        Compute["Compute Commands<br/>BeginCompute<br/>DispatchCompute"]
        Transfer["Transfer Commands<br/>CopyBufferToTexture<br/>CopyTextureToTexture"]
    end
    
    Commands --> Rendering
    Commands --> Compute
    Commands --> Transfer
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/include/RGL/CommandBuffer.hpp:99-185]()

### Command Buffer Lifecycle

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant App as Application
    participant CB as ICommandBuffer
    participant Backend as Backend Implementation
    participant GPU as GPU Queue
    
    App->>CB: Reset()
    Note over CB: Clear previous commands
    App->>CB: Begin()
    Note over CB: Start recording
    App->>CB: BeginRendering(renderPass)
    App->>CB: BindRenderPipeline(pipeline)
    App->>CB: SetVertexBuffer(buffer)
    App->>CB: Draw(nVertices)
    App->>CB: EndRendering()
    App->>CB: End()
    Note over CB: Finalize command buffer
    App->>CB: Commit(config)
    CB->>Backend: Submit to queue
    Backend->>GPU: Execute commands
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/include/RGL/CommandBuffer.hpp:100-107](), [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:47-85]()

### Rendering Commands

| Method | Purpose | Parameters |
|--------|---------|------------|
| `BeginRendering(RGLRenderPassPtr)` | Start a render pass with color/depth attachments | Render pass configuration |
| `EndRendering()` | Finish the current render pass | None |
| `BindRenderPipeline(RGLRenderPipelinePtr)` | Set active graphics pipeline | Pipeline state object |
| `SetVertexBuffer(RGLBufferPtr, VertexBufferBinding)` | Bind vertex data | Buffer, binding slot, offset |
| `SetIndexBuffer(RGLBufferPtr)` | Bind index data for indexed drawing | Buffer reference |
| `Draw(uint32_t, DrawInstancedConfig)` | Non-indexed draw call | Vertex count, instance config |
| `DrawIndexed(uint32_t, DrawIndexedInstancedConfig)` | Indexed draw call | Index count, instance config |
| `ExecuteIndirect(IndirectConfig)` | GPU-driven indirect draw | Indirect buffer, draw count |

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/include/RGL/CommandBuffer.hpp:109-134]()

### Compute Commands

| Method | Purpose | Parameters |
|--------|---------|------------|
| `BeginCompute(RGLComputePipelinePtr)` | Start compute pass | Compute pipeline |
| `EndCompute()` | End compute pass | None |
| `DispatchCompute(x, y, z, ...)` | Launch compute shader | Threadgroups and threads per group |
| `DispatchIndirect(DispatchIndirectConfig)` | GPU-driven compute dispatch | Indirect buffer configuration |

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/include/RGL/CommandBuffer.hpp:114-116]()

Resources must be bound to specific shader stages before use:

## Resource State Management

RGL automatically tracks resource states and inserts barriers as needed. Each backend handles this differently based on API requirements.

### Vulkan State Tracking

The Vulkan backend explicitly tracks image layouts and buffer access patterns using `TextureLastUse` and `BufferLastUse` structures.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Texture State Tracking"
        TextureUse["RecordTextureBinding()<br/>TextureLastUseKey"]
        CheckLayout["Check Current Layout"]
        NeedTransition{Layout<br/>Changed?}
        InsertBarrier["Insert VkImageMemoryBarrier"]
        UpdateTracker["Update activeTextures map"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Buffer State Tracking"
        BufferUse["RecordBufferBinding()<br/>BufferVk*"]
        CheckAccess["Check Last Access"]
        NeedSync{Previous<br/>Write?}
        InsertBufferBarrier["Insert VkBufferMemoryBarrier2"]
        UpdateBufferTracker["Update activeBuffers map"]
    end
    
    TextureUse --> CheckLayout
    CheckLayout --> NeedTransition
    NeedTransition -->|Yes| InsertBarrier
    NeedTransition -->|No| UpdateTracker
    InsertBarrier --> UpdateTracker
    
    BufferUse --> CheckAccess
    CheckAccess --> NeedSync
    NeedSync -->|Yes| InsertBufferBarrier
    NeedSync -->|No| UpdateBufferTracker
    InsertBufferBarrier --> UpdateBufferTracker
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.hpp:50-66](), [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:407-530]()

#### Vulkan Texture Layout Transitions

The Vulkan backend maintains per-subresource layout tracking using `TextureLastUseKey`:

```cpp
struct TextureLastUseKey {
    const TextureVk* texture;
    covered_mips_t coveredMips;      // Bitmask of covered mip levels
    covered_layers_t coveredLayers;  // Bitmask of covered array layers
};
```

When a texture is bound, `RecordTextureBinding()` checks if the current layout matches the needed layout for the operation:

- **Color attachment**: `VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL`
- **Depth attachment**: `VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_DEPTH_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL`
- **Shader read**: `VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL` or `VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_DEPTH_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL`
- **Storage image**: `VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_GENERAL`
- **Transfer source**: `VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL`
- **Transfer destination**: `VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL`

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.hpp:11-30](), [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:447-530]()

#### Vulkan Buffer Barriers

Buffer barriers are simpler than texture barriers. The `RecordBufferBinding()` method inserts a `VkBufferMemoryBarrier2` if the buffer was previously written to:

```cpp
VkBufferMemoryBarrier2 bufferBarrier{
    .srcStageMask = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_ALL_COMMANDS_BIT,
    .srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_2_SHADER_WRITE_BIT | VK_ACCESS_2_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT | ...,
    .dstStageMask = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_ALL_COMMANDS_BIT,
    .dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_2_SHADER_READ_BIT | VK_ACCESS_2_TRANSFER_READ_BIT | ...,
    .buffer = buffer->buffer,
    .offset = 0,
    .size = buffer->getBufferSize()
};
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:407-445]()

### DirectX 12 State Tracking

DirectX 12 uses explicit resource state transitions via `ID3D12GraphicsCommandList::ResourceBarrier()`. The `CommandBufferD3D12` class tracks `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATES` for buffers and textures.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "D3D12 Resource State Management"
        SyncCall["SyncIfNeeded(resource, neededState)"]
        LookupCurrent["Lookup activeBuffers/<br/>activeTextures map"]
        CompareState{Current state<br/>== Needed state?}
        CheckWritten{Previously<br/>written to?}
        TransitionBarrier["CD3DX12_RESOURCE_BARRIER::Transition"]
        UAVBarrier["CD3DX12_RESOURCE_BARRIER::UAV"]
        ExecuteBarrier["commandList->ResourceBarrier()"]
        UpdateState["Update state tracker"]
    end
    
    SyncCall --> LookupCurrent
    LookupCurrent --> CompareState
    CompareState -->|Different| TransitionBarrier
    CompareState -->|Same| CheckWritten
    TransitionBarrier --> ExecuteBarrier
    CheckWritten -->|Yes + UAV| UAVBarrier
    CheckWritten -->|No| UpdateState
    UAVBarrier --> ExecuteBarrier
    ExecuteBarrier --> UpdateState
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.hpp:46-52](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:601-660]()

#### D3D12 Texture State Transitions

Common DirectX 12 resource states:

| State | Usage |
|-------|-------|
| `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_RENDER_TARGET` | Color render target |
| `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_DEPTH_WRITE` | Depth/stencil write |
| `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_DEPTH_READ` | Depth read in shader |
| `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_PIXEL_SHADER_RESOURCE` | Texture read in pixel shader |
| `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_NON_PIXEL_SHADER_RESOURCE` | Texture read in non-pixel shader |
| `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_UNORDERED_ACCESS` | UAV (read-write) |
| `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_COPY_SOURCE` | Copy source |
| `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_COPY_DEST` | Copy destination |

The `SyncIfNeeded()` method handles per-subresource transitions for mip levels and array layers.

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:259-280](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:661-740]()

#### D3D12 UAV Barriers

For Unordered Access Views (UAVs), DirectX 12 requires explicit UAV barriers between consecutive writes to ensure proper ordering:

```cpp
auto barrier = CD3DX12_RESOURCE_BARRIER::UAV(resource->GetResource());
commandList->ResourceBarrier(1, &barrier);
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:647-651](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:696-701]()

### Metal Resource Tracking

Metal handles resource state transitions automatically in most cases. The `CommandBufferMTL` implementation explicitly declares resource usage via `useResource()` calls rather than barriers.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Metal Resource Usage"
        UseResource["UseResource(texture/buffer)"]
        IsRender{Render or<br/>Compute?}
        RenderUse["[encoder useResource:... usage:...]<br/>stages: MTLRenderStageVertex | Fragment"]
        ComputeUse["[encoder useResource:... usage:...]<br/>MTLResourceUsageRead | Write"]
    end
    
    UseResource --> IsRender
    IsRender -->|Render| RenderUse
    IsRender -->|Compute| ComputeUse
```

Metal automatically handles:
- Memory coherency between shader stages
- Hazard tracking for read-after-write and write-after-write
- Synchronization between render passes

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:314-330]()

## Command Encoding Patterns

### Vulkan Deferred Encoding

Vulkan backend uses **deferred command encoding**. Commands are stored in a `std::variant` and encoded during `EncodeQueuedCommands()`:

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Deferred Encoding"
        Record["BindBuffer()<br/>SetTexture()<br/>Draw()"]
        Store["Store in renderCommands<br/>std::vector<std::variant<...>>"]
        Encode["EncodeQueuedCommands()"]
        Visit["std::visit with Overload"]
        Execute["vkCmd... calls"]
    end
    
    Record --> Store
    Store --> Encode
    Encode --> Visit
    Visit --> Execute
```

The `renderCommands` vector holds command variants:

```cpp
std::vector<std::variant<
    CmdSetVertexBuffer,
    CmdBeginRendering,
    CmdDraw,
    CmdBindBuffer,
    // ... many more command types
>> renderCommands;
```

Commands are encoded using a visitor pattern with lambda overloads for each command type.

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.hpp:190-218](), [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:532-1007]()

### DirectX 12 Immediate Encoding

DirectX 12 backend encodes commands **immediately** when methods are called:

```cpp
void CommandBufferD3D12::Draw(uint32_t nVertices, const DrawInstancedConfig& config) {
    commandList->DrawInstanced(nVertices, config.nInstances, 
                               config.startVertex, config.firstInstance);
}
```

This approach is simpler but requires careful state tracking.

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:332-339]()

### Metal Immediate Encoding

Metal also uses **immediate encoding** with encoder objects:

```cpp
void CommandBufferMTL::Draw(uint32_t nVertices, const DrawInstancedConfig& config) {
    [currentCommandEncoder drawPrimitives:MTLPrimitiveType(currentPrimitiveType) 
        vertexStart:config.startVertex * vertexBuffer->stride 
        vertexCount:nVertices 
        instanceCount:config.nInstances 
        baseInstance:config.firstInstance];
}
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:258-260]()

## Pipeline State Objects

### Render Pipeline Binding

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Pipeline Binding Flow"
        BindPipeline["BindRenderPipeline(pipeline)"]
        VkBind["Vulkan:<br/>vkCmdBindPipeline"]
        D3D12Bind["D3D12:<br/>SetPipelineState<br/>SetGraphicsRootSignature<br/>IASetPrimitiveTopology"]
        MTLBind["Metal:<br/>setRenderPipelineState<br/>setDepthStencilState<br/>setCullMode, setWinding"]
    end
    
    BindPipeline --> VkBind
    BindPipeline --> D3D12Bind
    BindPipeline --> MTLBind
```

Pipeline binding sets:
- Shader programs (vertex, fragment, etc.)
- Input assembly state (topology, primitive restart)
- Rasterizer state (cull mode, winding order, polygon mode)
- Depth/stencil state (depth test, stencil operations)
- Blend state (blend equations, write masks)

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:86-90](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:149-155](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:158-174]()

### Compute Pipeline Binding

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant App
    participant CB as CommandBuffer
    participant Pipeline as ComputePipeline
    participant Backend
    
    App->>CB: BeginCompute(pipeline)
    CB->>Backend: Bind compute PSO
    App->>CB: BindComputeBuffer(buffer, binding)
    App->>CB: SetComputeTexture(texture, index)
    App->>CB: DispatchCompute(x, y, z)
    Backend->>Backend: Execute compute shader
    App->>CB: EndCompute()
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:133-143](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:156-165](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:176-186]()

## Resource Binding Architecture

### Descriptor/Binding Models

Each backend has a different resource binding model:

| Backend | Binding Model | Implementation |
|---------|---------------|----------------|
| **Vulkan** | Descriptor sets with push descriptors | `vkCmdPushDescriptorSetKHR` for dynamic binding |
| **DirectX 12** | Root signature with descriptor tables | Root parameters for CBVs, SRVs, UAVs |
| **Metal** | Direct argument buffer binding | `setVertexBuffer`, `setFragmentTexture` at index |

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:656-709](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:171-185](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:202-222]()

### Vulkan Push Descriptors

Vulkan backend uses `VK_KHR_push_descriptor` for efficient dynamic binding without pre-allocated descriptor sets:

```cpp
VkWriteDescriptorSet writeinfo{
    .sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_WRITE_DESCRIPTOR_SET,
    .dstSet = VK_NULL_HANDLE,  // push descriptors
    .dstBinding = bindingOffset,
    .descriptorCount = 1,
    .descriptorType = VK_DESCRIPTOR_TYPE_STORAGE_BUFFER,
    .pBufferInfo = &bufferInfo,
};
vkCmdPushDescriptorSetKHR(commandBuffer, bindPoint, pipelineLayout, 0, 1, &writeinfo);
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:759-788]()

### DirectX 12 Root Signature

DirectX 12 uses root signatures to define resource binding layout. Resources are bound via:
- **Root descriptors** (direct GPU virtual addresses for CBVs/SRVs/UAVs)
- **Root constants** (inline 32-bit values)
- **Descriptor tables** (ranges in descriptor heaps)

```cpp
// Root descriptor for storage buffer
commandList->SetGraphicsRootShaderResourceView(bindPoint, 
    buffer->BufferLocation + offsetIntoBuffer);

// Root constant for push constants
commandList->SetGraphicsRoot32BitConstants(offset, size, data, 0);
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:170-185](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:212-225]()

### Metal Argument Buffers

Metal binds resources directly to shader argument indices. For bindless access, Metal uses argument buffers stored in global buffers:

```cpp
[currentCommandEncoder setVertexBuffer:buffer offset:offsetIntoBuffer atIndex:offsetIndex];
[currentCommandEncoder setFragmentTexture:texture atIndex:index];
```

For bindless textures:
```cpp
[currentCommandEncoder setFragmentBuffer:owningQueue->owningDevice->globalTextureBuffer 
                                  offset:0 
                                 atIndex:index];
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:202-221](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:343-350]()

## Transfer Operations

### Buffer and Texture Copies

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Copy Operations"
        CopyBufToTex["CopyBufferToTexture"]

        CopyBufToBuf["CopyBufferToBuffer"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Vulkan Implementation"
        VkCopyBufImg["vkCmdCopyBufferToImage"]
        VkCopyImgBuf["vkCmdCopyImageToBuffer"]

        VkCopyBuf["vkCmdCopyBuffer"]
    end
    
    subgraph "D3D12 Implementation"
        D3DCopyTex["CopyTextureRegion"]
        D3DCopyBuf["CopyBufferRegion"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Metal Implementation"
        MTLBlit["MTLBlitCommandEncoder"]
        MTLCopyBufImg["copyFromBuffer:toTexture"]
        MTLCopyImgBuf["copyFromTexture:toBuffer"]
        MTLCopyImg["copyFromTexture:toTexture"]
        MTLCopyBuf["copyFromBuffer:toBuffer"]
    end
    
    CopyBufToTex --> VkCopyBufImg
    CopyBufToTex --> D3DCopyTex
    CopyBufToTex --> MTLCopyBufImg
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:267-319](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:366-497](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:372-430]()

### Transfer Synchronization

Transfer operations require proper state transitions:

**Vulkan**:
- Source texture: `VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL`
- Destination texture: `VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL`
- Buffers: Automatically synced via `RecordBufferBinding()`

**DirectX 12**:
- Source: `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_COPY_SOURCE`
- Destination: `D3D12_RESOURCE_STATE_COPY_DEST`
- Explicit transitions via `SyncIfNeeded()`

**Metal**:
- No explicit states, uses `MTLBlitCommandEncoder`
- Automatic hazard tracking

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:278-283](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:434-437]()

## Indirect Rendering

RGL supports GPU-driven indirect rendering where draw parameters are sourced from GPU buffers.

### Indirect Draw Commands

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Indirect Command Structures"
        IndirectCmd["IndirectCommand<br/>vertexCount<br/>instanceCount<br/>firstVertex<br/>firstInstance"]
        IndirectIndexedCmd["IndirectIndexedCommand<br/>indexCount<br/>instanceCount<br/>indexStart<br/>baseVertex<br/>baseInstance"]
        ComputeIndirectCmd["ComputeIndirectCommand<br/>x, y, z"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Execution"
        ExecuteIndirect["ExecuteIndirect(config)"]
        ExecuteIndirectIndexed["ExecuteIndirectIndexed(config)"]
        DispatchIndirect["DispatchIndirect(config)"]
    end
    
    IndirectCmd --> ExecuteIndirect
    IndirectIndexedCmd --> ExecuteIndirectIndexed
    ComputeIndirectCmd --> DispatchIndirect
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/include/RGL/CommandBuffer.hpp:55-84]()

### Backend Implementations

**Vulkan**:
```cpp
vkCmdDrawIndexedIndirect(commandBuffer, 
    indirectBuffer, 
    offsetIntoBuffer, 
    nDraws, 
    sizeof(IndirectIndexedCommand));
```

**DirectX 12**:
```cpp
commandList->ExecuteIndirect(
    multidrawIndexedSignature,  // ID3D12CommandSignature
    nDraws,
    indirectBuffer,
    offsetIntoBuffer,
    nullptr, 0);
```

**Metal** (multi-draw via loop):
```cpp
for(uint32_t i = 0; i < config.nDraws; i++) {
    [encoder drawIndexedPrimitives:... 
        indirectBuffer:buffer->buffer 
        indirectBufferOffset:offsetIntoBuffer + i * sizeof(IndirectIndexedCommand)];
}
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:790-798](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:508-523](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:453-465]()

## Synchronization Primitives

### Fences

Fences enable CPU-GPU synchronization. The `Commit()` method accepts an optional fence to signal upon completion:

```cpp
CommitConfig config{
    .signalFence = myFence
};
commandBuffer->Commit(config);
```

**Vulkan**: Signals `VkFence` via `vkQueueSubmit`
**DirectX 12**: Signals `ID3D12Fence` via `ID3D12CommandQueue::Signal`
**Metal**: Uses `MTLCommandBuffer` completion handlers

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/include/RGL/CommandBuffer.hpp:46-48](), [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:339-344](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:499-507]()

### BlockUntilCompleted

For immediate synchronization, `BlockUntilCompleted()` waits for the command buffer to finish execution:

**Vulkan**:
```cpp
vkWaitForFences(device, 1, &internalFence, VK_TRUE, UINT64_MAX);
```

**DirectX 12**:
```cpp
internalFence->SetEventOnCompletion(1, internalFenceEvent);
WaitForSingleObject(internalFenceEvent, DWORD_MAX);
```

**Metal**:
```cpp
[currentCommandBuffer waitUntilCompleted];
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:376-379](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:589-596](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:482-492]()

## Push Constants / Root Constants

Small amounts of data can be pushed directly to shaders without requiring buffer allocation.

### API Comparison

| Backend | Name | Max Size | API Call |
|---------|------|----------|----------|
| **Vulkan** | Push constants | 128-256 bytes | `vkCmdPushConstants` |
| **DirectX 12** | Root constants | Unlimited (32-bit values) | `SetGraphicsRoot32BitConstants` |
| **Metal** | Bytes | 4KB | `setVertexBytes`, `setFragmentBytes` |

### Implementation

**Vulkan**:
```cpp
vkCmdPushConstants(commandBuffer, layout, stages, offset, size, data);
```

**DirectX 12**:
```cpp
auto size = data.size() / 4 + (data.size() % 4 != 0 ? 1 : 0);
commandList->SetGraphicsRoot32BitConstants(offset, size, data.data(), 0);
```

**Metal** (16-byte alignment):
```cpp
auto size = closest_multiple_of<uint64_t>(data.size(), 16);
[currentCommandEncoder setVertexBytes:tmp length:size atIndex:offset];
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:818-841](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:212-220](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:233-255]()

```cpp
VkViewport vp{
    .x = viewport.x,
    .y = viewport.height - viewport.y,
```

```cpp
MTLViewport vp{
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:943-953](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:341-353](), [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:272-283]()

## Backend-Specific Optimizations

### Vulkan Deferred Barrier Application

Vulkan accumulates barriers in `barriersToAdd` vector and applies them before rendering/compute blocks via `ApplyBarriers()`:

```cpp
void CommandBufferVk::ApplyBarriers() {
    if (barriersToAdd.size() == 0) return;
    
    VkDependencyInfo depInfo{
        .sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_DEPENDENCY_INFO,
        .bufferMemoryBarrierCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(barriersToAdd.size()),
        .pBufferMemoryBarriers = barriersToAdd.data(),
    };
    vkCmdPipelineBarrier2(commandBuffer, &depInfo);
    barriersToAdd.clear();
}
```

This batches multiple barriers into a single pipeline barrier call for efficiency.

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.hpp:302-303](), [deps/RGL/src/VkCommandBuffer.cpp:1044-1058]()

### DirectX 12 Subresource Tracking

DirectX 12 tracks per-mip-per-layer states using `D3D12TextureLastUseKey` for fine-grained transitions:

```cpp
auto subresource = texture->SubresourceIndexForMipLayer(mip, layer);
auto barrier = CD3DX12_RESOURCE_BARRIER::Transition(
    resource, currentState, neededState, subresource);
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.hpp:11-28](), [deps/RGL/src/D3D12CommandBuffer.cpp:712-729]()

### Metal Automatic Hazard Tracking

Metal's GPU driver automatically:
- Detects read-after-write hazards
- Inserts memory barriers
- Manages coherency between render/compute encoders

The only requirement is declaring resource usage via `useResource()`:

```cpp
[currentCommandEncoder useResource:texture 
    usage:MTLResourceUsageRead | MTLResourceUsageWrite 
    stages:MTLRenderStageVertex | MTLRenderStageFragment];
```

**Sources**: [deps/RGL/src/MTLCommandBuffer.mm:314-330]()
