## Asset Pipeline Integration

The `pack_resources()` CMake function integrates asset compilation into the build system. It processes meshes, animations, skeletons, shaders, textures, audio, and UI files, then packages them into a `.rvedata` archive:

```mermaid
graph TD
    PackResources["pack_resources()<br/>[cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-326]"]
    
    PackResources --> ParseArgs["Parse Arguments<br/>TARGET, MESHES, ANIMATIONS,<br/>SKELETONS, SHADERS,<br/>TEXTURES, SOUNDS, UIS, etc."]
    
    ParseArgs --> CopyStaging["Copy to Staging Directory<br/>${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${TARGET}/"]
    
    CopyStaging --> CompileMeshes["Compile Meshes<br/>rvemc â†’ .rvem<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:122-144]"]
    CopyStaging --> CompileSkeletons["Compile Skeletons<br/>rveskc â†’ .rves<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:146-162]"]
    CopyStaging --> CompileAnimations["Compile Animations<br/>rveac â†’ .rvea<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:164-180]"]
    CopyStaging --> CompileShaders["Compile Shaders<br/>rvesc â†’ bytecode<br/>[cmake/shaders.cmake]"]
    
    CompileMeshes --> CreateArchive["Create .rvedata Archive<br/>ZIP all assets<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:290-297]"]
    CompileSkeletons --> CreateArchive
    CompileAnimations --> CreateArchive
    CompileShaders --> CreateArchive
    CopyStaging --> CreateArchive
    
    CreateArchive --> PlatformOutput{Platform}
    
    PlatformOutput -->|Apple| BundleResources["Add to App Bundle<br/>MACOSX_PACKAGE_LOCATION<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:301-303]"]
    PlatformOutput -->|UWP| DeploymentContent["VS Deployment Content<br/>VS_DEPLOYMENT_CONTENT<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:308-309]"]
    PlatformOutput -->|Win32/Linux| CopyToOutput["Copy to Output Directory<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:312-322]"]
```

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-326]()

### Usage Example

A typical integration in a game project's `CMakeLists.txt`:

```cmake
file(GLOB objects "objects/*.obj" "objects/*.fbx")
file(GLOB textures "textures/*")
file(GLOB shaders "shaders/*.vsh" "shaders/*.fsh" "shaders/*.csh")
file(GLOB fonts "fonts/*.ttf")
file(GLOB sounds "sounds/*.ogg")
file(GLOB uis "ui/*.rml" "ui/*.rcss")

pack_resources(TARGET "${PROJECT_NAME}" 
    MESHES ${meshes}
    OBJECTS ${objects}
    SHADERS ${shaders}
    TEXTURES ${textures}
    UIS ${uis}
    FONTS ${fonts}
    SOUNDS ${sounds}
)
```

[README.md:50-64]()

**Sources:** [README.md:50-64](), [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:1-326]()

### Mesh Compilation

Mesh compilation reads JSON configuration files specifying source model files:

[cmake/pack_resources.cmake:123-144]()

The output `.rvem` file contains optimized vertex/index buffers and mesh metadata.

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:122-144]()

### Streaming Assets

Streaming assets (files accessed directly at runtime, not packed in archives) receive platform-specific handling:

[cmake/pack_resources.cmake:68-97]()

- **Apple:** Placed in app bundle's `Resources/${TARGET}_Streaming/` directory using `MACOSX_PACKAGE_LOCATION`
- **UWP:** Deployed via `VS_DEPLOYMENT_CONTENT` property
- **Other:** Copied to `${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/$<CONFIGURATION>/${TARGET}_Streaming/`

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:68-97]()

## Shader Compilation

Shader compilation differs between Apple platforms (Metal) and others (Vulkan/DirectX):

```mermaid
graph TD
    ShaderCompile["Shader Compilation Entry<br/>[cmake/shaders.cmake]"]
    
    ShaderCompile --> DetectPlatform{Platform}
    
    DetectPlatform -->|Apple| MetalPath["Metal Shader Path"]
    DetectPlatform -->|Other| SPIRVPath["SPIRV Shader Path"]
    
    MetalPath --> XcodeConfig["Xcode MTL Configuration<br/>MTL_LANGUAGE_REVISION=Metal30<br/>MTL_OPTIMIZATION_LEVEL<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:18-24]"]
    
    XcodeConfig --> MetalCompile["Xcode Metal Compiler<br/>Compile to .metallib"]
    
    MetalCompile --> MetalBundle["Add to Bundle Resources<br/>Embedded in app"]
    
    SPIRVPath --> RVESC["rvesc Tool<br/>GLSL â†’ Platform bytecode"]
    
    RVESC --> PlatformBytecode["Platform Bytecode<br/>SPIR-V (Vulkan)<br/>DXIL (DirectX)<br/>WGSL (WebGPU)"]
    
    PlatformBytecode --> CMRC["CMRC Embedding<br/>cmrc_add_resource_library()<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:207-238]"]
    
    CMRC --> StaticLib["${TARGET}_ShaderResources<br/>Static library with shaders"]
    
    StaticLib --> LinkTarget["Link to Target<br/>[pack_resources.cmake:216]"]
```

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:18-238](), [cmake/shaders.cmake]()

On Apple platforms, Xcode compiles Metal shaders into `.metallib` libraries automatically. The build system configures Metal compiler settings:

[cmake/pack_resources.cmake:18-24]()

- `MTL_OPTIMIZATION_LEVEL`: Optimize in Release builds

**Sources:** [cmake/pack_resources.cmake:18-25]()

## Dependency Management

RavEngine uses CMake's `add_subdirectory()` to include third-party libraries, configuring them to avoid unwanted builds:

### Common Patterns

**Disable tests and examples:**
```cmake
set(LIBRARY_BUILD_TESTS OFF CACHE INTERNAL "")
set(LIBRARY_BUILD_EXAMPLES OFF CACHE INTERNAL "")
```

**Use static linking:**
```cmake
set(LIBRARY_BUILD_STATIC ON CACHE INTERNAL "")
set(LIBRARY_BUILD_SHARED OFF CACHE INTERNAL "")
```

**Exclude from install:**
```cmake
set(LIBRARY_INSTALL OFF CACHE INTERNAL "")
add_subdirectory(deps/library EXCLUDE_FROM_ALL)
```

## RTTI Configuration

RavEngine disables RTTI (Run-Time Type Information) across most of the codebase to reduce binary size and improve performance:

[cmake/rtti.cmake:1-7]()

[cmake/rtti.cmake:9-30]()

## Purpose and Scope

This document covers RavEngine's mesh and geometry processing systems, including the `MeshAsset` and `MeshAssetSkinned` classes, mesh data structures, serialization formats, GPU upload, and navigation mesh generation using Recast/Detour. 

For information about skeletal animation and the skinning compute shader pipeline, see [Skeletal Skinning Pipeline](#6.4). For GPU-driven rendering and culling, see [GPU-Driven Rendering Techniques](#9.2). For transform hierarchy management, see [Transform and Scene Hierarchy](#3.3).

---

## Mesh Data Structures

### MeshPart and Vertex Attributes

The engine uses `MeshPart` as the primary CPU-side representation of mesh geometry. This structure stores vertex attributes in separate vectors for data-oriented layout:

| Attribute | Type | Flag | Description |
|-----------|------|------|-------------|
| `positions` | `Vector<vector3>` | `MeshAttributes::position` | Vertex positions in local space |
| `normals` | `Vector<vector3>` | `MeshAttributes::normal` | Per-vertex normals |
| `tangents` | `Vector<vector4>` | `MeshAttributes::tangent` | Tangent space vectors (w = handedness) |
| `bitangents` | `Vector<vector3>` | `MeshAttributes::bitangent` | Bitangent vectors |
| `uv0` | `Vector<vector2>` | `MeshAttributes::uv0` | Primary texture coordinates |
| `lightmapUVs` | `Vector<vector2>` | `MeshAttributes::lightmapUV` | Lightmap UV coordinates |
| `indices` | `Vector<uint32_t>` | N/A | Triangle indices |

**MeshAttributes Structure**

The `MeshAttributes` struct uses bit flags to track which vertex attributes are present in a mesh. This enables the rendering system to configure the appropriate vertex input layout:

```cpp
struct MeshAttributes {
    bool position : 1;
    bool normal : 1;
    bool tangent : 1;
    bool bitangent : 1;
    bool uv0 : 1;
    bool lightmapUV : 1;
};
```

**MeshPartView**

For read-only access without copying, `MeshPartView` provides `std::span`-based views into existing mesh data. This is used during GPU upload to avoid redundant allocations.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/Mesh.hpp](), [include/RavEngine/MeshAsset.hpp:22-61]()

---

## MeshAsset Class

### Overview

`MeshAsset` is the runtime representation of static mesh geometry. It manages both CPU-side data (optional) and GPU-side allocations, calculating bounding volumes and handling deserialization from the `.rvem` format.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "MeshAsset Lifecycle"
        Constructor["MeshAsset Constructor"]
        Deserialize["DeserializeMeshFromMemory()"]
        Init["InitializeFromRawMesh()"]
        CalcBounds["Calculate Bounding Box<br/>and Radius"]
        GPUAlloc["RenderEngine::AllocateMesh()"]
        MeshRange["MeshRange Allocation"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Data Storage"
        SystemRAM["systemRAMcopy<br/>(optional MeshPart)"]
        GPUBuffer["GPU Vertex/Index Buffers<br/>(via MeshRange)"]
        Metadata["Bounds, Radius,<br/>Attributes, Counts"]
    end
    
    Constructor --> Deserialize
    Deserialize --> Init
    Init --> CalcBounds
    Init --> GPUAlloc
    GPUAlloc --> MeshRange
    
    Init -.->|if keepInSystemRAM| SystemRAM
    MeshRange --> GPUBuffer
    CalcBounds --> Metadata
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/MeshAsset.hpp:27-144](), [src/MeshAsset.cpp:82-180]()

### .rvem Serialization Format

RavEngine uses a custom binary format (`.rvem`) produced by the `rvemc` mesh compiler. The format is optimized for fast loading with minimal parsing:

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "SerializedMeshDataHeader"
        Magic["Magic: 'rvem'<br/>(4 bytes)"]
        NumVerts["numVertices<br/>(uint32)"]
        NumIndices["numIndicies<br/>(uint32)"]
        AttrFlags["attributes<br/>(bitfield)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Vertex Data Blocks"
        Positions["Positions<br/>(if hasPositionsBit)"]
        Normals["Normals<br/>(if hasNormalsBit)"]
        Tangents["Tangents<br/>(if hasTangentsBit)"]
        Bitangents["Bitangents<br/>(if hasBitangentsBit)"]
        UV0["UV0<br/>(if hasUV0Bit)"]
        LightmapUV["LightmapUV<br/>(if hasLightmapUVBit)"]
    end
    
    IndexData["Index Buffer<br/>(uint32 array)"]
    
    Magic --> NumVerts
    NumVerts --> NumIndices
    NumIndices --> AttrFlags
    AttrFlags --> Positions
    Positions --> Normals
    Normals --> Tangents
    Tangents --> Bitangents
    Bitangents --> UV0
    UV0 --> LightmapUV
    LightmapUV --> IndexData
```

**Deserialization Process**

The `DeserializeMeshFromMemory()` function [src/MeshAsset.cpp:23-80]() performs zero-copy deserialization:

1. **Read header** - Extract magic number, vertex/index counts, attribute flags
2. **Validate magic** - Ensure file starts with "rvem" signature
3. **Load vertex attributes** - For each enabled attribute flag, read `numVertices` elements directly into vectors
4. **Load indices** - Read `numIndicies` uint32 values
5. **Return offset** - Return bytes consumed for potential additional data (used by `MeshAssetSkinned`)

**Sources:** [src/MeshAsset.cpp:18-80](), [include/RavEngine/MaterialShared.hpp]() (SerializedMeshDataHeader)

### GPU Upload and Allocation

When `MeshAssetOptions::uploadToGPU` is true (default), mesh data is uploaded to the GPU through the `RenderEngine`:

```mermaid
graph TD
    InitRawMesh["InitializeFromRawMeshView()"]
    CheckUpload{uploadToGPU?}
    AllocMesh["RenderEngine::AllocateMesh()"]
    
    subgraph "RenderEngine Allocation"
        AppendVerts["Append vertices to<br/>global vertex buffer"]
        AppendIndices["Append indices to<br/>global index buffer"]
        ReturnRange["Return MeshRange<br/>(vertexStart, indexStart, counts)"]
    end
    
    StoreMeshRange["Store meshAllocation<br/>(MeshRange)"]
    
    InitRawMesh --> CheckUpload
    CheckUpload -->|Yes| AllocMesh
    AllocMesh --> AppendVerts
    AppendVerts --> AppendIndices
    AppendIndices --> ReturnRange
    ReturnRange --> StoreMeshRange
    CheckUpload -->|No| End[End]
    StoreMeshRange --> End
```

The `MeshRange` structure records the mesh's location in the global vertex/index buffers:

| Field | Type | Description |
|-------|------|-------------|
| `vertexStart` | `uint32_t` | Offset into global vertex buffer |
| `indexStart` | `uint32_t` | Offset into global index buffer |
| `vertexCount` | `uint32_t` | Number of vertices |
| `indexCount` | `uint32_t` | Number of indices |

**Sources:** [src/MeshAsset.cpp:154-180](), [include/RavEngine/MeshAllocation.hpp]()

### Bounding Volume Calculation

During initialization, `MeshAsset` computes an axis-aligned bounding box (AABB) and a bounding sphere radius by iterating all vertex positions:

```cpp
// Pseudocode from InitializeFromRawMeshView
for (const auto& pos : positions) {
    bounds.max = max(bounds.max, pos);
    bounds.min = min(bounds.min, pos);
    radius = max(radius, distance(pos, vec3(0)));
}
```

The `Bounds` struct stores the min/max corners as `vector3` values. The radius represents the maximum distance from the local origin (0,0,0) to any vertex, used for quick sphere-based culling.

**Sources:** [src/MeshAsset.cpp:157-168]()

### System RAM Copy Option

By default, mesh data is discarded after GPU upload. Setting `MeshAssetOptions::keepInSystemRAM = true` preserves a copy in `systemRAMcopy` for features requiring CPU access:

- **Physics colliders** - PhysX mesh colliders need vertex/index data
- **NavMesh generation** - Recast requires CPU-side geometry
- **Runtime mesh modification** - Procedural geometry or deformation

The system copy can be manually deallocated later via `DeallocSystemCopy()` to free memory:

```cpp
auto mesh = New<MeshAsset>("model", MeshAssetOptions{
    .keepInSystemRAM = true,  // Keep CPU copy
    .uploadToGPU = true       // Also upload to GPU
});

// Later, after using for physics setup:
mesh->DeallocSystemCopy();  // Free system memory
```

**Sources:** [src/MeshAsset.cpp:147-152](), [include/RavEngine/MeshAsset.hpp:129-143]()

### Multiple MeshPart Initialization

`MeshAsset` can be constructed from multiple `MeshPart` fragments, which are combined into a single GPU-resident mesh:

```cpp
void InitializeFromMeshPartFragments(
    const Vector<MeshPart>& meshes,
    const MeshAssetOptions& options
);
```

This process [src/MeshAsset.cpp:106-145]():

1. **Validates** all fragments have identical `MeshAttributes`
2. **Concatenates** vertex data from all fragments
3. **Remaps indices** by adding per-fragment base offsets
4. **Uploads** combined mesh as a single allocation

This is useful for importing models with multiple sub-meshes that should be treated as one draw call.

**Sources:** [src/MeshAsset.cpp:106-145]()

---

## MeshAssetSkinned

### Overview

`MeshAssetSkinned` extends `MeshAsset` to support skeletal animation by adding vertex weight and bone index data. It integrates with `SkeletonAsset` for GPU-based vertex skinning.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "MeshAssetSkinned Structure"
        Base["MeshAsset Base<br/>(positions, normals, etc.)"]
        Weights["weightsBuffer<br/>(RGLBufferPtr)"]
        VertexWeights["VertexWeights Struct<br/>(4 bone indices + 4 weights)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Data Layout per Vertex"
        BoneIdx["boneIndices[4]<br/>(uint16_t)"]
        BoneWeight["boneWeights[4]<br/>(float)"]
    end
    
    Base --> Weights
    Weights --> VertexWeights
    VertexWeights --> BoneIdx
    VertexWeights --> BoneWeight
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/MeshAssetSkinned.hpp:12-32]()

### VertexWeights Structure

Each vertex stores up to 4 bone influences:

```cpp
struct VertexWeights {
    uint16_t boneIndices[4];  // Indices into skeleton's joint array
    float boneWeights[4];     // Normalized weights (sum = 1.0)
};
```

This data is stored in a separate GPU storage buffer (`weightsBuffer`) referenced during the skinning compute shader pass. The bone indices correspond to joints in the associated `SkeletonAsset`.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/MaterialShared.hpp]() (VertexWeights definition)

### .rvem Extended Format for Skinned Meshes

Skinned mesh files append weight data after the standard mesh data:

```mermaid
graph LR
    StandardMesh["Standard .rvem Data<br/>(header + vertices + indices)"]
    WeightData["VertexWeights Array<br/>(numVertices elements)"]
    
    StandardMesh --> WeightData
```

The constructor [src/MeshAssetSkinned.cpp:25-71]():

1. **Deserializes base mesh** using parent's `DeserializeMeshFromMemory()`
2. **Validates weight data exists** - Checks remaining bytes >= 4
3. **Extracts weight array** - Reads `VertexWeights[numVertices]`
4. **Creates GPU buffer** - Uploads weights to storage buffer
5. **Asserts size match** - Ensures weight count equals vertex count

**Sources:** [src/MeshAssetSkinned.cpp:25-71]()

### Integration with Skeletal Animation

The skinning pipeline (detailed in [Skeletal Skinning Pipeline](#6.4)) uses `MeshAssetSkinned` in conjunction with `SkeletonAsset` and `AnimatorComponent`:

1. **AnimatorComponent** calculates skinning matrices (pose Ã— inverse bindpose)
2. **Skinning compute shader** (`skinning_cs_csh`) reads:
   - Base vertex positions/normals from `MeshAsset`
   - `VertexWeights` from `weightsBuffer`
   - Skinning matrices from `AnimatorComponent`
3. **Output** writes transformed vertices to dynamic GPU buffers

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/MeshAssetSkinned.hpp:12-32](), Animation system integration from high-level diagrams

---

## Navigation Mesh Generation

### Overview

`NavMeshComponent` generates navigation meshes from `MeshAsset` geometry using the Recast library for pathfinding. It requires the mesh to have `keepInSystemRAM = true` since Recast operates on CPU-side data.

```mermaid
graph TD
    MeshAsset["MeshAsset with<br/>systemRAMcopy"]
    Options["NavMeshComponent::Options<br/>(agent params, cell sizes)"]
    
    Constructor["NavMeshComponent(mesh, opt)"]
    
    subgraph "Recast Build Pipeline"
        Config["rcConfig Setup"]
        Heightfield["rcHeightfield<br/>Voxelization"]
        Filter["Filter Walkable Areas"]
        CompactHF["rcCompactHeightfield<br/>Simplification"]
        Regions["Region Partitioning<br/>(Watershed/Monotone/Layer)"]
        Contours["rcContourSet<br/>Edge Tracing"]
        PolyMesh["rcPolyMesh<br/>Polygon Generation"]
        DetailMesh["rcPolyMeshDetail<br/>Height Detail"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Detour Runtime"
        DetourData["dtNavMeshData<br/>Creation"]
        NavMesh["dtNavMesh Allocation"]
        NavQuery["dtNavMeshQuery<br/>(for pathfinding)"]
    end
    
    MeshAsset --> Constructor
    Options --> Constructor
    Constructor --> Config
    Config --> Heightfield
    Heightfield --> Filter
    Filter --> CompactHF
    CompactHF --> Regions
    Regions --> Contours
    Contours --> PolyMesh
    PolyMesh --> DetailMesh
    DetailMesh --> DetourData
    DetourData --> NavMesh
    NavMesh --> NavQuery
```

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/NavMeshComponent.hpp:11-67](), [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:17-252]()

### Configuration Options

The `NavMeshComponent::Options` struct configures the navigation mesh generation:

| Parameter | Default | Description |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| `cellSize` | 0.3 | Voxel XZ-plane size (world units) |
| `cellHeight` | 0.2 | Voxel Y-axis size (world units) |
| `agent.height` | 2.0 | Agent height for clearance |
| `agent.radius` | 0.6 | Agent radius for obstacle erosion |
| `agent.maxClimb` | 0.9 | Maximum climbable step height |
| `agent.maxSlope` | 45.0 | Maximum walkable slope (degrees) |
| `maxEdgeLen` | 12.0 | Maximum edge length in cells |
| `maxSimplificationError` | 1.3 | Edge simplification tolerance |
| `regionMinDimension` | 8.0 | Minimum region size (cellsÂ²) |
| `regionMergeDimension` | 20.0 | Region merge threshold (cellsÂ²) |
| `maxVertsPerPoly` | 6 | Maximum vertices per polygon |
| `detailSampleDist` | 6.0 | Detail mesh sample spacing |
| `detailSampleMaxError` | 1.0 | Detail mesh height error |
| `partitionMethod` | Watershed | Region partitioning algorithm |

**Agent Configuration**

The `Agent` struct defines the physical characteristics of entities that will use the navigation mesh. Recast uses these to:

- **Erode walkable area** by `agent.radius` to ensure clearance
- **Filter slopes** steeper than `agent.maxSlope`
- **Allow step climbing** up to `agent.maxClimb`
- **Ensure ceiling clearance** of `agent.height`

**Partition Methods**

Three region partitioning algorithms are available:

| Method | Quality | Speed | Use Case |
|--------|---------|-------|----------|
| `Watershed` | Best | Slowest | Complex multi-level environments |
| `Monotone` | Worst | Fastest | Simple flat terrains |
| `Layer` | Good | Medium | Tiled navmeshes with moderate complexity |

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/NavMeshComponent.hpp:21-46](), [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:43-63]()

### Build Process Steps

The `UpdateNavMesh()` method [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:21-252]() executes the Recast pipeline:

#### Step 1: Configuration and Heightfield Rasterization

```cpp
rcConfig cfg;
cfg.cs = opt.cellSize;
cfg.ch = opt.cellHeight;
cfg.walkableHeight = ceil(opt.agent.height / cfg.ch);
cfg.walkableRadius = ceil(opt.agent.radius / cfg.cs);
// ... additional config

rcHeightfield* solid = rcAllocHeightfield();
rcCreateHeightfield(ctx, *solid, cfg.width, cfg.height, ...);
```

Converts mesh triangles into a voxel grid heightfield [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:68-97]().

#### Step 2: Walkability Filtering

```cpp
rcMarkWalkableTriangles(ctx, cfg.walkableSlopeAngle, verts, ...);
rcRasterizeTriangles(ctx, verts, indices, ...);
rcFilterLowHangingWalkableObstacles(ctx, ...);
rcFilterLedgeSpans(ctx, ...);
rcFilterWalkableLowHeightSpans(ctx, ...);
```

Identifies and filters walkable surfaces based on slope and clearance [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:94-104]().

#### Step 3: Compact Heightfield and Region Building

```cpp
rcCompactHeightfield* chf = rcAllocCompactHeightfield();
rcBuildCompactHeightfield(ctx, ...);
rcErodeWalkableArea(ctx, cfg.walkableRadius, *chf);

// Partition based on selected method
switch (opt.partitionMethod) {
    case Watershed: rcBuildRegions(ctx, ...); break;
    case Monotone: rcBuildRegionsMonotone(ctx, ...); break;
    case Layer: rcBuildLayerRegions(ctx, ...); break;
}
```

Simplifies heightfield and partitions into walkable regions [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:107-144]().

#### Step 4: Contour Tracing and Polygon Mesh Generation

```cpp
rcContourSet* cset = rcAllocContourSet();
rcBuildContours(ctx, *chf, ...);

rcPolyMesh* pmesh = rcAllocPolyMesh();
rcBuildPolyMesh(ctx, *cset, cfg.maxVertsPerPoly, *pmesh);
```

Traces region edges and creates navigation polygon mesh [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:147-166]().

#### Step 5: Detail Mesh and Detour Data

```cpp
rcPolyMeshDetail* dmesh = rcAllocPolyMeshDetail();
rcBuildPolyMeshDetail(ctx, *pmesh, *chf, ...);

dtNavMeshCreateParams params;
// ... populate params from pmesh and dmesh
dtCreateNavMeshData(&params, &navData, &navDataSize);

navMesh = dtAllocNavMesh();
navMesh->init(navData, navDataSize, DT_TILE_FREE_DATA);

navMeshQuery = dtAllocNavMeshQuery();
navMeshQuery->init(navMesh, 2048);
```

Generates height detail and creates Detour runtime structures [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:169-246]().

**Sources:** [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:21-252]()

### Pathfinding Queries

Once built, the `dtNavMeshQuery` enables pathfinding via `CalculatePath()`:

```mermaid
graph TD
    Start["CalculatePath(start, end)"]
    FindPoly["dtNavMeshQuery::findNearestPoly()<br/>(for start and end)"]
    FindPath["dtNavMeshQuery::findPath()<br/>(returns polygon path)"]
    Straight["dtNavMeshQuery::findStraightPath()<br/>(converts to waypoints)"]
    Return["Return vector3 array"]
    
    Start --> FindPoly
    FindPoly --> FindPath
    FindPath --> Straight
    Straight --> Return
```

The process [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:260-319]():

1. **Find nearest polygons** - Locates navigation polygons near start/end points using bounding box search
2. **Calculate polygon path** - Detour's A* finds polygon sequence from start to end
3. **Generate straight path** - Converts polygon path to linear waypoints using funnel algorithm
4. **Return waypoints** - Converts Detour's float array to `Vector<vector3>`

**Thread Safety**

The `NavMeshComponent` uses a `SpinLock mtx` [include/RavEngine/NavMeshComponent.hpp:17]() to protect concurrent access during:
- NavMesh rebuilds (`UpdateNavMesh`)
- Pathfinding queries (`CalculatePath`)
- Debug rendering (`DebugDraw`)

**Sources:** [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:260-319](), [include/RavEngine/NavMeshComponent.hpp:11-67]()

### Debug Visualization

`NavMeshComponent` implements `IDebugRenderable` to visualize the navigation mesh:

```cpp
void NavMeshComponent::DebugDraw(DebugDrawer& dbg, const Transform& tr) const {
    mtx.lock();
    duDebugDrawNavMesh(&GetApp()->GetRenderEngine(), *navMesh, 0);
    mtx.unlock();
}
```

This uses Recast's `DebugUtils` (`duDebugDrawNavMesh`) to render the navigation mesh polygons, which integrates with RavEngine's immediate-mode debug drawing system.

**Sources:** [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:321-327]()

---

## Memory Management and Lifecycle

### MeshAsset Destruction

`MeshAsset` destructor [src/MeshAsset.cpp:97-104]() deallocates GPU resources:

```cpp
MeshAsset::~MeshAsset() {
    if (auto app = GetApp()) {
        app->GetRenderEngine().DeallocateMesh(meshAllocation);
    }
}
```

The `RenderEngine::DeallocateMesh()` does **not** immediately free GPU buffers. Instead, it marks the `MeshRange` as free in the global allocator, allowing reuse for future mesh uploads. The actual buffer memory persists for the engine's lifetime.

**Sources:** [src/MeshAsset.cpp:97-104]()

### MeshAssetSkinned Destruction

`MeshAssetSkinned` additionally enqueues the weights buffer for garbage collection:

```cpp
MeshAssetSkinned::~MeshAssetSkinned() {
    if (auto app = GetApp()) {
        app->GetRenderEngine().gcBuffers.enqueue(weightsBuffer);
    }
}
```

The `gcBuffers` queue is a lock-free SPSC queue that the render thread processes at safe points to destroy RGL buffers.

**Sources:** [src/MeshAssetSkinned.cpp:16-23]()

### NavMeshComponent Destruction

Recast/Detour structures are manually freed:

```cpp
NavMeshComponent::~NavMeshComponent() {
    dtFree(navMesh);
    dtFree(navMeshQuery);
    dtFree(navData);
}
```

These use Detour's allocator which wraps standard `malloc`/`free`.

**Sources:** [src/NavMeshComponent.cpp:254-258]()

### Asset Manager Integration

Both `MeshAsset` and `MeshAssetSkinned` provide `Manager` typedefs for weak reference caching:

```cpp
// MeshAsset
struct Manager : public GenericWeakReadThroughCache<std::string, MeshAsset> {};

// MeshAssetSkinned
struct Manager : public GenericWeakReadThroughCache<std::string, MeshAssetSkinned> {};
```

This enables automatic caching and weak reference management for loaded meshes. When all `Ref<MeshAsset>` references are released, the asset is destroyed and removed from the cache.

**Sources:** [include/RavEngine/MeshAsset.hpp:82](), [include/RavEngine/MeshAssetSkinned.hpp:25]()

---

## Integration with Other Systems

### Rendering System

The `MeshRange` stored in `meshAllocation` [include/RavEngine/MeshAsset.hpp:47]() is used by the rendering system during GPU culling and indirect draw generation. See [GPU-Driven Rendering Techniques](#9.2) for details on how culling shaders access mesh data.

### Physics System

`PhysicsCollider` can create mesh colliders from `MeshAsset`:

```cpp
auto collider = PhysicsCollider::MeshCollider(meshAsset);
```

This requires `MeshAssetOptions::keepInSystemRAM = true` since PhysX needs CPU-side vertex/index data to build acceleration structures.

### Animation System

`MeshAssetSkinned` is paired with `SkeletonAsset` and `AnimatorComponent` for skeletal animation. The compute shader reads:
- `MeshAsset` base geometry (positions, normals)
- `MeshAssetSkinned::weightsBuffer` (bone influences)
- Skinning matrices from `AnimatorComponent::skinningmats`

See [Skeletal Skinning Pipeline](#6.4) for the complete GPU skinning process.

**Sources:** High-level architecture diagrams, system integration descriptions3e:Tab83,# API Reference

This page provides comprehensive documentation of RavEngine's primary classes, organized by system. Each entry describes the purpose, key methods, and relationships of classes that form the public API. For architectural overviews and system-level documentation, see [Overview](#1). ## Core Application Classes

### App

**File**: [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:49-260]()

The `App` class is the entry point for all RavEngine applications. It manages the main loop, world lifecycle, and coordinates all engine subsystems.

**Key Members**:
- `tf::Executor executor` - Global thread pool for parallel task execution
- `NetworkManager networkManager` - Networking interface
- `TickMode tickMode` - Controls whether the application runs at dynamic or fixed rate
- `static constexpr float evalNormal = 60` - Baseline tick rate (60 Hz)

**Key Methods**:
- `int run(int argc, char** argv)` - Main application loop, invoked automatically
- `double GetCurrentTime()` - Returns time in seconds since application launch
- `void SetRenderedWorld(Ref<World> newWorld)` - Sets the world to be ticked and rendered
- `void AddWorld(Ref<World> world)` - Adds a world to the tick list
- `void RemoveWorld(Ref<World> world)` - Removes a world from the tick list
- `void DispatchMainThread(const T& f)` - Dispatches a task to execute on the main thread
- `float CurrentTPS()` - Returns current application tick rate

**Virtual Methods to Override**:
- `virtual AppConfig OnConfigure(int argc, char** argv)` - Configure render backend and settings
- `virtual void OnStartup(int argc, char** argv)` - Initialization logic
- `virtual void OnFatal(const std::string_view msg)` - Custom fatal error handler
- `virtual bool NeedsAudio() const` - Return false to disable audio subsystem
- `virtual bool NeedsNetworking() const` - Return true to enable networking subsystem

```mermaid

    App["App<br/>Main Application Class"]
    AppConfig["AppConfig<br/>Configuration Structure"]
    World["World<br/>ECS Container"]
    RenderEngine["RenderEngine<br/>Graphics Subsystem"]
    AudioPlayer["AudioPlayer<br/>Audio Subsystem"]
    NetworkManager["NetworkManager<br/>Networking"]
    
    App -->|"configures"| AppConfig
    App -->|"manages"| World
    App -->|"owns"| RenderEngine
    App -->|"owns"| AudioPlayer
    App -->|"contains"| NetworkManager
    
    App -->|"run(argc, argv)"| MainLoop["Main Loop Execution"]
    MainLoop -->|"calls"| OnStartup["OnStartup()"]
    MainLoop -->|"ticks"| World
    MainLoop -->|"draws"| RenderEngine
```

**Sources**: [include/RavEngine/App.hpp:49-260](), [src/App_priv.hpp:1-441](), [src/App.cpp:1-3]()

## World and Entity Management

### World

**File**: [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:156-999]()

The `World` class is the primary ECS container. It stores entities, components, and systems, and orchestrates the game simulation tick.

**Key Inner Types**:
- `EntitySparseSet<T>` - Sparse set container for storing components of type T
- `PolymorphicIndirection` - Manages polymorphic component access
- `RenderData` - GPU-friendly parallel data structures for rendering

**Key Methods**:
- `Entity Spawn()` - Creates a new entity and returns a handle
- `void Destroy(Entity e)` - Destroys an entity and all its components
- `void Tick(float scale)` - Advances simulation by one frame
- `template<typename T, typename... A> T& EmplaceComponent(Entity e, A&&... args)` - Adds component to entity
- `template<typename T> void DestroyComponent(Entity e)` - Removes component from entity
- `template<typename T> bool HasComponent(Entity e)` - Checks if entity has component
- `template<typename... T, typename Fn> void Filter(const Fn& fn)` - Iterates entities with specified components

**System Management**:
- `template<typename T> auto EmplaceSystem()` - Adds parallel system to world
- `template<typename T> auto EmplaceSerialSystem()` - Adds serial system to world
- `template<typename T> void EmplacePolymorphicSystem()` - Adds polymorphic system
- `template<typename A, typename B> void CreateDependency()` - Defines system execution order

### Entity

**File**: [include/RavEngine/Entity.hpp]()

A lightweight handle representing an entity in the world. Contains an ID and version number for detecting use-after-destroy bugs.

**Key Methods**:
- `template<typename T, typename... A> T& EmplaceComponent(A&&... args)` - Adds component
- `template<typename T> void DestroyComponent()` - Removes component
- `template<typename T> bool HasComponent() const` - Checks component existence
- `template<typename T> T& GetComponent()` - Retrieves component reference
- `Transform& GetTransform()` - Gets the entity's transform component
- `entity_t GetID() const` - Returns the entity's numeric ID

**Sources**: [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:156-999]()

## Transform System

### Transform

**File**: [include/RavEngine/Transform.hpp:20-293]()

Represents the position, rotation, and scale of an entity in the scene graph. Supports parent-child hierarchies with automatic dirty flag propagation.

**Key Members**:
- `vector3 position` - Local position relative to parent
- `quaternion rotation` - Local rotation relative to parent
- `vector3 scale` - Local scale relative to parent
- `matrix4 matrix` - Cached world transform matrix

**Key Methods**:
- `void SetLocalPosition(const vector3& pos)` - Sets position in parent space
- `void SetLocalRotation(const quaternion& rot)` - Sets rotation in parent space
- `void SetLocalScale(const vector3& scale)` - Sets scale in parent space
- `vector3 GetWorldPosition() const` - Computes position in world space
- `quaternion GetWorldRotation() const` - Computes rotation in world space
- `matrix4 GetWorldMatrix() const` - Computes full world transform
- `void SetParent(const ComponentHandle<Transform>& newParent)` - Establishes parent-child relationship
- `void AddChild(const ComponentHandle<Transform>& child)` - Adds a child transform
- `void RemoveChild(const ComponentHandle<Transform>& child)` - Removes a child transform

**Coordinate System Helpers**:
- `vector3 Forward() const` - Returns forward direction vector
- `vector3 Right() const` - Returns right direction vector
- `vector3 Up() const` - Returns up direction vector

```mermaid
graph TD
    TransformRoot["Transform<br/>Root Entity"]
    TransformChild1["Transform<br/>Child 1"]
    TransformChild2["Transform<br/>Child 2"]
    TransformGrandchild["Transform<br/>Grandchild"]
    
    TransformRoot -->|"AddChild()"| TransformChild1
    TransformRoot -->|"AddChild()"| TransformChild2
    TransformChild1 -->|"AddChild()"| TransformGrandchild
    
    TransformRoot -->|"isDirty = true"| PropagateDown["Propagate Dirty Flag"]
    PropagateDown --> TransformChild1
    PropagateDown --> TransformChild2
    PropagateDown --> TransformGrandchild
    
    TransformRoot -->|"GetWorldMatrix()"| ComputeWorld["Compute World Transform"]

```

## Rendering System

### RenderEngine

**File**: [include/RavEngine/RenderEngine.hpp:63-363]()

The `RenderEngine` manages all GPU operations, including the multi-pass rendering pipeline, material systems, and GPU resource allocation.

**Key Members**:
- `RGLDevicePtr device` - Graphics device abstraction
- `RGLCommandQueuePtr mainCommandQueue` - Primary command submission queue
- `RGLCommandBufferPtr mainCommandBuffer` - Main rendering command buffer
- `RGLSamplerPtr textureSampler, shadowSampler, depthPyramidSampler` - Texture samplers
- Various `RGLRenderPassPtr` - Render pass objects for different pipeline stages

**Key Methods**:
- `RGLCommandBufferPtr Draw(Ref<World>, std::span<RenderViewCollection>, float guiScaleFactor)` - Main rendering entry point
- `RenderTargetCollection CreateRenderTargetCollection(dim size, bool createDepth)` - Creates render targets
- `MeshRange AllocateMesh(const MeshPartView&)` - Allocates space in shared vertex/index buffers
- `void DeallocateMesh(const MeshRange&)` - Frees mesh allocation

**Texture Formats**:
- `static constexpr RGL::TextureFormat colorTexFormat = RGBA16_Sfloat` - Main color buffer
- `static constexpr RGL::TextureFormat depthFormat = D32SFloat` - Depth buffer
- `static constexpr RGL::TextureFormat ssaoOutputFormat = R16_Float` - Ambient occlusion output

## Material System

### Material

**File**: [include/RavEngine/Material.hpp:45-115]()

Base class representing a shader program. Materials define how objects are rendered and manage pipeline state.

**Constructor Parameters** (via `MaterialConfig`):
- `vertConfig` - Vertex attribute configuration
- `colorBlendConfig` - Color blending configuration
- `bindings` - Shader resource bindings
- `opacityMode` - Opaque or Transparent
- `cullMode` - Face culling mode
- `requiredAttributes` - Which mesh attributes are needed

**Key Methods**:
- `RGLRenderPipelinePtr GetMainRenderPipeline() const` - Returns main render pipeline
- `RGLRenderPipelinePtr GetShadowRenderPipeline() const` - Returns shadow pipeline
- `RGLRenderPipelinePtr GetDepthPrepassPipeline() const` - Returns depth prepass pipeline
- `MeshAttributes GetAttributes() const` - Returns required mesh attributes

**Material Manager**:
- `template<typename T, typename... A> static Ref<T> Material::Manager::Get(A&&... args)` - Gets or creates material instance

### PBRMaterial

**File**: [include/RavEngine/BuiltinMaterials.hpp:44-91]()

Physically-based rendering material with support for metallic-roughness workflow.

**Texture Slots**:
- `AlbedoTexture` - Base color texture
- `NormalTexture` - Tangent-space normal map
- `MetallicRoughnessTexture` - Metallic (B) and roughness (G) packed texture
- `EmissiveTexture` - Emissive color texture
- `OcclusionTexture` - Ambient occlusion texture

**User Shader Functions**:

Template materials parameterized by `LightingMode` (Lit or Unlit).

**Template Parameters**:

- `LightingMode::Unlit` - Ignores lighting calculations

## Lighting System

### Light

**File**: [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:21-63]()

Base class for all light types. Lights can be constrained to illuminate or shadow specific layers.

**Key Members**:
- `ColorRGBA color` - Light color (RGBA)
- `float Intensity` - Light intensity multiplier
- `renderlayer_t illuminationLayers` - Bitmask of layers to illuminate
- `renderlayer_t shadowLayers` - Bitmask of layers to shadow (if applicable)

**Key Methods**:
- `void SetColorRGBA(const ColorRGBA& color)` - Sets light color
- `void SetIntensity(float intensity)` - Sets light intensity
- `void SetIlluminationLayers(renderlayer_t layers)` - Sets which layers are illuminated
- `void SetShadowLayers(renderlayer_t layers)` - Sets which layers cast shadows

**Sources**: [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:21-63]()

---

### DirectionalLight

**File**: [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:134-159]()

Parallel light source simulating distant lights like the sun. Supports cascaded shadow mapping.

**Key Members**:
- `Array<float, MAX_CASCADES> shadowCascades` - Shadow cascade split distances
- `uint8_t numCascades` - Number of active shadow cascades (1-4)
- `float maxShadowDistanceFactor` - Multiplier for maximum shadow distance

**Shadow Data**:
- `Array<RGLTexturePtr, MAX_CASCADES> shadowMap` - Shadow map textures per cascade

---

### PointLight

**File**: [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:161-191]()

Omnidirectional light source that emits light in all directions from a point. Supports omnidirectional shadow mapping via cubemaps.

**Key Members**:
- `float radius` - Attenuation radius (not enforced, for hint purposes)
- `Array<RGLTexturePtr, 6> cubeShadowmaps` - Cubemap shadow faces

**Shadow Calculation**:
- Renders 6 shadow maps (one per cubemap face)
- Uses `CalcViewMatrix(position, faceIndex)` to compute view matrices
- Uses `CalcProjectionMatrix()` for 90Â° FOV perspective projection

**Sources**: [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:161-191](), [src/Light.cpp:62-266]()

---

### SpotLight

**File**: [include/RavEngine/Light.hpp:193-227]()

Conical light source with controllable cone angle. Supports shadow mapping.

**Key Members**:
- `float coneAngle` - Full cone angle in degrees
- `float penumbraAngle` - Soft edge angle in degrees
- `RGLTexturePtr shadowMap` - Single shadow map texture

**Key Methods**:
- `void SetConeAngle(float angle)` - Sets cone angle
- `void SetPenumbraAngle(float angle)` - Sets penumbra angle

## Physics System

### PhysicsBodyComponent

**File**: [include/RavEngine/PhysicsBodyComponent.hpp:39-383]()

Base class for physics bodies in the PhysX simulation. Bodies can be dynamic (affected by forces) or static (immovable).

**Derived Classes**:
- `RigidBodyDynamicComponent` - Dynamic physics body
- `RigidBodyStaticComponent` - Static (immovable) physics body

**Key Members**:
- `physx::PxRigidActor* rigidActor` - Underlying PhysX rigid actor

**Key Methods**:
- `void SetPosition(const vector3& pos)` - Sets body position
- `void SetRotation(const quaternion& rot)` - Sets body rotation
- `void SetScale(const vector3& scale)` - Sets body scale
- `vector3 GetPosition() const` - Gets body position
- `quaternion GetRotation() const` - Gets body rotation

**Collision Callbacks**:
- `void SetOnColliderEnter(const Function<void(PhysicsBodyComponent&)>& fn)` - Called when collision begins
- `void SetOnColliderPersist(const Function<void(PhysicsBodyComponent&)>& fn)` - Called while collision persists
- `void SetOnColliderExit(const Function<void(PhysicsBodyComponent&)>& fn)` - Called when collision ends

    PhysicsBodyComponent -->|"specialized by"| RigidBodyDynamic
    PhysicsBodyComponent -->|"specialized by"| RigidBodyStatic
    
    PhysicsBodyComponent -->|"owns"| PxRigidActor["physx::PxRigidActor*<br/>rigidActor"]
    PxRigidActor -->|"contains"| Colliders["PhysicsCollider<br/>Shapes"]

### PhysicsCollider

**File**: [include/RavEngine/PhysicsCollider.hpp]()

Defines the collision shape for a physics body. Multiple colliders can be attached to a single body.

**Collider Types**:
- `BoxCollider` - Box shape
- `SphereCollider` - Sphere shape
- `CapsuleCollider` - Capsule shape
- `MeshCollider` - Triangle mesh (static bodies only)
- `ConvexMeshCollider` - Convex hull approximation

**Key Methods**:

- `void SetLocalRotation(const quaternion& rot)` - Sets collider rotation
- `void SetIsTrigger(bool isTrigger)` - Configures as trigger volume
- `void SetFilterData(const FilterData& data)` - Sets collision filtering

## Animation System

### AnimatorComponent

**File**: [include/RavEngine/AnimatorComponent.hpp:132-400]()

State machine-based animation controller with support for layered animation, blend trees, and skeletal skinning.

**Key Inner Types**:
- `State` - Represents an animation state with clip, speed, looping
- `Layer` - Animation layer with state machine
- `Transition` - Defines blend between states

**Key Methods**:
- `Layer& AddLayer(uint16_t id, float weight = 1.0f)` - Adds animation layer
- `Layer& GetLayer(uint16_t id)` - Retrieves layer by ID
- `void UpdateSkeleton(float dt)` - Advances animation and computes skinning matrices
- `const std::vector<matrix4>& GetSkinningMats() const` - Returns bone transformation matrices

**Layer Methods**:
- `State& AddState(anim_id_t id, Ref<IAnimGraphable> clip, bool looping, float speed)` - Adds state
- `void Goto(anim_id_t newState, bool skipTransition, bool restartAnimation)` - Transitions to state
- `void SetBlendTree(const AnimBlendTree& tree)` - Sets blend tree as layer source
- `anim_id_t GetCurrentState() const` - Returns current state ID

    Layer["Layer"]
    StateMachine["State Machine"]
    BlendTree["AnimBlendTree<br/>Spatial Blending"]
    
    Layer -->|"owns"| StateMachine
    Layer -->|"or owns"| BlendTree
    
    StateMachine -->|"contains"| States["State Map"]
    States -->|"state ID â†’ State"| State["State"]
    State -->|"references"| AnimClip["AnimationAsset<br/>Ozz Animation"]
    State -->|"transitions"| Transition["Transition<br/>Tween Blend"]
    
    BlendTree -->|"contains"| BlendNodes["BlendTree::Node[]"]
    BlendNodes -->|"positioned"| GraphPos["clamped_vec2<br/>Graph Position"]

## Audio System

### AudioPlayer

**File**: [include/RavEngine/AudioPlayer.hpp]()

Multi-threaded audio engine that processes 3D spatial audio using Steam Audio and Resonance Audio.

**Architecture**:
- Dedicated audio thread with 2 worker threads (Taskflow executor)
- Snapshot-based rendering with double-buffering
- Lock-free communication between main thread and audio thread

**Key Methods**:
- `void Tick()` - Advances audio simulation by one buffer (called on audio thread)
- `static uint32_t GetSamplesPerSec()` - Returns sample rate
- `static uint16_t GetNChannels()` - Returns channel count
- `static uint32_t GetBufferSize()` - Returns buffer size in samples

```mermaid
graph LR
    MainThread["Main Thread<br/>World::Tick"]
    AudioSnapshot["AudioSnapshot<br/>Point Sources, Spaces"]
    DoubleBuffer["Double-Buffered<br/>Atomic Swap"]
    AudioThread["Audio Thread<br/>AudioPlayer::Tick"]
    Taskflow["Taskflow Executor<br/>2 Worker Threads"]
    
    MainThread -->|"creates"| AudioSnapshot
    AudioSnapshot -->|"SwapCurrrentAudioSnapshot()"| DoubleBuffer
    DoubleBuffer -->|"lock-free"| AudioThread
    
    AudioThread -->|"dispatches"| Taskflow
    Taskflow -->|"parallel"| ProcessProviders["Process DataProviders"]
    Taskflow -->|"parallel"| ProcessAmbient["Process Ambient Sources"]
    Taskflow -->|"parallel"| ProcessSpaces["Process Audio Spaces"]
    
    ProcessSpaces -->|"SimpleAudioSpace"| SteamAudio["Steam Audio<br/>HRTF + Binaural"]
    ProcessSpaces -->|"GeometryAudioSpace"| SteamAudioSim["Steam Audio<br/>Full Simulation"]
    ProcessSpaces -->|"BoxReverbationAudioSpace"| ResonanceAudio["Resonance Audio<br/>Room Reverb"]
    
    ProcessProviders --> FinalMix["Final Mix"]
    ProcessAmbient --> FinalMix
    ProcessSpaces --> FinalMix
    FinalMix -->|"interleave"| SDLOutput["SDL_PutAudioStreamData"]
```

**Sources**: [include/RavEngine/AudioPlayer.hpp](), [src/AudioPlayer.cpp:1-577]()

---

## Component Lifecycle

All components follow a consistent lifecycle pattern:

```mermaid
graph TD
    SpawnEntity["Entity entity = world.Spawn()"]
    EmplaceComponent["T& comp = entity.EmplaceComponent&lt;T&gt;(args)"]
    ComponentConstructor["T::T(args)<br/>Constructor Called"]
    ComponentActive["Component Active<br/>Processed by Systems"]
    DestroyComponent["entity.DestroyComponent&lt;T&gt;()"]
    ComponentDestroy["T::Destroy()<br/>If HasDestroy&lt;T&gt;"]
    ComponentDestructor["T::~T()<br/>Destructor Called"]
    DestroyEntity["world.Destroy(entity)"]
    
    SpawnEntity --> EmplaceComponent
    EmplaceComponent --> ComponentConstructor
    ComponentConstructor --> ComponentActive
    ComponentActive --> DestroyComponent
    DestroyComponent --> ComponentDestroy
    ComponentDestroy --> ComponentDestructor
    ComponentActive --> DestroyEntity
    DestroyEntity --> ComponentDestroy
```

**Component Requirements**:
- Must inherit from `AutoCTTI` or `Queryable<T>`
- Should define `MOVE_NO_COPY(T)` macro for proper move semantics
- Optional `void Destroy()` method for cleanup logic
- Stored in `EntitySparseSet<T>` for efficient lookup

**Sources**: [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:188-284](), [src/World.cpp:1-818]()

---

## ECS Filtering and Queries

The `World::Filter()` method enables efficient parallel iteration over entities with specific component combinations:

```cpp
// Iterate entities with Transform and StaticMesh components
world->Filter([](Transform& transform, const StaticMesh& mesh) {
    // Process each entity
    transform.SetLocalPosition(vector3(0, 1, 0));
});

// Multiple component types
world->Filter([](const AnimatorComponent& anim, 
                 SkinnedMeshComponent& skinned,
                 Transform& transform) {
    // Access multiple components per entity
});
```

**Query Rules**:
- Filters execute in parallel across worker threads
- Non-const references allow modification
- Const references optimize for read-only access
- Automatically skips entities missing required components

```mermaid
graph LR
    Filter["world->Filter&lt;T1, T2&gt;(fn)"]
    Taskflow["Taskflow Parallel"]
    Worker1["Worker Thread 1"]
    Worker2["Worker Thread 2"]
    Worker3["Worker Thread 3"]
    
    Filter -->|"dispatches"| Taskflow
    Taskflow -->|"entities 0-N/3"| Worker1
    Taskflow -->|"entities N/3-2N/3"| Worker2
    Taskflow -->|"entities 2N/3-N"| Worker3
    
    Worker1 -->|"fn(t1, t2)"| ProcessEntities1["Process Subset"]
    Worker2 -->|"fn(t1, t2)"| ProcessEntities2["Process Subset"]
    Worker3 -->|"fn(t1, t2)"| ProcessEntities3["Process Subset"]
```

**Sources**: [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:724-779](), [src/World.cpp:54-138]()

---

## System Execution Order

Systems are executed according to dependency relationships defined via `CreateDependency<A, B>()`:

```cpp
// Physics read runs before animator
world->CreateDependency<PhysicsLinkSystemRead, AnimatorSystem>();

// Physics write runs before scripts
world->CreateDependency<PhysicsLinkSystemWrite, ScriptSystem>();

// Animator runs before socket system
world->CreateDependency<SocketSystem, AnimatorSystem>();
```

```mermaid
graph TD
    PreTick["PreTick Phase"]
    PhysicsWrite["PhysicsLinkSystemWrite"]
    ScriptSystem["ScriptSystem"]
    PhysicsRead["PhysicsLinkSystemRead"]
    PhysicsExecute["PhysX Scene::Simulate()"]
    AnimatorSystem["AnimatorSystem"]
    SocketSystem["SocketSystem"]
    PostTick["PostTick Phase"]
    RenderTasks["Render Data Sync"]
    
    PreTick --> PhysicsWrite
    PhysicsWrite --> ScriptSystem
    ScriptSystem --> PhysicsRead
    PhysicsRead --> PhysicsExecute
    PhysicsExecute --> AnimatorSystem
    AnimatorSystem --> SocketSystem
    SocketSystem --> PostTick
    PostTick --> RenderTasks
```

**Sources**: [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:150-303](), [src/World.cpp:77-302]()

---

## Rendering Data Synchronization

The `World::RenderData` structure maintains GPU-friendly parallel copies of component data:

**Key Structures**:
- `BufferedVRAMVector<matrix4> worldTransforms` - Entity world matrices
- `BufferedVRAMSparseSet<entity_id_t, DirLightUploadData> directionalLightData` - Directional lights
- `BufferedVRAMSparseSet<entity_id_t, PointLightUploadData> pointLightData` - Point lights
- `BufferedVRAMSparseSet<entity_id_t, SpotLightDataUpload> spotLightData` - Spot lights
- `OrderedMap<MaterialSort, MDIICommand> staticMeshRenderData` - Static mesh draw commands
- `OrderedMap<MaterialSort, MDIICommandSkinned> skinnedMeshRenderData` - Skinned mesh draw commands

```mermaid

    RenderData["World::RenderData<br/>GPU Structures"]
    
    MainThread -->|"transform.SetLocalPosition()"| DirtyFlags
    DirtyFlags -->|"isTickDirty = true"| RenderTasks
    
    RenderTasks -->|"updateRenderDataStaticMesh"| SyncStaticMesh["Sync Static Meshes"]
    RenderTasks -->|"updateRenderDataSkinnedMesh"| SyncSkinnedMesh["Sync Skinned Meshes"]
    RenderTasks -->|"updateInvalidatedDirs"| SyncDirLights["Sync Directional Lights"]
    RenderTasks -->|"updateInvalidatedPoints"| SyncPointLights["Sync Point Lights"]
    
    SyncStaticMesh --> RenderData
    SyncSkinnedMesh --> RenderData
    SyncDirLights --> RenderData
    SyncPointLights --> RenderData
    
    RenderData -->|"EncodeSync()"| GPUBuffers["GPU Private Buffers<br/>BufferedVRAMVector"]
```

**Sources**: [include/RavEngine/World.hpp:419-449](), [src/World.cpp:311-521]()

## Material Instance Configuration

Material instances store per-object rendering state and texture bindings:

```cpp
auto material = Material::Manager::Get<PBRMaterial>();
auto instance = New<PBRMaterialInstance>(material);

// Configure textures
instance->SetAlbedoTexture(Texture::Manager::Get("albedo.png"));
instance->SetNormalTexture(Texture::Manager::Get("normal.png"));
instance->SetMetallicRoughnessTexture(Texture::Manager::Get("metallic.png"));

// Assign to mesh
auto& mesh = entity.EmplaceComponent<StaticMesh>(meshAsset, instance);
```

**Texture Binding Methods**:
- `void SetTexture(TextureBindingSlot slot, Ref<Texture> texture)`
- Specialized methods per material type (e.g., `SetAlbedoTexture()`)
